# Module Authority Map — Ade

> **Status:** Living architectural document. Regenerated; not hand-edited.
> Per-project instance of `~/.claude/methodology/templates/codemap.md`.

> 11 crates, 460 canonical types, 2413 tests, 157 CI checks at HEAD (`5ec841c8`, PHASE4-N-AI close — live fork-choice rollback-follow wiring, single-best-peer FOLLOW (NOT full ChainSel); the sole new BLUE authority is the version-gated `WalEntry::RollBack` durable MARKER + its `RollbackPoint` / `RollbackReason` payload types).
>
> **PHASE4-N-AI cluster-close refresh (load-bearing — live fork-choice rollback-follow wiring; single-best-peer FOLLOW, NOT full ChainSel).** The prior on-disk CODEMAP was pinned at HEAD `5858288e` (the PHASE4-N-AH close — 458 canonical types, 2365 tests by the documented grep, 148 CI checks, 347 rules). This regeneration folds the `8e2c3672..5ec841c8` span — the **PHASE4-N-AI** cluster (live fork-choice rollback-follow wiring of the EXISTING `ade_runtime::consensus::chain_selector` orchestrator + `select_best_chain` into the live `--mode node` receive path, single-best-peer FOLLOW; `DC-NODE-23`…`DC-NODE-29`; close `5ec841c8`). **This span DOES change BLUE — it is the FIRST BLUE delta since the G-N span: +2 canonical types** (verified mechanically: `git grep -hE "^(pub )?(struct|enum) "` over the BLUE `core_paths` trees is 458 → **460**, the +2 being the NEW `ade_ledger::wal::event::{RollbackPoint, RollbackReason}` payload types of the new closed-sum variant `WalEntry::RollBack` — `ade_ledger` 177 → 179; `git diff 8e2c3672..HEAD -- Cargo.toml` is empty — still **11 crates**). The span touches exactly THREE BLUE files — `ade_ledger::wal::{event, replay}` (the new version-gated `WalEntry::RollBack {to_point, reason, prior_tip, selected_tip}` DURABLE MARKER at the reserved RollBackward tag 1 + the replay arm that re-anchors the fp chain to `to_point`'s in-chain `post_fp` and re-invokes the EXISTING `materialize_rolled_back_state` + lockstep `commit_rollback` on the recovery/materialize layer — a MARKER, **NOT** a second rollback implementation; tag 2 `CaptureSnapshot` stays reserved) plus `ade_ledger::wal::{error, mod, store_trait}` (the new closed `WalError::RollbackTargetNotInChain` + accessor plumbing) and `ade_core::consensus::fork_choice` (**production UNCHANGED — `select_best_chain` is byte-identical; the ONLY hunk is `@@ -340,4 +340,89 @@ mod tests` — a `#[cfg(test)]`-only arrival-order-permutation determinism proof for `CN-CONS-01`**). Everything else is RED/GREEN on the `ade_node` + `ade_runtime` shells: the GREEN-by-function `node_sync::{classify_receive, resolve_disposition}` venue-blind detector + venue-split resolver, the closed `NodeSyncItem {Block | RollBack(Point)}` / `ReceiveClass` / `ReceiveDisposition` / `CandidateSummary`, the extended `NodeSyncError {Pump | Capture | UnexpectedRollback | RollbackPointSlotMismatch}`, `ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending` + `pending_reselection_forge_refusal`; the RED `node_lifecycle::{apply_chain_event, run_participant_sync, declare_participant_venue}` + `ForgeActivation.pending_reselection` + the new `AppliedTip` / `ApplyError`; and the RED `ade_runtime::admission::wire_pump` `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward {peer, point, tip}` preservation (the rollback POINT is now a closed event, no longer downgraded to a `TipUpdate`; `Origin` fails closed `UnsupportedRollbackPoint`). **SEVEN new rules** (`DC-NODE-23`…`DC-NODE-29`), ALL `enforced`; **status flips:** enforced 213 → 221 (+8 — the 7 new + one existing partial→enforced), partial 20 → 19, declared 114 unchanged. Registry **347 → 354** (+7). **NINE new CI gates (148 → 157), all ADDED (0 modified, 0 removed): `ci_check_wal_rollback_replay_equiv.sh`** (DC-NODE-27), **`ci_check_receive_detector_venue_split.sh`** (DC-NODE-23/24), **`ci_check_live_fork_choice_apply.sh`** + **`ci_check_live_fork_choice_wiring.sh`** (DC-NODE-25/26/28), **`ci_check_wire_rollback_signal_preserved.sh`** (DC-PUMP-01 strengthening / AI-S4a), **`ci_check_participant_venue_inert.sh`** (DC-NODE-28 / AI-S4b-i), **`ci_check_rollback_target_canonical_binding.sh`** (DC-NODE-29 / AI-S6 H-1), **`ci_check_chain_selection_arrival_order_independent.sh`** (CN-CONS-01 / AI-S5), and **`ci_check_convergence_evidence_schema.sh`** (CE-AI-5 / AI-S5). **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** N-AI is **single-best-peer rollback-follow** wiring, **NOT full ChainSel** — it follows ONE peer, classifies its candidates ONCE venue-blind, and on a Participant venue routes a non-spine candidate through the EXISTING `chain_selector` → BLUE `select_best_chain` (DC-CONS-03) durable-apply path; it does **NOT** maintain a multi-peer candidate set, does **NOT** add a second selection authority, and `CN-CONS-03` was **NOT** flipped to enforced (it stays `partial` with the explicit honesty note that only the single-best-peer venue was exercised). The sole new BLUE authority is `WalEntry::RollBack` (a durable MARKER re-invoking existing rollback authority on replay — not a second rollback impl); `pump_block` stays the SOLE roll-forward durable admit (`DC-NODE-05`/`DC-NODE-12` unchanged); the SingleProducer venue stays **fail-closed unchanged** (`run_node_sync` returns `NodeSyncError::UnexpectedRollback` on any `NodeSyncItem::RollBack` — it never adopts a peer rollback; `DC-NODE-20`/`DC-NODE-24` `RefuseSingleProducer`); the rollback target is bound to the durable `ChainDb`'s stored slot for the hash and fails closed pre-mutation on any mismatch (`DC-NODE-29`); and there is **NO RO-LIVE flip** (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated; CE-AI-6 is the operator-pass convergence evidence, vacuous-until-committed). The delta stack below is newest-first (AI, then AH/AG/AF, then the carried AE.F, N-AE close refresh, N-AC, N-AB, N-AA, the gate-hygiene note, N-U, G-R … G-K, and G-A…G-J stacks — compressed, not deleted).

Registry **341 → 347** (+6). **SIX new CI gates (142 → 148): `ci_check_single_producer_extend_own_spine.sh`** (N-AF, DC-NODE-18 — ADDED at the N-AF close, after the on-disk base), **`ci_check_single_producer_loop_continuation.sh`** (N-AG, DC-NODE-19), **`ci_check_local_durable_forge_base.sh`** (N-AH, DC-NODE-20), **`ci_check_cert_evidence_only.sh`** (N-AH, DC-NODE-21), **`ci_check_warm_start_re_entry.sh`** (N-AH, DC-NODE-22), and **`ci_check_live_transcript_forge_base.sh`** (N-AH S4a, CN-NODE-04 / DC-NODE-20 evidence); `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh` was **phase-split / repaired** in place for the DC-NODE-20 call chain (the INITIAL catch-up gate verified via `run_relay_loop_with_sched -> dc_node_15_refusal -> forge_followed_tip_admission`, the POST-self-admit forge base asserted as the local `ChainDb::tip` with NO followed re-check), and `ci_check_node_path_fidelity.sh` was edited in place (the S2 cert-removal 28→29 reconcile) — both modified, not added. **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** the N-AF→N-AH span makes a declared rung-1 single-producer venue forge on Ade's OWN local durable spine head (`ChainDb::tip`) — and nothing more. > > **PHASE4-N-AH delta (local selected durable chain forge-base authority — in a declared rung-1 single-producer venue, after Ade self-admits a valid forged block through `pump_block` onto its local durable ChainDB spine, the next forge base is Ade's LOCAL SELECTED DURABLE TIP (`ChainDb::tip`), NOT `followed_peer_tip` and NOT an operator adoption certificate; the cert is evidence-only and REMOVED; warm-start re-enters the extend state on the recovered own-spine tip — `DC-NODE-20` / `DC-NODE-21` / `DC-NODE-22`):** **RED/GREEN-ONLY — ZERO BLUE diff** (458 canonical types unchanged; the BLUE `ChainDb::tip` + `pump_block` + chain-selection paths reused unchanged — verified: `git diff 600581e8..HEAD` over the BLUE `core_paths` trees touches **no** file and adds **zero** `^+(pub )?(struct|enum)` lines). The cluster closed in 4 slices + 2 sub-slices (cluster doc `c72cc9b5` + declare `DC-NODE-20`/`DC-NODE-21`; S1 `b0fb8817`; S2 `050237e9`; S3 `dad29b43`; S4a `7049d813`; S4b `e7b9be7e`; close `5858288e`). **Root cause (the run-4 live finding, recorded honestly):** Ade forged block 11, a real Haskell relay ADOPTED it, but Ade returned `no_tip_available` every subsequent tick because the `proceed_to_forge` gate required `durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip` — which fails the instant Ade self-admits a block the non-producing relay does not re-announce — and the only escape (the DC-NODE-18 cert-promotion into extend mode) raced and lost to the follow-link EOF. The cert had leaked from evidence into forge-loop authority. **S1 (DC-NODE-20 local-tip forge base):** `node_sync::forge_mode_after_admit` now enters `SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine{adopted_root = own, current_tip = own}` DIRECTLY on a real self-admit from `CaughtUpToPeerTip` — the `FirstOwnBlockServed` cert-wait intermediate is FOLDED OUT of the `ForgeMode` enum (now 3-state: `InitialCatchupRequired → CaughtUpToPeerTip → SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine`); `single_producer_forge_decision` derives the forge base from the local durable spine head under a 6-condition fence (`VenueRole::SingleProducer`; NO competing block observed on the canonical receive stream since catch-up — an OBSERVED-FEED fence, NOT fork-choice; relay non-producing; admitted via `pump_block`; spine contiguous/servable; no fork-choice required — mechanically DERIVED from the observed-feed fence), failing closed (`ForgeRefused::SingleProducerFenceViolation` over the closed `SingleProducerFenceReason`) on any violation. `forge_followed_tip_admission` REMAINS the DC-NODE-15 INITIAL catch-up gate (durable == followed before the first own-forge); DC-NODE-20 supersedes ONLY the repeated post-self-admit re-check. **S2 (DC-NODE-21 cert evidence-only):** the `VenueAdoptionCertificate` type + the `read_adoption_cert` / `parse_hex32` parsers + the `--adoption-cert-path` CLI flag are FULLY DELETED from `ade_node` — the cert is rung-1 RED operator EVIDENCE parsed by the harness OUTSIDE the node, never a forge-base input; `ci_check_cert_evidence_only.sh` asserts no cert token survives in the forge path (run-4 transcript: `cert_path_present=false` ×461, `cert_path_present:true` count = 0). **S3 (CE-AH-4 replay):** a hermetic replay corpus over the local-tip-derived forged successors (no new canonical type; reuses the WAL/ChainDB) — removing the RED cert/timing from the authority path makes the post-self-admit forge MORE deterministic / replay-equivalent (T-REC-03/05 extended). **S4a (CN-NODE-04 / DC-NODE-20 evidence):** the closed emit-only `NodeSchedEvent` vocabulary gains a `ForgeBaseSelected` event (`forge_base_source = local_chaindb_tip`, the entered forge mode, `cert_path_present`) + an enriched `ForgeResult` (`self_admit_via_pump_block`) so the sched transcript directly witnesses the forge-base decision; RED evidence ONLY — it serializes the decision already made, never read by the planner or any authority path. **S4b (DC-NODE-22 warm-start re-entry):** the NEW GREEN `node_sync::warm_start_forge_mode(venue_role, recovered_tip, replayed_anchor_block_no)` re-enters `SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine{current_tip = ChainDb::tip}` for a single-producer venue whose recovered tip is ABOVE the replay anchor (`recovered_tip.block_no > replayed_anchor_block_no` ⇔ recovery replayed ≥ 1 own block — a local continuation spine), WITHOUT a fresh followed-peer catch-up; every other case FAILS CLOSED to `InitialCatchupRequired`. The `replayed_anchor_block_no` is a DERIVED recovery summary on `BootstrapState` (`recovered_tip.block_no − admit_count`), NOT an independently persisted chain point. **Registry → 347 rules**: NEW `DC-NODE-20` (`tier = derived`, `enforced`, `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-AH"`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_local_durable_forge_base.sh ci/ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh`, `cross_ref = [DC-NODE-05, DC-NODE-12, DC-NODE-15, DC-NODE-18, DC-NODE-19, DC-NODE-21, DC-CONS-03, DC-CONS-23, T-REC-03, T-REC-05]`), `DC-NODE-21` (`derived`, `enforced`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_cert_evidence_only.sh ci/ci_check_node_path_fidelity.sh`, `cross_ref = [DC-NODE-20, DC-NODE-18, DC-NODE-19, DC-CONS-03]`), `DC-NODE-22` (`derived`, `enforced`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_warm_start_re_entry.sh`, `cross_ref = [DC-NODE-20, DC-NODE-19, DC-NODE-15, DC-NODE-12, DC-NODE-05, T-REC-05, CN-NODE-02, DC-CONS-03]`). Strengthened (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AH"`): `CN-NODE-04` (the closed sched vocabulary now also carries the DC-NODE-20 forge-base evidence — `ForgeBaseSelected` + enriched `ForgeResult`) and `DC-NODE-19` (the proven extend state now survives warm-start). **FIVE NEW CI gates this cluster (143 → 148): `ci_check_single_producer_loop_continuation.sh`** (DC-NODE-19, landed in N-AG), **`ci_check_local_durable_forge_base.sh`** (DC-NODE-20), **`ci_check_cert_evidence_only.sh`** (DC-NODE-21), **`ci_check_warm_start_re_entry.sh`** (DC-NODE-22), **`ci_check_live_transcript_forge_base.sh`** (CN-NODE-04 / DC-NODE-20 evidence); `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh` phase-split + `ci_check_node_path_fidelity.sh` reconcile are in-place modifications. **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** N-AH makes the post-self-admit forge base the LOCAL durable spine head and removes the cert from authority — and nothing more. The forge base is `ChainDb::tip` (NOT `followed_peer_tip`, NOT a cert) under the 6-condition fence; the observed-feed competing-block fence FAILS CLOSED (NOT fork-choice — that is rung 2, DC-CONS-03 untouched); the cert is REMOVED (not just demoted) from `ade_node`; `pump_block` stays the SOLE durable admit authority (the forge advances no tip directly — `DC-NODE-05`/`DC-NODE-12`); there is **NO new BLUE canonical type or authority** (the only new pub item carrying a chain point is the GREEN `warm_start_forge_mode` + the RED `BootstrapState.replayed_anchor_block_no` derived summary; 458 unchanged); and there is **NO RO-LIVE flip** — the run-4 live transcript (a real Haskell relay adopting Ade's cert-free local-tip-forged blocks, sustained > k immutable across a follow-link EOF + a restart; `docs/evidence/phase4-n-ah-ce-ah-6-close.{md,jsonl}`) is the C2-LOCAL rung-1 mechanism, NOT operator-witnessed bounty acceptance on preprod (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated; rung-2 fork-choice + multi-producer + preprod are explicitly out of scope).

> > **PHASE4-N-AG delta (single-producer forge-loop continuation after follow-link EOF — in a certified single-producer venue already in the DC-NODE-18 extend state, a `LoopState::Ending` caused SOLELY by a structural feed EOF MUST NOT by itself terminate the forge loop; it continues forging successors on its OWN certified durable spine, fenced — `DC-NODE-19`, declared/partial):** **GREEN/RED-ONLY — ZERO BLUE diff** (458 unchanged; no new BLUE type/authority). The cluster (cluster doc `c87f7109` + declare `DC-NODE-19`; S1 `b9ef6e69` GREEN planner; S2 `46098c8c` RED loop continuation; S3 `a65e2039` replay-equivalence; S4 doc `267364b9` operator-gated live acceptance) refines the loop's TERMINATION authority off feed-liveness onto explicit operator shutdown / fatal error (the same move `DC-NODE-09` made for the serve-listener lifetime) while PRESERVING `DC-NODE-05` (the forge advances no durable tip directly; `run_node_sync -> pump_block` stays the sole durable tip-advance authority; available feed work still drains via `SyncOnce` before any `ForgeTick`). **S1 (DC-NODE-19, CE-AG-1):** `run_loop_planner::plan_loop_step` gains an explicit GREEN 5th input `venue_policy: VenuePolicy` (the closed 2-variant `HaltOnFeedEnd | ContinueInSingleProducerExtend`) — the 32-case total table; the GREEN `node_sync::venue_policy(venue_role, forge_mode)` projection returns `ContinueInSingleProducerExtend` ONLY in an explicitly declared single-producer venue already in `SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine`, else `HaltOnFeedEnd` (the verbatim prior feed-end-halts behaviour). The default `VenueRole::Unknown` venue takes the verbatim prior `HaltCleanly`-on-feed-end path. **S2 (DC-NODE-19, CE-AG-2/3):** the RED `node_lifecycle` loop threads the venue policy + restructures the Idle-under-feed-end wait so a dead feed does not starve the forge cadence; the continuation is FENCED to the certified single-producer run and FAILS CLOSED on any of the 7 conditions (not single-producer; not in the extend state; operator shutdown; forge-validity bound fails; competing chain observed; relay-producing evidence; cert absent/malformed — the DC-NODE-18 `SingleProducerFenceReason` set). NO numeric "max blind forges" cap (an artificial operator policy, not a Cardano semantic invariant). Only a CLEAN structural feed EOF is continued; a `LoopState::Ending` representing a real shutdown or a fatal source failure exits via `Err`/fail-fast and is NEVER continued. **S3 (CE-AG-4):** replay-equivalence over a chain that includes successors forged AFTER a feed EOF (T-REC-03 two-clean-runs byte-identical + T-REC-05 kill/warm-start byte-identical; the feed-end event is replay-neutral — no WAL append). **DC-NODE-19 status = `declared`** (`tier = derived`, `introduced_in = "TBD"`, `strengthened_in = ["PHASE4-N-AH"]`, `ci_script = ""` at N-AG close → the `ci_check_single_producer_loop_continuation.sh` gate landed but the rule's full enforcement (the committed sustained-past-k live transcript CE-AF-6b) is gated on the rung-1 C2-LOCAL operator harness; DC-NODE-19 was subsequently RE-HOMED onto the DC-NODE-20 local-tip path at N-AH and its sustained-past-k proof closed there). A loop-lifecycle refinement, NOT a fork-choice change — **DC-CONS-03 stays the sole follow/fork authority; the continuation never selects/reorders/prefers chains.** **NO RO-LIVE flip.**

> > **PHASE4-N-AF delta (single-producer extend-own-durable-spine — a declared single-producer venue may forge on Ade's OWN durable spine WITHOUT a relay echo, AFTER an explicit RED venue-adoption certificate matched by CHAIN-POINT IDENTITY, NEVER inferred from self-admit; fail-closed — `DC-NODE-18`; this is the deferred N-AF CODEMAP debt, recorded honestly):** **GREEN/RED-ONLY — ZERO BLUE diff** (458 unchanged; the touched `.rs` are the GREEN `node_sync` classifier + the RED `node_lifecycle` loop + `cli` — none in the BLUE `core_paths`). The single-slice cluster (invariants `c58575ec`; cluster/slice docs `b7b1bb52`; impl `f746084f` + close `f87d0056`) flipped `DC-NODE-18` declared → enforced + declared `DC-NODE-17` (the OQ-1 live-disproved-as-fix observation invariant, retained SAFETY-ONLY, no gate). A mode-aware `ForgeTick` gate (the `ForgeMode` enum — at N-AF a 4-state `InitialCatchupRequired → CaughtUpToPeerTip → FirstOwnBlockServed → SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine`, GREEN transition fn, no booleans) let a DECLARED single-producer venue forge on Ade's OWN durable spine WITHOUT a relay echo, AFTER an explicit RED venue-adoption certificate matched by CHAIN-POINT IDENTITY (hash + block_no), NEVER inferred from self-admit; fail-closed `ForgeRefused::SingleProducerFenceViolation`; the certificate was ADMISSIBILITY-ONLY (never persisted / replay-visible); the default `VenueRole::Unknown` path was the VERBATIM prior DC-NODE-15 gate. **N-AF added the 5 GREEN `ForgeMode`/`VenueRole`/`VenueAdoptionCertificate`/`SingleProducerFenceReason`/`SingleProducerForgeDecision` enums/structs (all GREEN `node_sync`, NOT canonical-counted; 458 unchanged) and 1 CI gate** (`ci_check_single_producer_extend_own_spine.sh`); registry 341 → 343 (+DC-NODE-17 declared + DC-NODE-18 enforced). **DC-CONS-03 untouched.** **SUPERSEDED by N-AH (recorded honestly):** N-AH FOLDED OUT the `FirstOwnBlockServed` cert-wait intermediate (the `ForgeMode` enum is now 3-state) and REMOVED the `VenueAdoptionCertificate` type + cert parser — the N-AF cert-promotion mechanism is gone; the extend state is now entered DIRECTLY on local self-admit (`DC-NODE-20`). The N-AF live proof (run c2t7 — block 11 forged WITHOUT echo after an adoption certificate) validated the cert-free architecture N-AH then made the production path. **NO RO-LIVE flip.**

> **PHASE4-N-AE.F refresh (load-bearing — receive idempotency).** The prior on-disk CODEMAP was pinned at HEAD `a76672b9` (the PHASE4-N-AE cluster close — 458 canonical types, 2337 tests by the documented grep, 141 CI checks, 340 rules). The follow-on fix commit `6363683e` (`fix(phase4-n-ae): AE.F receive idempotency — survive the post-adoption echo (DC-NODE-16)`) refreshed the OTHER three grounding docs (SEAMS / HEAD_DELTAS / TRACEABILITY) but left the CODEMAP at the N-AE close; this regeneration folds the `a76672b9..6363683e` AE.F delta into the CODEMAP. **AE.F is RED-only — ZERO BLUE diff, ZERO new module, ZERO new type** (verified mechanically: `git diff a76672b9..6363683e` over the BLUE `core_paths` trees adds **zero** `^+(pub )?(struct|enum)` lines; `git diff a76672b9..6363683e -- Cargo.toml` is empty — still **11 crates**). The whole span touches exactly TWO source files: the RED `ade_runtime::forward_sync::pump` (production change — the new hash-exact already-have idempotency gate in `pump_block`) and the RED `ade_node::node_sync` (one new `#[tokio::test]` only — the live-shape echo regression). **AE.F (DC-NODE-16 receive idempotency):** `pump_block`, immediately AFTER `decode_block` and BEFORE the BLUE chokepoint reducer (`forward_sync_step`), queries `db.get_block_by_hash(&decoded.block_hash)`; if `Some(stored)` AND `stored.slot == decoded.header_input.slot` it returns `Ok(None)` — an idempotent no-op (no reducer step, no WAL append, no tip change; the post-state is identical and replay-equivalent). `get_block_by_hash` is hash-exact, so a DIFFERENT block (different hash) at/before the last-applied slot returns `None` here, falls through to the unchanged BLUE header authority, and fails closed (`SlotBeforeLastApplied` / `BlockNoOutOfOrder`) — the skip is gated on HASH equality vs the durable store, NEVER slot alone, with no skip-past and no fork-choice (DC-CONS-03 untouched). **Root cause (the post-CE-A5 echo, recorded honestly):** after the real cardano-node relay `AddedToCurrentChain` Ade's forged block 17 (the N-AE CE-A5 manifest), the relay re-announced that same block over Ade's follow link; the BLUE header authority correctly rejected `SlotBeforeLastApplied{last=421,attempted=421}`, which terminated a continuous run (exit 43) AFTER the manifest — not a manifest blocker, but it ends a continuous run. **ONE new rule, enforced** (`DC-NODE-16`); **ZERO strengthenings**; registry **340 → 341** (+1; enforced 208 → 209). **ONE new CI gate (141 → 142): `ci_check_receive_idempotency.sh`** (fences hash-keyed `get_block_by_hash(&decoded.block_hash)`, the `Ok(None)` no-op gated by that hit, the gate PRECEDING the BLUE reducer `forward_sync_step`, and the `stored.slot == decoded.header_input.slot` slot-consistency check). **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** AE.F makes a re-announce of an ALREADY-HAVE block (same hash, same slot) a no-op at the RED durable-admit chokepoint — and nothing more. It is a RED-chokepoint refinement of the AE.F invariants-sketch's BLUE `ReceiveOutcome::AlreadyHave`: `get_block_by_hash` is a DETERMINISTIC durable-store query (not nondeterminism), so the gate lives at the chokepoint with no new reducer input and the BLUE authority is UNTOUCHED. There is **NO new BLUE canonical type or authority** (458 unchanged); the skip is **HASH-keyed** (a different block still fails closed in the unchanged BLUE authority); the no-op appends **NOTHING to the WAL** (T-REC-05 / DC-WAL-02 preserved — warm-start replay is unaffected); there is **NO skip-past / NO fork-choice** (DC-CONS-03 stays the follow authority); and there is **NO RO-LIVE flip** (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated). The delta stack below is newest-first (AE.F, then the carried N-AE close refresh, N-AC, N-AB, N-AA, the gate-hygiene note, N-U, G-R … G-K, and G-A…G-J stacks — compressed, not deleted).

> > **PHASE4-N-AE delta (recover→serve continuity + forge-on-followed-tip admissibility — a recovered/following `--mode node` may forge ONLY on the followed peer tip it can prove servable/intersectable, and a recovered anchor parent is made FindIntersect-only-projectable so a relay rolls forward onto the forged successor — `DC-NODE-14` / `DC-NODE-15` / `DC-CONS-24` / `DC-PROTO-10`):** **ZERO new BLUE canonical type** (458 unchanged — verified mechanically: `git diff 1d54abb4..a76672b9` over the BLUE `core_paths` trees adds **zero** `^+(pub )?(struct\|enum)` lines). The two BLUE-tree touches are both ADDITIVE-by-signature, no new type: (a) `ade_ledger::block_validity::header_input::DecodedBlock` gains a `prev_hash: PrevHash` field, populated from `hb.prev_hash` already parsed for `check_header_position` — the decode logic / hashing / determinism are byte-unchanged (`block_hash` / `computed_body_hash` / position rule all identical); (b) `ade_network::chain_sync::server::producer_chain_sync_serve` sets `state.last_announced` from the matched intersect `Point` in the `IntersectFound` arm (an existing-field write — `ProducerChainSyncServerState` unchanged). Everything else is RED on the `--mode node` spine. **Root cause (the C2-LOCAL #8 / CE-A5 relay-adoption finding, recorded honestly):** a recovered-and-following Ade node forged a successor on its *recovered snapshot anchor* (the recovery tip) — a point NO Haskell relay could `FindIntersect` (the anchor is a snapshot head, not a servable StoredBlock the peer holds), AND the forge raced the follow (it built before catching up to the peer's selected tip), so the forged successor was never adoptable. Two sub-gaps: **2a forge-on-followed-tip** (the forge base must be the followed peer tip, not the recovered anchor) and **2b serve-continuity** (the served chain must expose an intersectable parent from which the peer rolls onto the forged successor). **AE.A (DC-NODE-15 + DC-CONS-24 forge-on-followed-tip gate):** `ade_node::node_sync` adds the GREEN-by-function classifier `forge_followed_tip_admission(durable_servable_tip, followed_peer_tip) -> ForgeFollowedTipAdmission` (closed: `CaughtUp` | `NotCaughtUp(NotCaughtUpReason)`; pure / total / deterministic — compares canonical hashes, never block-number alone), the RED `FollowedPeerTipSignal` (observes the wire stream's `TipUpdate`; a forge-ADMISSIBILITY input only — it may PREVENT a forge, never select/reorder/prefer chains, never reaches `select_best_chain` / `chain_selector` / `fork_choice`), and the typed `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp { local_servable_tip, followed_peer_tip, reason }` + `NodeForgeOutcome`. `ade_node::node_lifecycle`'s `run_relay_loop_with_sched` ForgeTick arm REMOVES the recovered-anchor (`recovered.tip`) forge-base fallback, calls the gate before the single fenced `forge_one_from_recovered`, and records a typed `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp` into `ForgeActivation.last_forge_refused` (no forge, no state transition, tip unchanged — distinct from a forge `Failed`); a `CaughtUp` forge builds on `selected_tip == durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip` with `prev_hash = PrevHash::Block(selected_tip.hash)` and `block_no == followed_tip.block_no + 1` (DC-CONS-24 — parent identity is the canonical hash). **AE.B (DC-NODE-14 recovered/forge-parent intersectability — Option B, FindIntersect-ONLY, proof-gated):** `ade_runtime::network::served_chain_projection::ChainDbServedSource::intersect` gains a SECOND clause after the durable-StoredBlock match — it projects the FORGE PARENT (the `prev_hash` of the EARLIEST servable StoredBlock, via the new bounded private helper `earliest_servable_block_prev_hash`, which reads exactly the earliest block via the N-AA `range_bytes_capped(0, u64::MAX, 1)` and reuses the BLUE `decode_block` + the new `DecodedBlock.prev_hash`). A relay that already holds the parent block can `FindIntersect` there and roll forward onto the real successor (`next_after` returns it via the slot range, since `parent.slot < successor.slot`). **HARD BOUNDARY:** NO bytes are EVER served for the projected point — `get_block_by_hash` / `serve_range` stay empty, so BlockFetch refuses structurally; NO synthetic StoredBlock; recover-only (no StoredBlock) ⇒ NO projection (fail-closed, never a magic anchor); a `Genesis` earliest-parent ⇒ no projection (a from-genesis root has no projectable parent). **AE.C (DC-WAL-02 + T-REC-05 recover→follow WAL prior-fp seed):** `ade_node::node_lifecycle` seeds the first followed `AdmitBlock`'s WAL `prior_fp` from the recovered post-state fingerprint, so the recover→follow WAL chain is continuous (no orphan / no fp break across the recover→serve handoff). **AE.E (DC-PROTO-10 chain-sync server FindIntersect cursor — the CE-A5 closer):** after `producer_chain_sync_serve` answers `IntersectFound(point)` at a NON-Origin point, its read cursor `last_announced` IS that point — the next `RequestNext` serves `next_after(point)` (the successor the client rolls onto), NEVER `next_after(None)` (the chain start). Before AE.E, a client intersecting at its own tip was served block 0 and rejected `UnexpectedBlockNo(tip_block_no + 1)(0)`; an `Origin` intersect still keeps the cursor `None` (serve from the chain start — correct). **Registry → 340 rules** (+4): NEW `DC-NODE-14` (`tier = derived`, `enforced`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh ci/ci_check_recovered_anchor_intersectable.sh`), `DC-NODE-15` (`derived`, `enforced`, `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh`), `DC-CONS-24` (`derived`, `enforced`, `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh`), `DC-PROTO-10` (`derived`, `enforced`, `ci_script = ""` — **test-enforced** by `producer_chain_sync_serve_find_intersect_sets_cursor_then_rolls_forward_past_it`). Strengthened (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AE"`): `CN-CONS-06` (block-production admissibility now requires caught-up-to-followed-tip), `CN-CONS-07` (serve-provenance now also covers the FindIntersect-only forge-parent projection), `DC-WAL-02` (recover→follow WAL prior-fp continuity), `DC-NODE-05` (the durable-tip-only forge rule now also gates on followed-tip admissibility), `DC-EPOCH-03`, `T-REC-05`, `DC-CONS-23`. **THREE new CI gates (138 → 141): `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh`** (the forge is admissible ONLY when `durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip`; the recovered anchor is never a forge base; the followed-tip signal never reaches a chain selector; the forged successor's `prev_hash` byte-equals the followed tip hash + `block_no + 1`), **`ci_check_recovered_anchor_intersectable.sh`** (the forge-parent projection is FindIntersect-ONLY — no bytes served for the projected point; recover-only ⇒ no projection; reuses the single `decode_block` + bounded read), and **`ci_check_recover_follow_wal_lineage.sh`** (the recover→follow WAL chain seeds `prior_fp` from the recovered post-state fp — no orphan / fp break). **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** N-AE makes a recovered/following node forge ONLY on a parent a peer can adopt, and exposes that parent as an intersect point — and nothing more. The followed-peer-tip signal is an ADMISSIBILITY input ONLY (it may PREVENT a forge, never select/replace/reorder/prefer chains — it never reaches `select_best_chain` / `chain_selector` / `fork_choice`; DC-CONS-03 stays the follow authority); the forge-parent projection serves **NO bytes** (FindIntersect-only; BlockFetch refuses structurally — no synthetic StoredBlock, no served chain head a peer cannot intersect); the recovered anchor is **NEVER** a forge base nor a served head; there is **NO new BLUE canonical type or authority** (the two BLUE touches are an additive field + an existing-field cursor write; 458 unchanged); and there is **NO RO-LIVE flip** — a recovered node that forges a peer-adoptable successor is the C2 mechanism, NOT operator-witnessed bounty acceptance (`RO-LIVE-01` stays `partial` / operator-gated; the genesis-density window still limits a from-genesis venue — cross-period / dense-tip forge→adopt is the C2 preprod-tip path).

> **PHASE4-N-AC cluster-close refresh (load-bearing).** The prior on-disk CODEMAP was pinned at HEAD `c6e7fafe` (the PHASE4-N-AB close — 458 canonical types, 2320 tests, 137 CI checks, 335 rules). > > **PHASE4-N-AC delta (KES signing evolves the operator key to the current period before signing — the RED signing shell advances the minted-at-period-0 key forward to the chain's current KES period before the single real KES sign, fail-closed backwards / beyond-lifetime — `DC-CRYPTO-10`):** **RED-ONLY — ZERO BLUE diff** (458 canonical types unchanged; the BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + KES verifier reused unchanged — verified mechanically: `git diff c6e7fafe..1d54abb4` over the BLUE `core_paths` trees touches **no** file and adds **zero** `^+(pub )?(struct\|enum)` lines; `T-KEY-01` preserved). The two source files changed in the whole span are both RED: `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/producer_shell.rs` (`//! RED` producer key-custody shell) + `crates/ade_node/src/produce_mode.rs` (`//! RED` forge). The cluster closed in 1 slice (cluster doc `cbe6633f` + declare `DC-CRYPTO-10`; S1 slice doc `68a85dbe` / impl `7d4a4a72`; close `1d54abb4`). **Root cause (surfaced by the C1 genesis-rehearsal re-run — recorded honestly, NOT a regression from N-U/AA/AB):** the C1 rehearsal stopped reproducing once the private net aged past one KES period (slot ~249659 / `slotsPerKESPeriod` 129600 -> KES period 1), because the forge's only real KES sign (`produce_mode.rs` step-3) called the raw `shell.kes_sign_header(kes_period, …)`, which requires `kes.current_period() == requested` — and NOTHING evolved the minted-at-period-0 operator key forward — so every leader slot failed `KesPeriodNotCurrent { requested: 1, current: 0 }` (`succeeded = 0`; the follower KeepAlive-timed-out waiting for a block). The wire/serve/intersection path was healthy. **S1 (DC-CRYPTO-10 evolve-then-sign):** NEW RED method `ProducerShell::kes_sign_header_advancing(&mut self, period: u32, preimage: &UnsignedHeaderPreImage) -> Result<KesSignature, ShellSignError>` = `self.kes_advance_to(period)?` THEN `self.kes_sign_header(period, preimage)`. `kes_advance_to -> kes_update` is the EXISTING deterministic Sum6KES update: `period == current` -> no-op evolution (the `while current < to` loop does nothing) then sign (existing period-0 signing UNCHANGED); `period > current` (in window) -> forward evolution then sign; `period < current` -> fail closed `Signing(EvolutionBackwards)` (a destroyed past period cannot be re-signed — forward-secrecy); `period` beyond the key lifetime / unreachable by sequential evolution -> fail closed `Signing(EvolutionExhausted)`. The `period` is passed VERBATIM (no `period ± N`). After a successful `kes_advance_to`, `current == period`, so `kes_sign_header` signs at the current period (no `KesPeriodNotCurrent`). The forge's single real KES sign (`produce_mode::run_real_forge_inner` step 3) now calls `kes_sign_header_advancing` instead of `kes_sign_header`; on `Err(_)` it still returns the closed `CoordinatorEvent::ForgeFailed`. The `&self` `kes_sign_at` / `kes_sign_header` REMAIN for callers that manage periods themselves. **Registry -> 336 rules**: NEW `DC-CRYPTO-10` (`tier = derived`, `enforced`, `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-AC"`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh`, `cross_ref = [CN-KES-HEADER-01, T-KEY-01, DC-CRYPTO-04, DC-CRYPTO-09, CN-FORGE-03]`). Strengthened (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AC"`): `CN-KES-HEADER-01` (the KES-signs-the-real-unsigned-header-pre-image invariant now ALSO covers period evolution — the signed pre-image is at the EVOLVED current period, not a stale minted-at-0 period). **One NEW CI gate (137 -> 138): `ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh`** — pins that the forge real KES sign uses `kes_sign_header_advancing` (NOT the raw `kes_sign_header` / `kes_sign_at`), that `kes_sign_header_advancing` calls `kes_advance_to(period)` VERBATIM before signing (no `period ± N` mutation), and that `kes_update` retains BOTH fail-closed guards (`EvolutionBackwards` + `EvolutionExhausted`); the standing `ci_check_no_signing_in_blue.sh` remains the BLUE `T-KEY-01` fence. **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** N-AC makes the RED signing shell EVOLVE the operator key to the requested period before signing — and nothing more. The Sum6KES evolution is the EXISTING deterministic `kes_update` primitive (reused, not re-implemented); signing stays **RED** (`T-KEY-01` preserved — no signing in BLUE); the BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + KES verifier + forge eligibility + wire rules are UNCHANGED. There is **NO new BLUE canonical type or authority** (`kes_sign_header_advancing` is a RED `&mut self` method; 458 unchanged); the period is passed **VERBATIM** (no manual `± N` adjustment); the evolution is **fail-closed both directions** (backwards / beyond-lifetime -> structured error + NO signature, never a key override); and there is **NO RO-LIVE flip** — a forged + self-accepted period-1 block that the real cardano-node DOWNLOADS with no KES/parse rejection is a wire-layer/header-acceptance event, NOT operator-witnessed bounty acceptance (`RO-LIVE-01` stays `partial` / operator-gated; the period-1 follower-adopt is genesis-density-window-limited (`CandidateTooSparse`, KES-INDEPENDENT) on a from-genesis net — cross-period forge->adopt is proven on the dense C2 tip path, not a net reset). Two pre-existing fail-closed INFO items are handed to C2 (recorded in the registry `evidence_notes`): (1) `kes_advance_to` zeroes the key on a FAILED advance (`std::mem::replace` before `kes_update`) — UNREACHABLE via the forge (the `kes_period_in_window` + `kes_period_for_slot` pre-check bounds the period before `kes_sign_header_advancing` is ever called), fail-safe (a zero key signs nothing the peer accepts); (2) the opcert window upper bound `opcert_start + 63` can diverge from the absolute Sum6KES ceiling 63 when `opcert_start > 0` (real preprod opcerts) — still fail-closed (`EvolutionExhausted`), but the C2 config must derive `kes_max_period` from the absolute ceiling, not `opcert_start + 63`.

> > **PHASE4-N-AB delta (outbound mux segmentation — the GREEN session reducer SEGMENTS a large outbound mini-protocol payload into ordered `<= MAX_PAYLOAD` mux frames, the outbound inverse of `CN-SESS-04` inbound reassembly — `CN-SESS-05`):** **GREEN-ONLY — ZERO BLUE diff** (458 canonical types unchanged; `mux::frame` reused unchanged — verified mechanically: `git diff 5c9f6cf6..c6e7fafe` over the BLUE `core_paths` trees touches **no** file). The single source file changed in the whole span is the GREEN `crates/ade_network/src/session/core.rs` (`//! GREEN session driver`, PHASE4-N-L). The cluster closed in 1 slice (S1 cluster/slice docs + impl `c6e7fafe`). Before N-AB, the session reducer reassembled INBOUND frames per mini-protocol (`CN-SESS-04`) but had no symmetric OUTBOUND path: an outbound payload larger than the `MAX_PAYLOAD` mux-frame limit (e.g. a Conway block-fetch response exceeding 65535 bytes) hit `encode_inner_frame`'s strict single-frame `MAX_PAYLOAD` guard and failed — so the producer-side serve could not transmit a large block over the wire. **S1 (CN-SESS-05 outbound segmentation):** `handle_outbound` (in `session::core`) now splits a payload with `MAX_PAYLOAD < len <= MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` into ordered `<= MAX_PAYLOAD` chunks (`payload.chunks(MAX_PAYLOAD)`), each encoded via the SAME single-frame `encode_inner_frame` authority (the outbound inverse of the `CN-SESS-04` inbound `drain_protocol_items` reassembly); every segment carries the SAME mini-protocol id + mode and the SAME single captured `timestamp` (GREEN — no per-segment clock read); an empty payload still emits exactly one (empty) frame; the ordered frame bytes are concatenated into one `SessionEffect::SendBytes`, and the receiver's demux + `CN-SESS-04` reassembly reconstructs the original — byte-preserving and lossless (`concat(segment payloads) == payload`). A payload ABOVE the NEW GREEN const `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES: usize = 16 * 1024 * 1024` (16 MiB — the symmetric outbound counterpart of the receive-side `MAX_REASSEMBLY_TAIL_BYTES = 16 MiB`; FIXED / closed / non-configurable — no CLI/env/config escape) fails closed with `SessionError::OutboundPayloadTooLarge { len }` BEFORE any segmentation. `encode_inner_frame` stays the STRICT single-frame encoder (its own `MAX_PAYLOAD` guard is preserved — it is never called with a chunk larger than `MAX_PAYLOAD`). **Registry → 335 rules**: NEW `CN-SESS-05` (`tier = derived`, `enforced`, `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-AB"`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_outbound_segmentation.sh`, `cross_ref = [CN-SESS-04, DC-LIVEMEM-01, CN-WIRE-08, DC-SERVEMEM-01, DC-CONS-17]`). Strengthened (`strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AB"`): `CN-SESS-04` (the inbound per-mini-protocol reassembly invariant now has its symmetric outbound inverse — the reassembly contract is restated as a round-trip: segment-then-reassemble is byte-identical) and `DC-SERVEMEM-01` (the bounded-serve path now also bounds the outbound frame-segmentation work via the fixed `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` ceiling). **One NEW CI gate (136 → 137): `ci_check_outbound_segmentation.sh`** — pins that `handle_outbound` segments a `> MAX_PAYLOAD` payload into ordered `<= MAX_PAYLOAD` frames via the single `encode_inner_frame` authority (no second/parallel frame encoder), that every segment keeps the same mini-protocol id + mode + the single captured timestamp (no per-segment clock), that segmentation never truncates / drops / reorders bytes, and that a payload above the FIXED non-configurable `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` fails closed (`OutboundPayloadTooLarge`, no escape hatch). **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** N-AB makes the outbound wire path SEGMENT large payloads into legal mux frames — and nothing more. It is the **GREEN, deterministic** inverse of the `CN-SESS-04` inbound reassembly; it transmits bytes the producer already produced, it does **NOT** decide which block is served, **NOT** advance a durable tip, and **NOT** make any peer-acceptance claim (`RO-LIVE-01` stays `partial` / operator-gated). There is **NO new BLUE canonical type** (`MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` is a GREEN const; 458 unchanged); **NO second frame encoder** (`encode_inner_frame` stays the single single-frame authority — `mux::frame` reused unchanged); **NO truncation / drop / reorder** (lossless, byte-preserving, ordered); **NO per-segment clock** (one captured `timestamp` reused — determinism preserved); and the upper bound is a **fixed, non-configurable** ceiling that fails closed above it (`OutboundPayloadTooLarge`), never an unbounded outbound buffer.

> > **PHASE4-N-AA delta (bounded peer-driven serve range — the `--mode node` serve path bounds per-request work and fails closed on oversized/inverted/undecodable ranges — `DC-SERVEMEM-01`):** **RED-ONLY — ZERO BLUE diff** (458 canonical types unchanged; no BLUE struct/enum/fn added — verified mechanically: `git diff 4e358e92..5c9f6cf6` over the BLUE `core_paths` trees adds **zero** `^+(pub )?(struct\|enum)` lines, and the lone BLUE-tree file touched, `ade_ledger/src/block_validity/mod.rs`, gains only a `// Core Contract:` comment header). The cluster closed in 2 slices + a security-review fix (S1 cluster/slice docs `a6e184e8`/`f34a2229`, impl `6b8f1779`; S2 slice doc `1bed02e3`, impl `3d853ec0`; security-review MEDIUM `5c9f6cf6`). It is the **serve-side analog of `DC-LIVEMEM-01`** (the receive-side bounded-memory cap) and closes the **PHASE4-N-U cross-slice security-review MEDIUM finding** (peer-driven serve resource amplification: the N-U serve-as-projection read via the unbounded `iter_from_slot`, which MATERIALIZES the full `from..tip` range and recovers each block's hash via a per-block `SLOT_BY_HASH` index scan — O(N²) — plus an O(N) `tip()`; a malicious peer could request an unbounded range and amplify storage/CPU before the BLUE decode). **S1 (CE-1 bounded read primitives):** the RED `ChainDb` trait (`ade_runtime::chaindb::contract` hosts the contract tests; `chaindb/mod.rs` carries the trait + signatures) gains TWO methods — `range_bytes_capped(from: SlotNo, to: SlotNo, max: usize) -> Result<CappedSlotRange, ChainDbError>` (a bounded, **hash-free**, slot-ascending read of `[from, to]` that reads at most `max + 1` blocks LAZILY, sets `CappedSlotRange.truncated = true` when the range held MORE than `max`, recovers NO hash — so NO `SLOT_BY_HASH` scan — and guards an inverted range `from > to` as empty) and `last_block_bytes() -> Result<Option<(SlotNo, Vec<u8>)>, ChainDbError>` (O(log N) tip — no full iteration, no hash scan; the serve derives the tip hash + `block_no` from the bytes). Both impls implement them — `PersistentChainDb` (redb) + `InMemoryChainDb` — with the inverted-range guard; 5 contract tests run against BOTH impls. The NEW RED value type `CappedSlotRange { blocks: Vec<(SlotNo, Vec<u8>)>, truncated: bool }` lives in `chaindb/types.rs`. `iter_from_slot` / `tip` are **doc-fenced as full/TRUSTED-CALLER-only** (recovery / rollback / node startup) — their internals are unchanged; the doc-fence directs the peer-driven serve path to the bounded primitives instead. **S2 (DC-SERVEMEM-01 serve projection cap + fail-closed):** `ade_runtime::network::served_chain_projection::ChainDbServedSource` `range_bytes` / `next_after` / `tip` now read via the S1 bounded primitives (never `iter_from_slot` / `chaindb.tip()`); a per-request cap `const MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS: usize = 256` (symmetric with `MAX_WIRE_PUMP_LOOKAHEAD`; FIXED / closed / non-configurable — no CLI/env/config escape, no unbounded mode); a NEW closed RED enum `ServeRangeOutcome { Served(Vec<(SlotNo, Hash32, Vec<u8>)>) | Empty | CapExceeded | ReadError }` distinguishes the four internal reasons (every non-`Served` variant maps to an empty `Vec` → the BLUE reducer's wire `NoBlocks`); the block hash is derived from each block's own bytes via the single BLUE `decode_block` authority (NO second hash authority, NO `SLOT_BY_HASH` reference on the serve path); and the serve fails closed — `CapExceeded` on an oversized range (decided BY THE BOUND, before any decode), `Empty` on an out-of-chain or inverted window, `ReadError` on an undecodable in-range block (the serve never emits a block it cannot authenticate via `decode_block`). **Security-review MEDIUM (`5c9f6cf6`):** the S2 cross-slice review added an explicit inverted-range (`from > to`, incl. `from = u64::MAX`) guard in the `chaindb` `range_bytes_capped` impls so a peer that controls both endpoints gets an empty result and NEVER a panic. **Registry → 334 rules**: NEW `DC-SERVEMEM-01` (`tier = derived`, `enforced`, `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-AA"`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_serve_range_bounded.sh`, `cross_ref = [DC-LIVEMEM-01, DC-NODE-13, DC-NODE-07, CN-CONS-07, DC-CONS-17]`). **One NEW CI gate (135 → 136): `ci_check_serve_range_bounded.sh`** — non-vacuous (pre-S2 HEAD had 2 `iter_from_slot` + 1 `chaindb.tip()` serve calls that its Guards 2/3 fire on; S2 has 0): pins that the serve projection reads via the S1 hash-free bounded primitives (never the unbounded `iter_from_slot` / O(N) `chaindb.tip()`), caps each request at the FIXED non-configurable `MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS` literal (no escape hatch / unbounded mode), and derives each block's hash via the single BLUE `decode_block` (no second hash authority, no `SLOT_BY_HASH` on the serve path). **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** N-AA is a **defensive resource bound on the read-only serve path** — and nothing more. The cap is an **implementation bound, NOT a Cardano semantic parameter** (it does not change which chain is served, only the per-request work ceiling) and **cannot be disabled at runtime**. There is **NO new canonical / BLUE type** (`CappedSlotRange` + `ServeRangeOutcome` are RED storage/serve value types — explicitly NOT canonical-counted); **NO second hash authority** (the serve derives the hash via the single BLUE `decode_block`; the bounded primitive is hash-FREE); **NO new dispatch authority** (the single `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound` is unchanged — DC-NODE-07 preserved; `ServeRangeOutcome` is an internal serve-read outcome, not a dispatch); the trusted recovery/rollback `iter_from_slot` internals are **OUT OF SCOPE** (doc-fenced, not peer-driven — unchanged); and there is **NO RO-LIVE flip** — bounding serve work ≠ operator-witnessed peer acceptance (`RO-LIVE-01` stays `partial` / operator-gated). It is a pre-RO-LIVE hardening item.

> > **PHASE4-N-F-G-R delta (stable served block 0 via a monotone serve gate — `DC-NODE-11`; mechanism SUPERSEDED by N-U S3 serve-as-projection):** **NO BLUE crate changed** (458 canonical types unchanged). RED-only on the `--mode node` serve spine (`ade_node::node_lifecycle`, `//! RED`). Two commits — S1 impl `32e4498b`, doc `f17413f5`, close `0d7624d4`. The genesis-successor rehearsal exposed a served-chain INSTABILITY: a freshly cold-start-forged block 0 could be re-proposed / re-served as the served tip churned, so a follower that had already adopted block 0 saw a non-monotone served chain. G-R adds a **monotone serve gate** in the node-spine serve sibling: once block 0 (the genesis successor) is served, the served tip only ever advances — a candidate that would move the served chain backward (or re-serve an already-served height with a different hash) is refused, so the follower adopts a **stable served block 0**. **Registry → 328 rules**: NEW `DC-NODE-11` (`tier = derived`, `enforced`, `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-F-G-R"`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_served_chain_stability.sh`). **One NEW CI gate (133 → 134): `ci_check_served_chain_stability.sh`** — pins the monotone serve gate (served tip never regresses; an already-served height is not re-served with a divergent hash). **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** G-R is a **served-chain STABILITY** fix on the read-only serve path — and nothing more. It makes the served tip monotone so a genesis-successor follower adopts a stable block 0; it is **NOT** a durable-tip advance (the forge engine still holds no `ChainDb` handle), **NOT** a peer-acceptance claim (`RO-LIVE-01` stays `partial` / operator-gated), and **NOT** an RO-LIVE flip. The fix lives in the serve sibling spawned OUTSIDE `run_relay_loop`; `run_relay_loop`'s containment gate is byte-/semantically unchanged. The live C1 leg stays operator-gated; the C1 evidence (below) is reproduction, not a bounty-completion claim.

> > **PHASE4-N-F-G-Q delta (forge-successor position from the evolved admitted spine state — `DC-NODE-10`):** **NO BLUE crate changed** (458 canonical types unchanged). RED-only (`ade_node::{node_sync, node_lifecycle}`, `//! RED`). Three commits — S1 impl `bd85892b`, doc `24c00644`, close `cd0d9d48`. After the genesis-successor block 0 is admitted, the NEXT forge (`block_number 1+`) must derive its `(block_number, prev_hash)` from the **evolved admitted spine state** — the position the just-admitted block established — not from the stale recovered tip. Pre-G-Q this re-used the recovered base and the successor forge crashed (`prev_hash`/`block_number` mismatch against the admitted block 0). > > **PHASE4-N-F-G-M delta (real cardano-node ChainSync FindIntersect compat — scoped indefinite decode + Origin reply — `CN-WIRE-11`):** **ONE NEW BLUE canonical type** — the closed `ArrayHead = Definite(u64) | Indefinite` in `ade_network::codec::primitives` (the codec BLUE submodule count `38 → 39`, total **457 → 458**) — plus the additive BLUE **fn** `decode_array_head_two_form(protocol, data, offset) -> Result<ArrayHead, …>` (a fn, no struct/enum). G-M (a) adds the **scoped** two-form array-head decode (`decode_find_intersect_points` accepts BOTH the definite `9f…` and indefinite forms; on `Indefinite` the caller consumes the matching `0xff` break; **no catch-all**, scoped to FindIntersect per `CN-WIRE-11` — NOT a general replacement for `decode_array_header`), and (b) makes `ade_network::chain_sync::server` answer **`IntersectFound[Origin]`** for an `Origin` point (the universal common ancestor — matching the real cardano-node, which answers `IntersectFound[Origin]` even with an empty served chain). Pinned against captured cardano-node 11.0.1 FindIntersect/IntersectFound fixtures. The `275a2318` follow-up scopes the chain-sync round-trip corpus to mux-framed captures (a test-corpus scope fix, not authority). **Registry → 322 rules**: NEW `CN-WIRE-11` (`tier = derived`, `enforced`, `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-F-G-M"`, `ci_script = ci/ci_check_chainsync_findintersect_compat.sh`). **One NEW CI gate (128 → 129): `ci_check_chainsync_findintersect_compat.sh`** — pins the scoped two-form FindIntersect decode + the `Origin → IntersectFound[Origin]` reply against the real-node fixtures. **Boundary honesty (load-bearing — do NOT soften / do NOT broaden):** G-M widens the ChainSync wire grammar to match the real cardano-node `FindIntersect` shape — and nothing more. The indefinite-length acceptance is **SCOPED to FindIntersect** (`decode_array_head_two_form` is NOT a general definite/indefinite decoder; the rest of the closed wire grammar stays definite-only); the `Origin` reply matches the spec/real-node behavior (the universal common ancestor), it does **NOT** widen the served chain. `ArrayHead` is a closed 2-variant enum; the change is additive to the BLUE codec authority, **NO** parallel codec, **NO** RO-LIVE flip.

---

## Conventions

- A **module** in Ade is a Cargo workspace crate (smallest independently-buildable unit). Source: `Cargo.toml` `[workspace] members` (11 entries). One exception to crate-granularity: `ade_network` is split by *submodule color* — `.idd-config.json` `core_paths` resolves BLUE at the submodule path level (9 paths), so its BLUE / GREEN / RED submodules are documented as separate entries.
- Several BLUE crates host sub-trees that carry a *different* TCB color by their own module banner; the RED `ade_runtime` and `ade_node` crates host numerous **GREEN-by-content** sub-trees. These are surfaced as sub-classification notes inside the owning crate's entry (or, where load-bearing, as their own GREEN/RED entries below).
- Modules are listed by TCB color (BLUE → GREEN → RED), alphabetical within each color.

### TCB color sources (in order of authority)

1. `.idd-config.json` `core_paths` — substring match against absolute path. BLUE crate prefixes: `ade_codec`, `ade_types`, `ade_crypto`, `ade_core`, `ade_ledger`, `ade_plutus`. Plus the 9 BLUE `ade_network` submodule paths: `mux/frame.rs`, `codec/`, `handshake/`, `chain_sync/`, `block_fetch/`, `tx_submission/`, `keep_alive/`, `peer_sharing/`, `n2c/`.
2. `.idd-config.json` `_core_paths_doc` — `ade_runtime` is RED; `ade_testkit` is GREEN; `ade_node` is RED; `ade_network::mux::transport` + `ade_network::session` are nominally RED (but `session/` is GREEN-by-content per PHASE4-N-L). `ade_core_interop` is RED.
3. **Module doc-comment banners** — every BLUE/GREEN source file opens with the `// Core Contract:` banner (the `ade_network` BLUE submodules use this first-line form) and/or a `//! BLUE …` / `//! GREEN …` / `//! RED …` line. This is the per-file authority that distinguishes GREEN-by-content from RED inside `ade_runtime` / `ade_node`. Verified directly against the tree at HEAD `65954fa3` for every new/changed module in this catch-up span: `ade_network::handshake::version_table.rs` + `chain_sync/server.rs` + `codec/{chain_sync,primitives}.rs` carry the BLUE `// Core Contract:` banner (BLUE `core_paths`, additive type/fn — no color change); `ade_ledger::seed_consensus_inputs.rs` → `//! BLUE` + `consensus_view.rs` → `//! BLUE`; `ade_runtime::admission/wire_pump.rs` → `//! RED`, `bootstrap.rs` → `//! GREEN`, `seed_consensus_merge.rs` → `//! GREEN`, `{genesis_bootstrap,mithril_bootstrap}.rs` → RED/GREEN composers; `ade_node::{node_lifecycle,node_sync}.rs` → `//! RED`; `ade_testkit::consensus::genesis_pinning.rs` → `// GREEN`.
4. Cluster TCB Color Maps under `docs/clusters/` and `docs/clusters/completed/` — §5 "TCB color map (FC/IS partition)" of each `cluster.md`.
5. The invariant registry `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml` (347 rules at HEAD) — each rule's `code_locus` + `statement` is the authoritative source for the **MUST NOT** rows below.

### Active cluster at HEAD

**What the binary `Node` arm actually runs (precise wiring honesty, updated for the catch-up span):**
- `main()` `Mode::Node → run_node_lifecycle → run_node_lifecycle_inner`. Bootstrap + recovery are fully wired and durable (first run `first_run_mithril_bootstrap`; non-empty store `warm_start_recovery` → WAL replay → verified recovered `BootstrapState`). **G-N (NEW):** WarmStart now overlays the recovered `epoch_nonce` (eta0) from the seed-epoch sidecar onto `chain_dep.epoch_nonce`, so the forge VRF input is `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)` (a recovered follower no longer fails `VRFKeyBadProof`).
- Forge intent (`Off`/`On(paths)`/`PartialKeySet`), forge constants from the recovered current ledger view, real opcert/genesis parsers, `checked_millis_to_slot` slot guard, `forge_epoch_admission` off-epoch guard, and the self-accept→serve handoff are carried (G-A/G-B unchanged).
- **G-J cold-start forge (carried):** the `ForgeTick` arm derives `(block_number, prev_hash)` via `node_sync::forge_header_position`; a both-`None` tip cold-starts block 0 + `PrevHash::Genesis` through `run_real_forge → self_accept → SelfAcceptedHandoff` when `may_cold_start_forge` holds.
- **G-Q forge-successor position (NEW):** after block 0 is admitted, the NEXT forge derives `(last_admitted_block_no + 1, PrevHash::Block(last_admitted_hash))` from the **evolved admitted spine state** — not the stale recovered tip — yielding the first stable node (block 1+, no successor crash). The forge engine still holds no `ChainDb` handle (no durable tip; N-U).
- **G-P feed header-validation view (NEW):** the live feed validates header Step 5 + ledger Step 7 against the recovered consensus surface's leader-threshold stake distribution (`from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`), so a valid live block 0 is ingested (`VerificationFailed` gone).
- **G-O feed tag-24 unwrap (NEW):** the live `WirePump` (`ade_runtime::admission::wire_pump`) strips the peer's BlockFetch `MsgBlock` tag-24 envelope via `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24` BEFORE the BLUE decode (`UnexpectedType` gone).
- **G-K/G-L/G-M serve-side (NEW):** the serve sibling stays up serving past feed-end (G-K, `DC-NODE-09`), advertises a per-version cardano-node-compatible N2N `versionData` via `encode_n2n_version_params` (G-L, `CN-WIRE-10`, fixes `TInt 1`), and answers a real follower's indefinite-length `FindIntersect` / `Origin` with `IntersectFound[Origin]` (G-M, `CN-WIRE-11`).
- **G-R served-chain stability (carried; mechanism SUPERSEDED by N-U S3):** the monotone serve gate that kept the served tip from regressing is retired — the durable-chain serve projection (below) provides the same stability more strongly (`DC-NODE-11`).
- **N-U forged-block durability (NEW):** the ForgeTick arm now routes the self-accepted forged block through the fenced `node_sync::admit_forged_block_durably` → `pump_block` durable chokepoint, so the forge's own block becomes **durable** (the durable tip advances; the next forge builds N+1 on it; a stale-tip forge fails closed — `DC-NODE-12` / `DC-CONS-23` / `DC-WAL-04`); `warm_start_recovery` recovers a forged-block durable tip byte-identically + drops an un-WAL'd orphan (`T-REC-05`); and the `--mode node` served view is now a deterministic READ-ONLY **projection of the durable ChainDb** (`ChainDbServedSource` over `ServedChainSource::DurableChainDb`) — a follower fetches coherent durable history A→B and serving survives restart (`DC-NODE-13`). The forge still advances no tip DIRECTLY (`pump_block` is the sole durable tip authority). **NO RO-LIVE flip** — durability + coherent serve ≠ operator-witnessed peer acceptance (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated).
- **N-AA bounded peer-driven serve (NEW):** the `--mode node` durable-chain serve projection (`ChainDbServedSource`) now reads via the bounded hash-free `ChainDb` primitives `range_bytes_capped` / `last_block_bytes` (never the unbounded `iter_from_slot` / O(N) `tip()`), caps each peer request at the FIXED non-configurable `MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS = 256` (closed `ServeRangeOutcome`), derives each served block's hash via the single BLUE `decode_block`, and fails closed on an oversized (`CapExceeded`), out-of-chain / inverted (`Empty`), or undecodable (`ReadError`) range — every non-served outcome maps to the reducer's wire `NoBlocks` (`DC-SERVEMEM-01`). A defensive resource bound on the read-only serve path; **NO RO-LIVE flip** (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated).
- **N-AC KES period evolution before sign (NEW):** the forge's single real KES sign now goes through `ProducerShell::kes_sign_header_advancing` — the RED signing shell EVOLVES the minted-at-period-0 operator KES key forward to the chain's current KES period (`kes_advance_to(period)` -> the deterministic Sum6KES `kes_update`) BEFORE signing, so a leader slot in KES period > 0 no longer fails `KesPeriodNotCurrent`; a backwards period (`EvolutionBackwards`) or a period beyond the key lifetime (`EvolutionExhausted`) fails closed with NO signature (`DC-CRYPTO-10`). Signing stays RED; the period is passed verbatim; the BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + KES verifier are unchanged. **NO RO-LIVE flip** — a period-1 block the real cardano-node downloads with no KES/parse rejection is a header-acceptance event, not operator-witnessed bounty acceptance (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated).
- **N-AE recover→serve continuity + forge-on-followed-tip admissibility (NEW):** on the recovered/following `--mode node` path, the ForgeTick arm REMOVES the recovered-anchor (`recovered.tip`) forge-base fallback and calls `node_sync::forge_followed_tip_admission` BEFORE the single fenced `forge_one_from_recovered` — a forge is admissible ONLY when `durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip` (canonical hash AND `block_no`), else it records a typed `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp` (no forge, no state transition, tip unchanged) (`DC-NODE-15`); a `CaughtUp` forge builds on `prev_hash = PrevHash::Block(selected_tip.hash)` with `block_no + 1` (`DC-CONS-24`). The `--mode node` durable-chain serve projection (`ChainDbServedSource::intersect`) gains a FindIntersect-ONLY second clause projecting the forge PARENT (the earliest servable StoredBlock's `prev_hash`) so a relay holding that parent rolls forward onto the forged successor — NO bytes are served for the projected point (BlockFetch refuses structurally), recover-only ⇒ no projection (`DC-NODE-14`). After `producer_chain_sync_serve` answers `IntersectFound(point)` at a non-Origin point, the read cursor IS that point so the next `RequestNext` serves the successor, not block 0 (`DC-PROTO-10`). The first followed `AdmitBlock` seeds its WAL `prior_fp` from the recovered post-state fp (recover→follow continuity; `DC-WAL-02` / `T-REC-05`). The followed-peer-tip signal is an ADMISSIBILITY input ONLY (never reaches a chain selector). **NO RO-LIVE flip** — a recovered node that forges a peer-adoptable successor is the C2 mechanism, not operator-witnessed acceptance (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated).
- **N-AF single-producer extend-own-durable-spine (carried; SUPERSEDED by N-AH):** a DECLARED single-producer venue could forge on Ade's OWN durable spine WITHOUT a relay echo after an explicit RED venue-adoption certificate matched by chain-point identity (hash + block_no), fail-closed `ForgeRefused::SingleProducerFenceViolation` (`DC-NODE-18`). The default `VenueRole::Unknown` path stays the verbatim DC-NODE-15 gate. N-AH folded out the `FirstOwnBlockServed` cert-wait + removed the cert.
- **N-AG single-producer loop-continuation-after-feed-EOF (NEW):** in a certified single-producer venue already in the extend state, a `LoopState::Ending` caused SOLELY by a structural feed EOF no longer terminates the forge loop — `plan_loop_step`'s GREEN 5th `VenuePolicy` input (`ContinueInSingleProducerExtend`) continues forging the own certified spine, fenced to the 7 certified-run conditions, until operator shutdown / a fatal error / a BLUE forge-validity bound / a competing chain (`DC-NODE-19`). `pump_block` stays the sole durable tip-advance authority; feed work still drains via `SyncOnce` first. **NO RO-LIVE flip.**
- **N-AH local selected durable chain forge-base authority (NEW):** after Ade self-admits a valid forged block through `pump_block`, the next forge base is Ade's LOCAL SELECTED DURABLE TIP (`ChainDb::tip`) — NOT `followed_peer_tip` and NOT a cert; the extend state is entered DIRECTLY on self-admit (`forge_mode_after_admit`, the `FirstOwnBlockServed` intermediate folded out) under the 6-condition fence (observed-feed competing-block fail-closed — NOT fork-choice); `forge_followed_tip_admission` stays the INITIAL catch-up gate (DC-NODE-15, phase-split). The adoption certificate is REMOVED from `ade_node` (evidence-only, harness-owned; `DC-NODE-21`). Warm-start re-enters the extend state on the recovered own-spine `ChainDb::tip` without a fresh catch-up (`warm_start_forge_mode`, `DC-NODE-22`; the `replayed_anchor_block_no` recovery summary comes from `BootstrapState`). The forge-base decision is witnessed by the closed `NodeSchedEvent::ForgeBaseSelected` sched transcript (CN-NODE-04 / DC-NODE-20). `pump_block` stays the sole durable tip-advance authority; `DC-CONS-03` untouched. **NO RO-LIVE flip** — the run-4 transcript (a real Haskell relay adopting cert-free local-tip-forged blocks, sustained > k across a follow-link EOF + a restart) is the C2-LOCAL rung-1 mechanism, not operator-witnessed acceptance.
- **N-AI live fork-choice rollback-follow (single-best-peer FOLLOW, NOT full ChainSel) (NEW):** on the live Participant `--mode node` receive path, every peer-origin item is classified ONCE venue-blind by the GREEN-by-function `node_sync::classify_receive(durable_tip, candidate) -> ReceiveClass {AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | Competing}`, then `resolve_disposition(class, venue)` splits by venue: `VenueRole::SingleProducer`/`Unknown` => `RefuseSingleProducer` (the DC-NODE-20 rung-1 fail-closed, byte-unchanged — `run_node_sync` returns `NodeSyncError::UnexpectedRollback` on any `NodeSyncItem::RollBack`); `VenueRole::Participant` => `NeedsForkChoice`, routed to the EXISTING `ade_runtime::consensus::chain_selector` orchestrator → BLUE `select_best_chain` (DC-CONS-03). The ordered live feed now carries rollbacks as `NodeSyncItem::RollBack(Point)` interleaved at their exact position; `run_participant_sync` resolves a `RollBackward(point)` against the durable `ChainDb` (the stored slot+hash is the SOLE authority — peer slot must equal stored slot for the hash, else fail closed BEFORE any mutation; `DC-NODE-29`), constructs `ChainEvent::RolledBack`, and `apply_chain_event` applies it durably via `materialize_rolled_back_state` (CN-STORE-07) → lockstep `commit_rollback` (DC-CONS-20) → an append-only `WalEntry::RollBack` MARKER (`DC-NODE-25`), then reconciles the orchestrator tip to the durable `ChainDb::tip` (`DC-NODE-26`). A pending fork-choice re-selection DISABLES forging (`ForgeActivation.pending_reselection` → `pending_reselection_forge_refusal` → typed `ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending`; the forge never builds on a stale pre-resolution local tip — `DC-NODE-28`). `pump_block` stays the sole roll-forward durable admit (a fork-choice win is durably adopted ONLY when its BODIES validate+apply; no header-only tip advance). Replay re-invokes the SAME materialize/reducer authority at the recorded `WalEntry::RollBack` point (byte-identical recovery incl. rollback+reselection — `DC-NODE-27`). **NO RO-LIVE flip** — single-best-peer rollback-follow is the C2 rung-2 mechanism, NOT operator-witnessed bounty acceptance; full multi-peer ChainSel is out of scope and `CN-CONS-03` stays partial.
- **Empty-source honesty (no-`--peer` arm, carried).** With no `--peer`, the source is empty and the planner halts before any `SyncOnce` / `ForgeTick` (unless a cold-start is permitted). The `On` arm is **forge-CAPABLE but not observable** without a live feed. An operator-witnessed accepted block is the `RO-LIVE-01` follow-on.

## BLUE Modules — Pure Functional Core

> **Shared header (applies to every BLUE entry below).** Every `.rs` source file begins with the `// Core Contract:` banner, and the following deny attributes are present in each crate's `lib.rs` (or, for `ade_network`, at the crate root — BLUE submodules inherit them):
> `#![deny(unsafe_code)]`, `#![deny(clippy::unwrap_used)]`, `#![deny(clippy::expect_used)]`, `#![deny(clippy::panic)]`, `#![deny(clippy::float_arithmetic)]`.
>
> Cross-cutting BLUE CI gates (all scope the full BLUE set — 6 BLUE crates + 9 BLUE `ade_network` submodule paths): `ci_check_module_headers.sh`, `ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh`, `ci_check_dependency_boundary.sh`, `ci_check_no_signing_in_blue.sh`, `ci_check_no_semantic_cfg.sh`, `ci_check_hash_uses_wire_bytes.sh`, `ci_check_ingress_chokepoints.sh`, `ci_check_pallas_quarantine.sh`, `ci_check_no_async_in_blue.sh`.
>
> Narrow BLUE / wire / forge gates carried + extended through this catch-up span: the N-W `ci_check_producer_praos_vrf.sh` (CN-FORGE-04), the N-X `ci_check_tag24_wire_authority.sh` (CN-WIRE-08), the N-Y `ci_check_forward_sync_chokepoint_only.sh` (DC-SYNC-01) / `ci_check_mithril_uses_bootstrap_initial_state.sh` (CN-MITHRIL-01) / `ci_check_no_haskell_fingerprint_equality.sh` (DC-COMPAT-01), the workspace-wide `ci_check_registry_code_locus_exists.sh`, the N-F-A `ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh` (CN-CINPUT-02), the N-F-G-J `ci_check_prevhash_single_wire_authority.sh` (CN-WIRE-09). **This span ADDED to the wire-authority + recovered-surface family:** `ci_check_n2n_handshake_versiondata_authority.sh` (G-L, CN-WIRE-10 — the single per-version N2N `versionData` encoder `encode_n2n_version_params`), `ci_check_chainsync_findintersect_compat.sh` (G-M, CN-WIRE-11 — the scoped two-form FindIntersect decode + the Origin→IntersectFound reply against real-node fixtures), `ci_check_feed_tag24_unwrap.sh` (G-O, CN-WIRE-12 — feed-side `unwrap_tag24` before decode), and `ci_check_warmstart_eta0_overlay.sh` (G-N, T-REC-04 + DC-CINPUT-03 — the eta0 sidecar field + WarmStart overlay; touches the BLUE `seed_consensus_inputs` codec). The G-K/G-P/G-Q/G-R gates (`ci_check_node_serve_lifetime.sh`, `ci_check_feed_leader_threshold_view.sh`, `ci_check_forge_successor_evolved_spine.sh`, `ci_check_served_chain_stability.sh`) are RED-spine gates in `ade_node` (not BLUE-set gates). The two BLUE-file touches in this span are additive: the G-L `encode_n2n_version_params` + G-M `decode_array_head_two_form` fns and the closed G-M `ArrayHead` enum (BLUE deny/closed-enum gates apply unchanged), and the G-N `SeedEpochConsensusInputs.epoch_nonce` field under the bumped version gate. **PHASE4-N-AI ADDED to the BLUE-touching family:** `ci_check_wal_rollback_replay_equiv.sh` (DC-NODE-27 — the `WalEntry::RollBack` marker + the replay re-anchor that re-invokes the EXISTING `materialize_rolled_back_state` + `commit_rollback`, byte-identical recovery incl. rollback+reselection) and `ci_check_chain_selection_arrival_order_independent.sh` (CN-CONS-01 — the `#[cfg(test)]` arrival-order proof over the UNCHANGED `select_best_chain`). The lone new BLUE canonical types in the span are the `ade_ledger::wal::event::{RollbackPoint, RollbackReason}` payload types of the additive `WalEntry::RollBack` closed-sum variant (BLUE deny/closed-enum gates apply unchanged); `select_best_chain` production is byte-unchanged.

### `ade_codec`

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | Owns Cardano-canonical CBOR ingress — the only place in the workspace that turns raw bytes into typed semantic values, with wire-byte preservation for every hash-bearing structure. Owns the standalone opcert byte authority and the canonical Conway-tx preserved-byte splitter, the canonical block-envelope encoder `cbor::envelope::encode_block_envelope`, and (N-X) the single workspace **tag-24 CBOR-in-CBOR wire-envelope authority** `cbor::tag24::{wrap_tag24, unwrap_tag24}` + closed `TagEnvelopeError`. Also exposes the shared canonical CBOR read/write primitives the BLUE codecs in `ade_ledger` + `ade_network` build on. **N-F-G-J** owns the POSITION-BLIND header `prev_hash` codec `shelley::block::decode_prev_hash` (`null -> Genesis` / `hash32 -> Block`; CN-WIRE-09). |
| **Creates** | `PreservedCbor<T>`, `RawCbor`, `BlockEnvelope`, `ByronDecodedBlock`, `CodecContext`, `CodecError`, `ContainerEncoding`, `IntWidth`, era-tagged block/tx wrappers, `OpCertCodecError`, `TxComponents<'a>`, `TagEnvelopeError` (closed). 11 public types (byte-stable across the G-K…G-R span). |
| **Interprets** | All canonical Cardano CBOR. `unwrap_tag24` is the single workspace authority that strips a tag-24 (`0xd8 0x18`) envelope (zero-copy borrow, fail-closed `TagEnvelopeError`). **N-F-G-O (carried-as-consumer):** the feed-side RED `ade_runtime::admission::wire_pump` now calls `unwrap_tag24` before the BLUE decode — `ade_codec` stays the single tag-24 authority (no parallel parser). `shelley::block::decode_prev_hash` decodes the header `prev_hash` POSITION-BLIND (CN-WIRE-09). |
| **MUST NOT** | (1) Construct `PreservedCbor` outside `ade_codec`. (2) Re-encode wire bytes when computing hashes. (3) Use any forbidden BLUE pattern. (4) Depend on any workspace crate except `ade_types`. (5)–(11) per-construct prohibitions (Conway cert/withdrawals/governance, opcert, tx_components, single block-envelope encoder). (12) `cbor::tag24` (CN-WIRE-08) — `wrap_tag24`/`unwrap_tag24` defined exactly once; `unwrap_tag24` fails closed (never panic); no second/hand-rolled tag-24 parse anywhere (incl. the feed-side WirePump, which MUST reuse this authority — CN-WIRE-12). (13) `shelley::block::decode_prev_hash` (CN-WIRE-09) — the codec is the byte representation only and MUST stay POSITION-BLIND (no `block_number`); the position-aware coupling lives in `ade_ledger::block_validity::header_position`, never here. |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_ledger` (heavy), `ade_plutus`, `ade_testkit`, `ade_network`, `ade_runtime`, `ade_core_interop`, `ade_node`. |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_types`. std-only; dev-deps `serde_json`, `toml`. |
| **Entry points** | `ade_codec::cbor::envelope::{decode_block_envelope, encode_block_envelope}`, `ade_codec::{wrap_tag24, unwrap_tag24, TagEnvelopeError}`, the `cbor::{read_*, write_*_canonical, canonical_width, ContainerEncoding, IntWidth}` primitives, `ade_codec::traits::AdeEncode`, per-era `decode_*_block`, `ade_codec::shelley::{opcert::{encode_opcert, decode_opcert}, tx_components::split_conway_tx_components, block::decode_prev_hash}`. |
| **Key modules** | `cbor/` (incl. `envelope.rs`, `tag24.rs`), `byron/`, `shelley/` (incl. `block.rs`, `cert.rs`, `opcert.rs`, `tx_components.rs`), `allegra/`, `mary/`, `alonzo/`, `babbage/`, `conway/`, `address/`, `preserved.rs`, `traits.rs`, `primitives.rs`, `error.rs`. |

### `ade_core`

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | BLUE authoritative Praos consensus core — canonical types + pure state-transitions deciding which header/chain Ade accepts: HFC era schedule + slot↔era↔time (`EraSchedule::locate`), Praos chain-dep state, VRF cert verification + leader-eligibility, KES + op-cert period verification, header validation, fork-choice, header-level rollback, leader-schedule query, canonical encodings, producer-side opcert acceptance, the closed `consensus::leader_check` evaluator, and the single era→leader-VRF-input authority `consensus::vrf_cert::{leader_vrf_input, leader_value_for, praos_vrf_input}`. The `consensus::nonce` epoch-boundary transitions exist but are **undriven on the `--mode node` forge path** (DC-EPOCH-03). **G-N (carried-as-consumer):** `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)` is the function the WarmStart eta0 overlay feeds the recovered `epoch_nonce` into; `Nonce` (the type carried in the G-N sidecar field) is owned here in `consensus::praos_state`. **PHASE4-N-AI (production UNCHANGED):** `consensus::fork_choice::select_best_chain` stays the SOLE chain-selection authority (DC-CONS-03) and is byte-identical — the only `fork_choice.rs` change is a `#[cfg(test)]`-only arrival-order-permutation determinism proof (`select_best_chain` picks the same fork-choice-maximal tip regardless of candidate presentation order; CN-CONS-01, strengthened). The live N-AI rollback-follow path ROUTES a Participant-venue competing candidate through this UNCHANGED `select_best_chain` (via the `ade_runtime::consensus::chain_selector` orchestrator) — it adds no second selector. |
| **Creates** | Schedule (`BootstrapAnchorHash`, `EraSchedule`, `EraSummary`, `EraLocation`); State (`PraosChainDepState`, `OpCertCounterMap`, `Nonce`); Points/events (`Point`, `ChainHash`, `BlockDistance`, `SecurityParam`, `ChainEvent`, `ChainSelectionReject`); errors; header surface (`HeaderInput`, `HeaderVrf`, `HeaderKes`, `ValidatedHeaderSummary`, `HeaderApplied`); fork-choice; VRF/leader (`ExpectedVrfInput`, `ActiveSlotsCoeff`, `LeaderScheduleQuery/Answer`); `LedgerView` trait; rollback; `leader_check` types. 49 public types (byte-stable across the G-K…G-R span). |
| **Interprets** | Canonical inputs from the `ade_runtime` shell. KES check verifies the hot-KES signature via `ade_crypto::kes::verify_kes`. `leader_vrf_input(era, slot, eta0)` constructs the era-correct alpha; `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)` the Praos input (the G-N WarmStart-overlaid eta0 flows in here). `EraSchedule::locate(slot)` resolves era/epoch (consumed by the forge epoch guard). |
| **MUST NOT** | (1)–(14) consensus carry-forward (no I/O, no clock, no `ChainDb` in BLUE consensus, no density in fork-choice, closed consensus enums). (15) `consensus::leader_check` (CN-FORGE-02) — no `LedgerView`/`EraSchedule`/`ChainDepState`/wall-clock/storage/RED dep; observes no secret key; `NotEligible` carries only a bounded fingerprint. (16) `consensus::vrf_cert` leader-VRF authority (CN-FORGE-04) — `leader_vrf_input` is the single era→construction authority; no path accepts both TPraos and Praos inputs for one era; Praos producer alpha = validator alpha. |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_ledger`, `ade_runtime` (heavy), `ade_testkit`, `ade_core_interop`, `ade_node`. |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_types`, `ade_crypto`, `minicbor`. Dev-deps: `ade_testkit`, `serde_json`, `cardano-crypto`. |
| **Entry points** | `use ade_core::consensus::{…}`; `validate_and_apply_header`, `select_best_chain`, `apply_rollback`, `apply_nonce_input`, `apply_op_cert`, `query_leader_schedule`, `verify_vrf_cert`; `EraSchedule::locate`; `opcert_validate`; `leader_check::{verify_and_evaluate_leader, LeaderCheckVerdict}`; `vrf_cert::{ExpectedVrfInput, ActiveSlotsCoeff, leader_vrf_input, leader_value_for, praos_vrf_input, praos_leader_value}`; `praos_state::Nonce`. |
| **Key modules** | `consensus/{era_schedule, praos_state, events, errors, vrf_cert, kes_check, nonce, op_cert, leader_schedule, header_summary, header_validate, candidate, fork_choice, rollback, ledger_view, encoding, opcert_validate, leader_check}.rs`. |
