### `ade_crypto`

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | Pure cryptographic verification primitives — Blake2b hashing, Ed25519 / Byron-bootstrap signature verification, KES verification with op-certs, VRF verification, plus closed signature-artifact types. Verification only — signing lives in RED `ade_runtime::producer::signing`. Owns the Ade-native `Sum6KES Ed25519DSIGN` algorithm (`kes_sum/`), byte-identical to Haskell `cardano-base`. (Unchanged across the G-K…G-R span.) |
| **Creates** | `Blake2b224`, `Blake2b256`, `HashAlgorithm`, `Ed25519VerificationKey`, `Ed25519Signature`, `ByronExtendedVerificationKey`, `KesVerificationKey`, `KesPeriod`, `OperationalCertData`, `VrfVerificationKey`, `VrfProof`, `VrfOutput`, `CryptoError`, `KesSignature`, `SUM6_KES_SIG_LEN = 448`; `kes_sum::` (`KesAlgorithm`, `Sum0..6Kes`, signing-key/signature wrappers, closed `KesError`/`KesParseError`). 21 public types (byte-stable across the span). |
| **Interprets** | Already-decoded byte slices. `Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes` interprets the canonical 608-byte expanded cardano-cli skey; `raw_deserialize_signature_kes` the 448-byte signature. |
| **MUST NOT** | (1) Implement signing as a top-level `pub fn sign_*`. (2) Allocate global state. (3) Use any BLUE-forbidden pattern. (4) `unsafe` outside the allowlisted FFI in `vrf.rs`. (5) `build_opcert_signable` must produce the spec-correct concat. (6) `KesSignature` (DC-CRYPTO-04) closed length-pinned wrapper. (7) `kes_sum` (DC-CRYPTO-08) — no `cardano_crypto::kes::*` in production paths. (8) `kes_sum::hash::expand_seed` — Haskell prefix bytes `0x01`/`0x02`. (9) every `*SigningKey` hand-rolls zeroizing `Drop` + redacting `Debug`. (10) `kes_sum` corpus — no `.skey` files. (11) error variants carry only non-secret primitives. |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_core`, `ade_ledger`, `ade_plutus`, `ade_testkit`, `ade_core_interop`, `ade_runtime`, `ade_node`. |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_types`, `blake2`, `ed25519-dalek`, `cardano-crypto` (`["vrf-draft03", "kes-sum", "dsign"]`, `kes-sum` test-only oracle). |
| **Entry points** | `ade_crypto::{blake2b_256, blake2b_224}`, `verify_ed25519`, `verify_byron_bootstrap`, `verify_kes`, `verify_opcert`, `verify_vrf`, `ade_crypto::kes::{KesSignature, SUM6_KES_SIG_LEN, KesVerificationKey}`, `ade_crypto::kes_sum::{KesAlgorithm, Sum6Kes, KesError, KesParseError}`. |
| **Key modules** | `blake2b.rs`, `ed25519.rs`, `error.rs`, `kes.rs`, `kes_sum/`, `traits.rs`, `vrf.rs`. |

### `ade_ledger`

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | The functional core (ledger half): stateless ledger rules for every era; B1 block-validity verdict; B2 tx-validity verdict + mempool admission; B3 Conway value-conservation; B4/B5 closed Conway cert-state + governance-cert accumulation; live committee enactment; the single BLUE wire-ingress chokepoint `mempool::ingress::mempool_ingress`; the BLUE producer authority (`producer::{forge, self_accept, served_chain, state}`); the single body-hash authority (`block_body_hash`); the receive/rollback/snapshot/WAL/bootstrap-anchor/genesis-source authorities; the KES-signing pre-image recipe `block_validity::unsigned_header_pre_image`; the exact-`Rational` arithmetic; the `ProtocolParameters` model; (N-F-A) the closed `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` recovered-state record + its SOLE codec, the `PoolDistrView::from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` projection, and the WAL provenance variant; (N-F-G-J) the single POSITION-AWARE header authority `block_validity::header_position::check_header_position`. **N-F-G-N (CHANGED):** `seed_consensus_inputs` gains the additive BLUE field `SeedEpochConsensusInputs.epoch_nonce: Nonce` (the recovered Praos eta0 for `epoch_no`, used so the WarmStart forge VRF input is `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)`; T-REC-04 / DC-CINPUT-03) and its sole codec **bumps `SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION 1 → 2`** (the outer record is now 7 fields; a v1 sidecar that omitted `epoch_nonce` decodes as `UnknownVersion`, NEVER a default-to-zero eta0). The `consensus_view` projection threads the recovered eta0. No new TYPE — an additive field on the existing closed record under a bumped version gate. **N-F-G-Q (carried):** position rule + forge-successor unchanged here. **PHASE4-N-U (CHANGED — the lone BLUE touch this cluster):** `block_validity::header_input::block_header_bytes(block_cbor: &[u8]) -> Result<&[u8], BlockValidityError>` is factored out of the existing `accepted_block_header_bytes` (which now delegates `block_header_bytes(accepted.as_bytes())`) so the `--mode node` durable-chain serve projection can read `StoredBlock.bytes` directly — the SAME single DC-CONS-18 `header_cbor_slice` recipe, generalized from `&AcceptedBlock` to `&[u8]`. No new authority, no new logic, no new type, no parallel splitter — only the input signature is generalized. **PHASE4-N-AE (CHANGED — additive field, no new type):** `block_validity::header_input::DecodedBlock` gains the additive field `prev_hash: PrevHash` (owned by `ade_types`, consumed here), populated in `decode_block` from `hb.prev_hash` — the parent linkage ALREADY parsed for `check_header_position` — so the RED `--mode node` serve projection can prove a recovered/forged parent is the parent of a real servable successor (AE.B / `DC-NODE-14`). NO decode-logic / hashing / determinism change: `block_hash`, `computed_body_hash`, and the position rule are byte-identical; no new type, no new authority. **PHASE4-N-AI (CHANGED — the FIRST new BLUE canonical types since G-N):** `wal::event` gains the closed-sum variant `WalEntry::RollBack {to_point, reason, prior_tip, selected_tip}` at the reserved RollBackward **tag 1** (tag 2 `CaptureSnapshot` stays reserved; append-only — CN-WAL-01) — a DURABLE MARKER that a rollback to `to_point` occurred; it records, it does NOT decide or materialize a rollback. Two NEW payload types — `RollbackPoint {slot, hash, block_no}` (struct) + `RollbackReason {ForkChoiceWin | PeerRollBackward}` (closed enum, uint wire code, unknown code fails closed). `wal::replay` gains the matching arm: it re-anchors the fp chain to `to_point`'s EXISTING in-chain `post_fp` (fp-ONLY — no materialize in replay) and the recovery/materialize layer re-invokes the EXISTING `rollback::materialize_rolled_back_state` (CN-STORE-07) + lockstep `receive::commit_rollback` (DC-CONS-20) — **NOT a second rollback implementation** (DC-NODE-25/27). `wal::error` gains the closed `WalError::RollbackTargetNotInChain {entry_index, to_slot}` (a rollback whose target is not an active in-chain point fails closed on replay). |
| **Creates** | ~177 public types (byte-stable across the G-K…G-R span — the G-N change is a field + a const bump, not a new type). Load-bearing: `BlockValidityError` (incl. `HeaderPositionInvalid`), `BlockVerdict`, `TxValidity*`, `MempoolState`, `ProducerTick`, `ForgedBlock`, `ForgeError`, `AcceptedBlock` (field private to `producer::self_accept`), `ServedChainSnapshot`, `PoolDistrView`, `PoolEntry`, `LedgerState`, `ProtocolParameters`, `Rational`, `WalEntry` (closed sum: `AdmitBlock` + `SeedEpochConsensusInputsImported` at tag 3), `RecoveredBootstrapProvenance`, `ReplayOutcome`, `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` (closed; now carries `epoch_nonce: Nonce`; `SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION = 2`), `SeedConsensusInputsError` (closed), `BootstrapAnchor`, `SeedProvenance` (closed), `SeedPoint`, `ANCHOR_SCHEMA_VERSION = 2`, `MithrilManifestReport`, `BootstrapAnchorError`, `ConwayGenesisConfig`, `GenesisSourceError`, `UnsignedHeaderPreImage`, `PrevHash` is owned by `ade_types` (consumed here; **PHASE4-N-AE** adds it as the additive `DecodedBlock.prev_hash` field — a field on the existing `DecodedBlock`, not a new type). **PHASE4-N-AI** adds **2** new public types (177 → **179**): `WalEntry::RollBack` is a closed-sum VARIANT (not counted) but its payload types `RollbackPoint` (struct) + `RollbackReason` (closed enum) ARE new public types; `WalError::RollbackTargetNotInChain` is a variant on the existing closed `WalError` (not counted). |
| **Interprets** | Canonical decoded blocks/txs/certs/snapshots; `mempool_ingress` is the sole BLUE chokepoint; `self_accept` re-validates a forged artifact; `decode_bootstrap_anchor` reads the version-gated framing; `verify_mithril_binding` cross-checks the Mithril manifest; `genesis_initial_state` produces the cold-start pair; `unsigned_header_pre_image` produces the canonical CBOR of `ShelleyHeaderBody` (carrying `prev_hash: PrevHash`); `decode_block` calls `check_header_position` before the header authority. **N-F-G-N:** `decode_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` (the SOLE sidecar decoder) now reads the 7-field v2 record incl. `epoch_nonce`, and rejects a v1 record as `UnknownVersion`. **PHASE4-N-U:** `block_header_bytes(&[u8])` projects the header CBOR sub-slice of a raw canonical `[era, block]` envelope via the same `header_cbor_slice` walker `accepted_block_header_bytes` uses (the durable-chain serve projection consumes it over `StoredBlock.bytes`); `decode_block` is reused by that projection for `block_no` / `era` — no second decoder. **PHASE4-N-AI:** `decode_wal_entry` decodes the tag-1 `WalEntry::RollBack` payload (10-element array: 3×`RollbackPoint` + uint reason code), failing closed on an unknown reason code; `wal::replay::compute_superseded` (a pure pre-pass) marks the AdmitBlock entries a later RollBack supersedes and validates each rollback target is an active in-chain point — replay re-anchors via the EXISTING materialize/`commit_rollback` authority, it does not re-decide a rollback. |
| **MUST NOT** | All carry-forward ledger prohibitions (no I/O, no clock, closed cert/governance enums, single body-hash recipe). `producer::{forge, self_accept, served_chain}` fences (CN-FORGE-01/03, CN-PROD-04). `unsigned_header_pre_image` (CN-KES-HEADER-01). `block_validity::header_position` (CN-WIRE-09 position clause) — the SINGLE position-aware authority, called from `decode_block`, never in `ade_codec`, never duplicated. `bootstrap_anchor` / `genesis_source` / `wal` provenance fences. **`seed_consensus_inputs` (CN-CINPUT-01, strengthened by T-REC-04 / DC-CINPUT-03):** `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` stays a single closed canonical type with a SOLE encoder/decoder pair; deterministic CBOR, `BTreeMap`-ordered, **version-gated** (the `epoch_nonce` field is additive ONLY behind the `SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION 1 → 2` bump — a v1 sidecar MUST fail closed as `UnknownVersion`, never default eta0 to zero); no `Default`, no `#[non_exhaustive]`; no I/O / clock / float. **`consensus_view::from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` (DC-CINPUT-02a):** a pure BLUE field-map preserving single-epoch semantics (now carrying eta0); no I/O / clock / `HashMap`. **`block_validity::header_input` header projection (DC-CONS-18, PHASE4-N-U):** `block_header_bytes(&[u8])` and `accepted_block_header_bytes(&AcceptedBlock)` MUST remain the SINGLE header-projection authority sharing the one `header_cbor_slice` recipe — `accepted_block_header_bytes` MUST delegate to `block_header_bytes` (no copied walker); the RED durable-chain serve projection MUST call `block_header_bytes`, never re-walk the envelope or rebuild an `AcceptedBlock` (no parallel splitter in `ade_runtime`). **`wal::{event, replay}` rollback marker (DC-NODE-27 / CN-WAL-01 / CN-STORE-07 / DC-CONS-20, PHASE4-N-AI):** `WalEntry::RollBack` is a DURABLE MARKER — it MUST NOT implement a second rollback (replay re-invokes the EXISTING `materialize_rolled_back_state` + lockstep `commit_rollback`, NEVER a parallel rollback path); the replay re-anchor MUST use `to_point`'s EXISTING in-chain `post_fp` (the `prior_tip` / `selected_tip` / `reason` fields are audit/reconciliation ONLY — replay MUST NOT set the durable tip from `selected_tip`); the WAL stays append-only (the variant is additive at the reserved tag 1, tag 2 stays reserved — no tag reuse, no re-numbering); a rollback target not in the active chain MUST fail closed (`RollbackTargetNotInChain`), never silently re-anchor; `ci_check_wal_rollback_replay_equiv.sh`. |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_testkit`, `ade_core_interop`, `ade_runtime`, `ade_node`. |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_types`, `ade_crypto`, `ade_codec`, `ade_plutus`, `ade_core` (incl. `consensus::praos_state::Nonce`, used by the G-N `epoch_nonce` field), `minicbor`, `num-bigint`, `num-integer`, `num-traits`. Dev-dep: `ade_testkit`. |
| **Entry points** | `ade_ledger::block_validity::{decode_block, validate_block, check_header_position, block_header_bytes, accepted_block_header_bytes, unsigned_header_pre_image::unsigned_header_pre_image}`, `ade_ledger::tx_validity::*`, `ade_ledger::mempool::{ingress::mempool_ingress, admit::*}`, `ade_ledger::producer::{forge::forge_block, self_accept::{self_accept, AcceptedBlock}, served_chain::*}`, `ade_ledger::block_body_hash::*`, `ade_ledger::{receive, rollback, snapshot}::*`, `ade_ledger::pparams::ProtocolParameters`, `ade_ledger::rational::Rational`, `ade_ledger::wal::*`, `ade_ledger::seed_consensus_inputs::{SeedEpochConsensusInputs, encode_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs, decode_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs, SeedConsensusInputsError, SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION}`, `ade_ledger::consensus_view::{PoolDistrView, PoolEntry}` (incl. `from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`), `ade_ledger::bootstrap_anchor::*`, `ade_ledger::genesis_source::*`, `ade_ledger::wal::event::{WalEntry::RollBack, RollbackPoint, RollbackReason, TAG_ROLLBACK}`, `ade_ledger::wal::replay::compute_superseded` (PHASE4-N-AI). |
| **Key modules** | `block_validity/` (incl. `unsigned_header_pre_image.rs`, **`header_input.rs`** — PHASE4-N-U: `block_header_bytes(&[u8])` factored out of `accepted_block_header_bytes`; **PHASE4-N-AE: `DecodedBlock.prev_hash: PrevHash` additive field** (from the already-parsed header — no decode/hash/determinism change), `header_position.rs`, `verdict.rs`), `tx_validity/`, `mempool/`, `cert_classify/`, `consensus_view.rs` (G-N: threads recovered eta0), `producer/`, `block_body_hash.rs`, `receive/`, `rollback/`, `snapshot/`, `pparams.rs`, `rational.rs`, `wal/`, `seed_consensus_inputs.rs` (**G-N: `epoch_nonce` field + `SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION = 2`**), `bootstrap_anchor/`, `genesis_source.rs`, `wal/` (incl. **`event.rs`** — PHASE4-N-AI: the `WalEntry::RollBack` variant + `RollbackPoint`/`RollbackReason` payload types at tag 1; **`replay.rs`** — the rollback re-anchor arm + `compute_superseded` pre-pass; **`error.rs`** — `WalError::RollbackTargetNotInChain`; `mod.rs`/`store_trait.rs` accessor plumbing). |

> **GREEN sub-classification:** `ade_ledger::mempool::{policy, canonicalize}` are GREEN-by-content. **RED sub-classification:** `ade_ledger::consensus_input_extract` is RED-by-content. Both carry their own module banner.

### `ade_network` *(BLUE submodules)*

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | Owns the Cardano Ouroboros mini-protocol authority — the closed wire grammar (CBOR codecs) and pure state machines for all N2N + N2C mini-protocols, plus the BLUE mux frame primitive and the producer-side server-role reducers. Owns the per-protocol tag-24 composition authorities. **N-F-G-L (CHANGED, `handshake/`):** owns the single per-version N2N `versionData` wire encoding `handshake::version_table::encode_n2n_version_params(version, network_magic) -> VersionParams` (V11..=V15 emit the 4-field `[networkMagic, diffusionMode, peerSharing, query]`; V16+ the extended shape — the cardano-node-compatible NodeToNodeV_15 encoding, CN-WIRE-10, fixes the `TInt 1` handshake reject). **N-F-G-M (CHANGED, `chain_sync/` + `codec/`):** owns the scoped two-form ChainSync `FindIntersect` decode `codec::primitives::decode_array_head_two_form` over the NEW closed `ArrayHead = Definite(u64) \| Indefinite` (accepts the real cardano-node's indefinite-length points list), and the `chain_sync::server` `Origin → IntersectFound[Origin]` reply (the universal common ancestor; CN-WIRE-11). **PHASE4-N-AE (CHANGED, `chain_sync/server.rs` — existing-field write, no new type):** `producer_chain_sync_serve`'s `FindIntersect` handler now sets the server read cursor `last_announced` to the resolved intersect `Point` (`Block → Some((slot,hash))`, `Origin → None`), so after `IntersectFound(point)` the next `RequestNext` serves `next_after(point)` (the successor the client rolls onto), never `next_after(None)` (block 0) — fixing a non-Origin-intersect client being served the chain start and rejecting `UnexpectedBlockNo(tip_block_no + 1)(0)` (`DC-PROTO-10`; the CE-A5 relay-adoption closer). `ProducerChainSyncServerState` is unchanged (an existing field is written). |
| **Creates** | **110** BLUE canonical types: `mux/frame.rs` 5, `codec/` **39** (`38 → 39`: the NEW closed `ArrayHead = Definite(u64) \| Indefinite`, G-M / CN-WIRE-11), `handshake/` 9, `chain_sync/` 11, `block_fetch/` 10, `tx_submission/` 5, `keep_alive/` 5, `peer_sharing/` 5, `n2c/` 21. **N-F-G-L** added the additive BLUE **fn** `handshake::version_table::encode_n2n_version_params` + `VersionParams` is reused (no new type in `handshake/` — count holds at 9). **N-F-G-M** added the additive BLUE **fn** `codec::primitives::decode_array_head_two_form` alongside the NEW `ArrayHead` enum. Carried: the additive BLUE fn `handshake::version_table::n2n_supported_for_magic` (N-F-G-H). |
| **Interprets** | Mini-protocol wire frames; `mux::frame::decode_frame` is the single frame decode authority; per-protocol `*_transition` reducers consume decoded messages. `decompose_blockfetch_block` / `decompose_rollforward_header` strip the per-protocol tag-24 composition (delegating the inner unwrap to `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24`). **N-F-G-M:** `decode_find_intersect_points` (in `codec/chain_sync.rs`) decodes the `FindIntersect` points list via `decode_array_head_two_form` — accepting BOTH the definite (`9f…`) and indefinite forms (on `Indefinite` the caller consumes the `0xff` break); SCOPED to FindIntersect per CN-WIRE-11, not a general definite/indefinite decoder. |
| **MUST NOT** | (1) `mux::frame` — single `encode_frame`/`decode_frame` pair. (2) handshake — single `n2n_transition` + single `n2c_transition`. (3) closed `AcceptedMiniProtocol` registry. (4) no socket I/O in BLUE submodules. (5) no async/tokio in BLUE submodules. (6) depend on no workspace crate beyond `ade_codec` + `ade_types`. (7) server reducers MUST NOT split headers in parallel or depend on signing. (8) tag-24 composition (CN-WIRE-08) — composers delegate byte-level wrap/strip to the single `ade_codec` authority; pinned byte-identically against captured cardano-node 11.0.1 fixtures. **(8b) `n2n_supported_for_magic` (DC-NODE-07) — parameterizes ONLY `network_magic`; no version-set widening.** **(8c) `encode_n2n_version_params` (CN-WIRE-10, N-F-G-L) — the SINGLE per-version N2N `versionData` encoder; MUST emit the cardano-node-compatible per-version field shape (the 4-field V11..=15 / extended V16+), MUST NOT widen the closed `N2N_SUPPORTED` version SET or introduce runtime negotiation of meaning; pinned against the real-node handshake fixture (`ci_check_n2n_handshake_versiondata_authority.sh`).** **(8d) `decode_array_head_two_form` / `ArrayHead` + the `Origin` reply (CN-WIRE-11, N-F-G-M) — the indefinite-length acceptance is SCOPED to ChainSync `FindIntersect` (MUST NOT become a general definite/indefinite decoder for the rest of the closed grammar); the `Origin → IntersectFound[Origin]` reply matches the real cardano-node and MUST NOT widen the served chain beyond the Origin intersect; pinned against the real-node FindIntersect/IntersectFound fixtures (`ci_check_chainsync_findintersect_compat.sh`).** **(8e) `producer_chain_sync_serve` FindIntersect cursor (DC-PROTO-10, N-F-G/N-AE):** after answering `IntersectFound(point)`, the server read cursor `last_announced` MUST equal that point so the next `RequestNext` serves `next_after(point)` (the client's successor), NEVER `next_after(None)` (the chain start) — a non-Origin intersect that left the cursor unset (serving block 0 to a client whose read pointer is its own tip → `UnexpectedBlockNo(tip_block_no + 1)(0)`) is forbidden; an `Origin` intersect MUST keep the cursor `None` (serve from the chain start — correct). Test-enforced (`producer_chain_sync_serve_find_intersect_sets_cursor_then_rolls_forward_past_it`; `ci_script = ""`).** |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_runtime`, `ade_node`, `ade_core_interop`, `ade_testkit` (and the `ade_network` GREEN/RED submodules). |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_types`, `ade_codec`. No external deps in BLUE submodules. |
| **Entry points** | `ade_network::mux::frame::{encode_frame, decode_frame}`, `ade_network::handshake::{n2n_transition, n2c_transition}`, `ade_network::handshake::version_table::{N2N_SUPPORTED, n2n_supported_for_magic, encode_n2n_version_params}` (the last NEW, N-F-G-L), `ade_network::chain_sync::{server::*, client::*}` (server `Origin → IntersectFound` reply, N-F-G-M), `ade_network::block_fetch::{server::*, client::*}`, `ade_network::codec::{block_fetch::{compose,decompose}_blockfetch_block, chain_sync::{compose,decompose}_rollforward_header, primitives::{decode_array_head_two_form, ArrayHead}}` (the last NEW, N-F-G-M), `ade_network::{tx_submission, keep_alive, peer_sharing, n2c}::*`. |
| **Key modules** | `mux/frame.rs`, `codec/` (incl. `block_fetch.rs`, `chain_sync.rs`, **`primitives.rs`** — the N-F-G-M `ArrayHead` + `decode_array_head_two_form`), `handshake/` (incl. **`version_table.rs`** — the N-F-G-L `encode_n2n_version_params`), `chain_sync/` (incl. **`server.rs`** — the N-F-G-M Origin reply + the **PHASE4-N-AE** FindIntersect cursor `last_announced` set, DC-PROTO-10), `block_fetch/` (incl. `server.rs`), `tx_submission/`, `keep_alive/`, `peer_sharing/`, `n2c/`. |

## GREEN Modules — Deterministic Glue

> Deterministic, non-authoritative. May depend on BLUE; must not affect authoritative outputs. GREEN sub-trees inside the RED `ade_runtime` and `ade_node` crates carry a `//! GREEN …` banner + the same deny attributes and are CI-gated for purity. **PHASE4-N-AC touched NO GREEN module** (it is RED-only — the two changed files are the RED `ade_runtime::producer::producer_shell` + `ade_node::produce_mode`). **PHASE4-N-AB touched ONE GREEN module — `ade_network::session::core`** (the session reducer; `//! GREEN session driver`, PHASE4-N-L) — adding the outbound-segmentation path `handle_outbound` + the GREEN const `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES = 16 MiB` (`CN-SESS-05`; full entry immediately below). No new GREEN module was added in the prior G-K…G-R span; the touched GREEN sites there (`ade_runtime::{seed_consensus_merge, bootstrap}`) only thread the recovered `epoch_nonce` (eta0) through for G-N. The full per-module GREEN entries below are carried forward from the PHASE4-N-F-G-J inventory.

### `ade_network::session` *(GREEN by content — PHASE4-N-L; outbound segmentation N-AB)*

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | The deterministic GREEN session reducer for the Cardano Ouroboros mux — `step` is the SOLE pure fn reducing `(SessionState, ByteChunkIn) -> Result<(SessionState', Vec<SessionEffect>), SessionError>` (CN-SESS-03), composing the BLUE `mux::frame::{encode,decode}_frame` + `handshake::n2n_transition` + the closed `AcceptedMiniProtocol` registry + the per-mini-protocol frame demux/reassembly. It owns the type-state (`Handshaking` → `Connected`; DC-SESS-01) and the symmetric per-mini-protocol payload assembly across mux-frame boundaries: INBOUND it accumulates a per-protocol buffer and emits one `DeliverPeerFrame` per COMPLETE CBOR item (CN-SESS-04). **N-AB (NEW):** it now also owns the OUTBOUND inverse — `handle_outbound` SEGMENTS an outbound mini-protocol payload larger than `MAX_PAYLOAD` into ordered `<= MAX_PAYLOAD` mux frames (via the single-frame `encode_inner_frame` authority), and fails closed above the fixed ceiling `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES = 16 MiB` (CN-SESS-05). Nominally RED in `.idd-config.json` (placeholder before PHASE4-N-L) but GREEN-by-content — every file is pure / deterministic / no tokio / SystemTime / Instant / rand; the async tokio layer lives in `ade_runtime::network::{mux_pump, n2n_dialer}`. |
| **Creates** | `SessionState` (type-state: `Handshaking`/`Connected`), `ConnectedState` (incl. the closed-sum-indexed `proto_buffers` reassembly struct — no HashMap), `HandshakeProgress`, `SessionEffect` (closed: `SendBytes`/`DeliverPeerFrame`/`HandshakeComplete`), `SessionError` (closed — incl. `ReassemblyBufferOverflow` (N-F-G-E) + `OutboundPayloadTooLarge` (the N-AB fail-closed variant)), `AcceptedMiniProtocol` (the CLOSED mini-protocol registry — a closed semantic surface, GREEN, NOT canonical-counted), `ByteChunkIn`, `HandshakeRole`, `FrameBuffer` (demux). The NEW const `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES = 16 * 1024 * 1024` (16 MiB) — a **GREEN constant, NOT a BLUE canonical type** (the receive-side counterpart of `MAX_REASSEMBLY_TAIL_BYTES`). None of these is canonical-counted (GREEN). |
| **MUST NOT** | Affect authoritative outputs; introduce nondeterminism (no wall-clock / rand / float / HashMap — the per-protocol buffer is a closed-sum-indexed struct so iteration / membership / lookup are deterministic). **CN-SESS-03 (the single reducer):** `step` is the SOLE reduction entry — no parallel reducer. **CN-SESS-01/02 (composition):** frame encode/decode goes through the single BLUE `mux::frame::{encode,decode}_frame`; handshake through the single `n2n_transition` — no hand-rolled framing/handshake. **DC-SESS-01 (type-state):** a `Handshaking` session MUST NOT deliver any non-handshake (id≠0) mini-protocol frame to the orchestrator inbox. **CN-SESS-04 (inbound reassembly):** maintain one accumulating buffer per `AcceptedMiniProtocol` variant; emit exactly one `DeliverPeerFrame` per COMPLETE CBOR item (never per mux frame); same canonical inbound byte stream → byte-identical `DeliverPeerFrame` sequence. **CN-SESS-05 (outbound segmentation, N-AB):** an outbound payload larger than `MAX_PAYLOAD` MUST be SEGMENTED into ordered `<= MAX_PAYLOAD` mux frames via the single `encode_inner_frame` authority (the outbound inverse of CN-SESS-04) — MUST NOT truncate, drop, or reorder bytes (`concat(segment payloads) == payload`), MUST NOT change the mini-protocol id / mode across segments, MUST NOT read a per-segment clock (it reuses the ONE captured `timestamp` — a determinism break otherwise), MUST NOT introduce a second / parallel frame encoder (`encode_inner_frame` stays the single single-frame encoder with its own `MAX_PAYLOAD` guard), and MUST fail closed (`OutboundPayloadTooLarge`) on a payload above the FIXED, non-configurable `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES = 16 MiB` ceiling — no CLI/env/config escape, no unbounded outbound buffer. **N-F-G-E:** the inbound reassembly tail is bounded by `MAX_REASSEMBLY_TAIL_BYTES = 16 MiB` (`ReassemblyBufferOverflow`, drop the peer). |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_runtime::network::{mux_pump, n2n_dialer, n2n_listener}` (the RED tokio layer + serve listener), `ade_runtime::admission::wire_pump` (the live admission feed), `ade_node::wire_only` (the `--mode wire_only` driver), `ade_network::mux::transport` (the RED socket shell). |
| **Outbound deps** | BLUE `ade_network::{mux::frame, handshake}`; `ade_codec` (`cbor::skip_item` for the CN-SESS-04 complete-item drain, `error::CodecError`); `ade_types`. No tokio / external runtime deps (GREEN). |
| **Entry points** | `ade_network::session::{step, FrameBuffer, SessionState, ConnectedState, HandshakeProgress, SessionEffect, SessionError, AcceptedMiniProtocol, ByteChunkIn, HandshakeRole}`, `ade_network::session::handshake_driver::{run_n2n_handshake_initiator, run_n2n_handshake_responder}`. The N-AB outbound segmentation is internal to `session::core::handle_outbound` (reached via `step`); `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` + `encode_inner_frame` are module-private. |
| **Key modules** | `session/core.rs` (the `step` reducer + inbound `drain_protocol_items` reassembly + **N-AB `handle_outbound` outbound segmentation + `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES`**), `session/state.rs` (`SessionState` + `ConnectedState.proto_buffers`), `session/demux.rs` (`FrameBuffer`), `session/event.rs` (the closed `SessionEffect` / `SessionError` / `AcceptedMiniProtocol`), `session/handshake_driver.rs`. |

> **GREEN classification (load-bearing):** `ade_network::session` is **promotable to BLUE on demand, never demotable to RED** — it is pure and deterministic, the RED layer (sockets / tokio) is strictly separated into `ade_runtime::network`. The N-AB outbound-segmentation addition stays on the GREEN side of that line: it reorders/segments already-produced bytes into legal mux frames deterministically and decides no authority. `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES` is a GREEN const (NOT canonical-counted); `mux::frame` is reused unchanged (`CN-SESS-05` adds NO BLUE type).

### `ade_runtime::seed_consensus_merge` *(GREEN by content — PHASE4-N-F-A A2; eta0 threaded N-F-G-N)*

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | The deterministic, no-I/O merge transform lifting a verified-bootstrap `LiveConsensusInputsCanonical` plus the minted anchor fingerprint + seed epoch into the BLUE single-map `SeedEpochConsensusInputs`. `total_active_stake` is the saturating sum of every pool's `active_stake`. **N-F-G-N:** the merge now also carries the recovered Praos `epoch_nonce` (eta0) into the BLUE record's new `epoch_nonce` field (so the recovered consensus inputs carry eta0 EXPLICITLY; T-REC-04) — a pure field-pass, no new authority. |
| **Creates** | `SeedConsensusMergeError` (closed: `PoolMissingVrfKeyhash` / `PoolMissingStake`). Not canonical-counted (GREEN). |
| **MUST NOT** | Affect authoritative outputs. Introduce nondeterminism (`BTreeMap` only). Default-fill on a provenance gap (a pool present in one map but absent from the other MUST fail closed with `SeedConsensusMergeError`, never a zero-hash fill). **N-F-G-N:** MUST carry the recovered eta0 verbatim into `epoch_nonce` — never default it to zero (DC-CINPUT-03 forbids a zero-eta0 fallback; the BLUE codec's v1→v2 gate backs this). |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_runtime::{genesis_bootstrap, mithril_bootstrap}` (the two verified-bootstrap composers). |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_ledger::{consensus_view::PoolEntry, seed_consensus_inputs::SeedEpochConsensusInputs}`, `ade_runtime::consensus_inputs::LiveConsensusInputsCanonical`, `ade_core::consensus::praos_state::Nonce` (the eta0 type, N-F-G-N), `ade_types`. |
| **Entry points** | `ade_runtime::seed_consensus_merge::{merge_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs, SeedConsensusMergeError}`. |

### `ade_testkit` *(GREEN — deterministic test/corpus infrastructure; dev-dep / `#[cfg(test)]`-scoped)*

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | GREEN deterministic TEST / CORPUS infrastructure for the workspace — the oracle/differential harness, the validity & tx-validity corpora (incl. the Conway `ConwayValidityCorpus` loader), the consensus & governance replay corpora, the producer reference vectors, and the snapshot/genesis/ledger diff loaders. | **MUST NOT** | (1) **Be a production runtime dependency.** `ade_testkit` is GREEN dev-dep / `#[cfg(test)]`-scoped test infrastructure — it is an INBOUND `[dev-dependencies]` of the BLUE crates (`ade_core`, `ade_ledger`) and the RED crates (`ade_network`, `ade_runtime`, `ade_node`), and MUST NEVER appear in any production crate's plain `[dependencies]` (its sole plain-`[dependencies]` edge is the RED-leaf `ade_core_interop`, itself a non-shipping live-interop / test driver depended on by nothing — so `ade_testkit` is on NO production runtime path). It MUST NOT be promoted onto a hashed/persisted/consensus path: its corpora + fixtures + reference vectors are **evidence, never a production source** of any canonical value. (2) Affect authoritative outputs or introduce nondeterminism (deterministic, no wall-clock / rand / HashMap / float — the `// Core Contract:` banner). (4) Compare an Ade-internal-state fingerprint to a Haskell-serialized-state hash — comparisons are over observable / derived surfaces only (DC-COMPAT-01; enforced for the `consensus::genesis_pinning` sub-module). (5) Commit secret key material in any corpus/fixture dir (no `*.skey` / `*.vkey`). (6) Overstate semantic truth — a passing differential / corpus replay is evidence of agreement on the compared surface, never a blanket equivalence claim. |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_core` (dev), `ade_ledger` (dev), `ade_network` (dev), `ade_runtime` (dev), `ade_node` (dev), `ade_core_interop` (plain — the RED-leaf interop/test driver). All consume it as TEST infrastructure (dev-dep everywhere except the non-shipping RED leaf). |

Its `consensus::genesis_pinning` sub-module is the `#[cfg(test)]` genesis-consistency pinning harness (it reads the committed private-net reference fixture, drives the REAL `ade_runtime::bootstrap::bootstrap_initial_state` warm-start, and pins Ade's recovered eta0 / ASC / stake / VRF-keyhash / `praos_vrf_input` against the genesis-derived reference; the in-test sidecar pre-seed is confined to that `#[cfg(test)]` module so the CN-CINPUT-02 populate-side fence keeps production population on the verified-bootstrap path only). **This `### ade_testkit` section was RESTORED in this regeneration after being silently dropped at the `08b64ffc` catch-up (it last appeared at `dd3bf44f`); see the Generation notes.**
