## RED Modules — Imperative Shell

> I/O, network, storage, clocks, retries. May depend on BLUE/GREEN. Must not modify core state directly or construct semantic types unsafely.

### `ade_runtime`

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | The imperative shell — moves bytes, owns sockets/files/clocks/keys, drives tokio tasks. Hosts: producer-mode key custody + shell composition (`producer/` — incl. the GREEN `self_accepted_handoff`); the N2N network drivers (`network/` — incl. `mux_pump`, the N-F-G-H shared `serve_dispatch` core, and the `n2n_listener` with `Arc<[(u16, VersionData)]>` magic-aware tables); the node orchestrator runners; the receive/rollback/admission shells (incl. the `admission::{dial_for_admission, run_admission_wire_pump}` reused by the live `--mode node` feed); the seed-import/WAL/consensus-inputs importers; ChainDB + recovery shells; the N-Y bootstrap/forward-sync surfaces; the N-Z `mithril_bootstrap` composition; the clock seam; and (N-F-A) the seed-epoch consensus-input recovered-state shell. **N-F-G-O (CHANGED, `admission::wire_pump`):** the feed-side WirePump now strips the peer's BlockFetch `MsgBlock` tag-24 (`0xd8 0x18`) envelope via the single `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24` authority **before** the BLUE decode (so the live feed decodes the inner `[era, block]` cleanly — `UnexpectedType` gone; CN-WIRE-12). **N-F-G-N (CHANGED, `bootstrap` / `seed_consensus_merge` / `{genesis,mithril}_bootstrap`):** the verified-bootstrap composers + WarmStart now thread the recovered Praos `epoch_nonce` (eta0) — the merge carries it into the BLUE sidecar record (v2), the sidecar restore reads it back, and WarmStart overlays it onto `chain_dep.epoch_nonce` so the forge VRF input is `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)` (T-REC-04 / DC-CINPUT-03). **PHASE4-N-U (NEW + CHANGED, `network/`):** NEW RED module `network::served_chain_projection` — `ChainDbServedSource<'a>`, a read-only projection of the durable ChainDb into the BLUE serve seams (`ServedHeaderLookup` / `ServedRangeLookup`) over `iter_from_slot` / `get_block_by_hash` / `tip`; it serves `StoredBlock.bytes` verbatim, reuses the single `ade_ledger::block_validity::{block_header_bytes, decode_block}` authorities, and is the serve-as-projection that supersedes the G-R monotone serve gate (DC-NODE-13). CHANGED `network::serve_dispatch` — adds the closed read-source enum `ServedChainSource { Snapshot(&ServedChainView) | DurableChainDb(&dyn ChainDb) }`; the single `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound` (DC-NODE-07) now reads EITHER source (`--mode produce` passes `Snapshot`; `--mode node` passes `DurableChainDb`) — still exactly one dispatch authority. **PHASE4-N-AA (CHANGED, `chaindb` + `network::served_chain_projection`; RED-only):** the RED `ChainDb` trait gains TWO bounded hash-free serve-read primitives — `range_bytes_capped(from, to, max) -> Result<CappedSlotRange, ChainDbError>` (bounded, slot-ordered, reads at most `max + 1` blocks lazily, NO `SLOT_BY_HASH` scan, inverted-range `from > to` guarded empty) + `last_block_bytes() -> Result<Option<(SlotNo, Vec<u8>)>, ChainDbError>` (O(log N) tip, no hash scan) — implemented by BOTH `PersistentChainDb` (redb) + `InMemoryChainDb`; the NEW RED value type `CappedSlotRange { blocks, truncated }` lives in `chaindb/types.rs`; `iter_from_slot` / `tip` are doc-fenced full/TRUSTED-CALLER-only (recovery/rollback/startup, internals unchanged). `network::served_chain_projection::ChainDbServedSource` `range_bytes` / `next_after` / `tip` now read via those bounded primitives, cap each peer request at `const MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS = 256` (FIXED / non-configurable), use the NEW closed RED enum `ServeRangeOutcome { Served | Empty | CapExceeded | ReadError }` (every non-`Served` → empty `Vec` → reducer `NoBlocks`), derive each block's hash via the single BLUE `decode_block` (no second hash authority), and fail closed on oversized/inverted/undecodable ranges (DC-SERVEMEM-01 — the serve-side analog of DC-LIVEMEM-01; closes the N-U cross-slice security-review MEDIUM resource-amplification finding). **PHASE4-N-AC (CHANGED, `producer/producer_shell`; RED-only):** the RED producer key-custody shell `ProducerShell` gains the NEW `&mut self` method `kes_sign_header_advancing(period, preimage) = kes_advance_to(period)? then kes_sign_header(period, preimage)` — the signing shell now EVOLVES the operator KES key FORWARD to the requested KES period (via the existing deterministic Sum6KES `kes_advance_to -> kes_update`) BEFORE the single real KES sign, so a leader slot in KES period > 0 no longer fails `KesPeriodNotCurrent`; it fails closed `Signing(EvolutionBackwards)` on a backwards period (forward-secrecy) and `Signing(EvolutionExhausted)` beyond the key lifetime / `SUM6_MAX_PERIOD = 63`. The `period` is passed VERBATIM; signing stays RED; the BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + KES verifier are reused unchanged (DC-CRYPTO-10; strengthens CN-KES-HEADER-01). The `&self` `kes_sign_at` / `kes_sign_header` remain for callers that manage periods themselves. **PHASE4-N-AE (CHANGED, `network::served_chain_projection`; RED-only):** `ChainDbServedSource::intersect` gains a SECOND clause (after the durable-StoredBlock match) — a proof-gated, FindIntersect-ONLY projection of the forge PARENT: the new private helper `earliest_servable_block_prev_hash` reads exactly the EARLIEST servable StoredBlock (via the N-AA bounded `range_bytes_capped(SlotNo(0), SlotNo(u64::MAX), 1)`) and returns its `prev_hash` from the reused BLUE `decode_block` (now carrying `DecodedBlock.prev_hash`). When a FindIntersect point matches that parent hash, `intersect` returns it (slot taken verbatim — the parent is NOT a StoredBlock), so a relay holding the parent rolls forward onto the real servable successor (`next_after` returns it via the slot range). HARD BOUNDARY: NO bytes are EVER served for the projected point — `get_block_by_hash` / `serve_range` stay empty (BlockFetch refuses structurally); NO synthetic StoredBlock; recover-only (no StoredBlock) ⇒ NO projection (fail-closed); a `Genesis` earliest-parent ⇒ no projection (`DC-NODE-14`). The forge-on-followed-tip gate (in `ade_node`) gives this projection an intersectable parent. **PHASE4-N-AE.F (CHANGED, `forward_sync::pump`; RED-only):** `pump_block` gains a hash-exact already-have idempotency gate — immediately AFTER `decode_block` and BEFORE the BLUE chokepoint reducer (`forward_sync_step`), it queries `db.get_block_by_hash(&decoded.block_hash)` and, on `Some(stored)` with `stored.slot == decoded.header_input.slot`, returns `Ok(None)` (an idempotent no-op: no reducer step, no WAL append, no tip change — replay-equivalent). A DIFFERENT block (different hash) at/before the last-applied slot returns `None` here, falls through to the unchanged BLUE header authority, and fails closed (`SlotBeforeLastApplied` / `BlockNoOutOfOrder`). The skip is HASH-keyed (never slot alone), with no skip-past and no fork-choice (DC-CONS-03 untouched) — closing the post-CE-A5 echo (the relay re-announcing Ade's own adopted forged tip over the follow link; `DC-NODE-16`). **PHASE4-N-AH (CHANGED, `bootstrap`; RED-only, no BLUE/durable change):** `BootstrapState` gains the additive field `replayed_anchor_block_no: Option<u64>` — a DERIVED warm-start recovery SUMMARY (`recovered_tip.block_no − admit_count`, equivalently the recovery's `admit_count > 0` threshold), `None` on cold-start / first-run (only `warm_start_recovery` populates it). It is NOT an independently persisted chain point and NOT a new authoritative WAL/durable surface — it is an auditable recovery summary the GREEN `ade_node::node_sync::warm_start_forge_mode` reads to distinguish a bare-anchor recovery from a recovery with a replayed own-spine continuation (DC-NODE-22). No new type, no new authority, no new persistence. **PHASE4-N-AI (CHANGED, `admission::wire_pump`; RED-only):** the feed-side WirePump now PRESERVES the peer's chain-sync rollback as a closed event — `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward {peer, point, tip}` carries the rollback POINT (previously a `RollBackward` was discarded and surfaced only as a `TipUpdate`); a rollback is NEVER represented as a `TipUpdate` only. A concrete `Block` point flows through; an `Origin` point (rollback-to-genesis) fails closed `AdmissionWirePumpError::UnsupportedRollbackPoint` (drop the peer — unsupported for single-best-peer within k). The new variant is RED admission plumbing (the closed `AdmissionPeerEvent` emit-only surface — DC-PUMP-01, strengthened), NOT a semantic type, and never decides a rollback (that is the BLUE/durable apply path in `ade_node`). |
| **Creates (RED-only)** | `KesSecret`, `VrfSigningKey`, `ColdSigningKey` custody wrappers; `KeyLoadError`; `MuxTransportHandle` consumers; `OutboundCommand` (closed); `PerPeerOutbound`; `DispatchError` (closed 4-variant, in `network::serve_dispatch`); `ServerPeerStates`; the GREEN-by-content `ServedBlockEvidence`; `ServedChainHandle`; `GenesisAnchor`; `ProducerShell` (+ `ShellInitError`); `AdmissionPeerEvent`. Clock: `SystemClock`, `DeterministicClock`, closed `SlotAlignmentError`. consensus_inputs: `LiveConsensusInputsCanonical` (carries `protocol_params_json` OUTSIDE the 15-field fingerprint), closed `ProtocolParamsParseError`, `ForgeCurrentPParamsError`. N-Y/N-Z/N-F-A: `forward_sync::pump::*`, `mithril_import::*`, `recovery::restart::*`, `mithril_bootstrap::*`, `bootstrap::{SeedEpochConsensusSource (closed), BootstrapState, BootstrapInputs, BootstrapError}`, `genesis_bootstrap::*`. **PHASE4-N-U (NEW RED types):** `ChainDbServedSource<'a>` (borrowed `&dyn ChainDb` read-only serve projection, in `network::served_chain_projection`) + the closed read-source enum `ServedChainSource<'a> { Snapshot | DurableChainDb }` (in `network::serve_dispatch`). Both RED — serve plumbing, never semantic/canonical types. No new `WalEntry` variant, no new `NodeBlockSource` variant. **PHASE4-N-AA (NEW RED types/methods — serve plumbing, NOT canonical-counted):** the RED value type `CappedSlotRange { blocks: Vec<(SlotNo, Vec<u8>)>, truncated: bool }` (`chaindb::types`); the two RED `ChainDb` trait methods `range_bytes_capped` + `last_block_bytes` (`chaindb` — methods, not types); the closed RED enum `ServeRangeOutcome { Served(Vec<(SlotNo, Hash32, Vec<u8>)>) | Empty | CapExceeded | ReadError }` + the `const MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS: usize = 256` cap (`network::served_chain_projection`). All RED — bounded storage/serve plumbing, NOT semantic/canonical types; no new `WalEntry` / `NodeBlockSource` variant. The G-O change adds a call to the existing `unwrap_tag24` in `wire_pump`; the G-N change threads the existing `Nonce` through the composers. **PHASE4-N-AI (RED admission plumbing — NOT canonical-counted):** `admission::wire_pump::AdmissionPeerEvent` gains the closed variant `RollBackward {peer, point, tip}` + the closed `AdmissionWirePumpError::UnsupportedRollbackPoint`. RED — admission signals, not semantic/canonical types; no new `WalEntry` / `NodeBlockSource` variant. Never semantic/canonical types. |
| **Interprets** | Canonicalizes peer bytes/files for the BLUE core: the cold/VRF/KES loaders; `genesis_parser::parse_shelley_genesis`; `opcert_envelope::parse_opcert_envelope`; `seed_import`; `admission::{dial_for_admission, run_admission_wire_pump}` (the N2N dial + chain-sync/block-fetch pump producing `AdmissionPeerEvent`). **N-F-G-O:** `admission::wire_pump` strips the peer's BlockFetch payload tag-24 envelope via `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24` before handing the inner bytes to the BLUE decode path (the single tag-24 authority; no hand-rolled parse). **N-F-G-N:** `bootstrap::restore_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` reads the anchor-fp-keyed sidecar (now the 7-field v2 record incl. `epoch_nonce`) and verifies it fail-closed; a v1 sidecar is rejected `UnknownVersion`. |
| **MUST NOT** | (1) Modify BLUE state directly or construct semantic types from raw bytes. (2) Bypass canonical validation. (3) `producer::signing` (DC-CRYPTO-03/05) — RED-confined custody. **(3b) `producer::producer_shell::kes_sign_header_advancing` (DC-CRYPTO-10, PHASE4-N-AC):** the forge's single real KES sign MUST evolve the operator KES signing key to the requested period BEFORE signing, via the EXISTING deterministic Sum6KES update (`kes_advance_to(period) -> kes_update`), passing the period VERBATIM (no `period ± N`); it MUST fail closed if the requested period is BEFORE the key's current period (`EvolutionBackwards` — a destroyed past period cannot be re-signed) or BEYOND the key lifetime / unreachable by sequential evolution (`EvolutionExhausted`) — a structured error + NO signature, NEVER a key override; `kes_update` MUST retain BOTH guards; signing stays RED (`T-KEY-01` — the standing `ci_check_no_signing_in_blue.sh` is the BLUE fence); the BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + KES verifier + forge eligibility + wire rules MUST be reused UNCHANGED (NO re-implemented evolution, NO new BLUE authority/type). `ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh`. (4) `producer::keys` — no `KesSecret::from_*` inside `load_kes_signing_key_skey`. (5) `producer::coordinator` is GREEN and holds no secrets. (6) `network::outbound_command` (CN-OUTBOUND-RELAY-01) — `OutboundCommand` is the sole channel to MuxPump's encoder. (7) per-peer outbound map (CN-PEER-OUTBOUND-MAP-01 / DC-OUTBOUND-FIFO-01). (7b) `network::serve_dispatch` (DC-NODE-07) — single `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound`, coordinator-free, request-driven, read-only over the borrowed `ServedChainView`. (7c) `network::n2n_listener` magic-aware serve table (DC-NODE-07) — built via `n2n_supported_for_magic`, never the static `N2N_SUPPORTED`. **(7d) `network::served_chain_projection::ChainDbServedSource` (DC-NODE-13 / CN-CONS-07 serve clause / DC-CONS-17 / DC-CONS-18, PHASE4-N-U):** the durable-chain serve projection is READ-ONLY — it advances no tip, admits nothing, derives no verdict, and mutates no ChainDb; it serves `StoredBlock.bytes` VERBATIM (no re-encode — DC-CONS-17); it reuses the single `block_header_bytes` header-projection (DC-CONS-18) + `decode_block` — NO parallel splitter, NO envelope re-walk, NO `AcceptedBlock` reconstruction; on a `ChainDbError` a lookup yields `None`/empty (serve nothing this round — availability, never wrong/partial bytes). `ServedChainSource` is a read-source enum, NOT a second dispatch authority — there stays exactly one `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound` (DC-NODE-07; `ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh` + `ci_check_single_serve_dispatch_authority.sh`). **PHASE4-N-AE forge-parent projection (DC-NODE-14):** the FindIntersect-only forge-parent `intersect` clause MUST serve NO bytes for the projected point — `get_block_by_hash` / `serve_range` MUST stay empty (BlockFetch refuses structurally); it MUST NOT mint a synthetic StoredBlock or serve the recovered snapshot anchor as a chain head a peer cannot intersect; it MUST project ONLY the `prev_hash` of the EARLIEST servable StoredBlock via the single BLUE `decode_block` over the bounded `range_bytes_capped` read (NO second decode/hash authority, NO unbounded scan — DC-SERVEMEM-01 preserved); recover-only or a `Genesis` earliest-parent MUST yield NO projection (fail-closed); `ci_check_recovered_anchor_intersectable.sh`. **(7e) `network::served_chain_projection` + `chaindb` bounded serve read (DC-SERVEMEM-01, PHASE4-N-AA):** the peer-driven `--mode node` serve path MUST bound per-request work — it MUST read via the hash-free bounded `ChainDb` primitives `range_bytes_capped` / `last_block_bytes` and MUST NOT use the unbounded `iter_from_slot` (full-range materialize + per-block `SLOT_BY_HASH` scan, O(N²)) or the O(N) `chaindb.tip()` on the serve path; it MUST cap each request at the FIXED, non-configurable `MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS = 256` literal (no CLI/env/config escape, no unbounded mode); it MUST derive each served block's hash from the bytes via the single BLUE `decode_block` authority (NO second hash authority, NO `SLOT_BY_HASH` reference on the serve path); and it MUST fail closed on oversized (`CapExceeded`), out-of-chain / inverted-`from > to` (`Empty`), or undecodable in-range (`ReadError`) ranges — every non-`Served` `ServeRangeOutcome` maps to an empty `Vec` (reducer `NoBlocks`), never a panic, never wrong/partial bytes; the `range_bytes_capped` impls MUST guard an inverted range (incl. `from = u64::MAX`) as empty. The cap is a defensive implementation bound, NOT a Cardano semantic parameter. The trusted recovery/rollback `iter_from_slot` internals are OUT OF SCOPE (doc-fenced, not peer-driven). `ci_check_serve_range_bounded.sh`. (8) `network::n2n_server` — no signing dep. (9) `forward_sync::pump` (DC-SYNC-01) — refuse to advance the tip before `StoreBlockBytes` + `AppendWal` return Ok. **(9b) `forward_sync::pump::pump_block` receive idempotency (DC-NODE-16, PHASE4-N-AE.F):** the already-have skip MUST be HASH-keyed (`get_block_by_hash(&decoded.block_hash)`), never slot-only, and MUST be placed BEFORE the BLUE chokepoint reducer (`forward_sync_step`) so the no-op runs no reducer step and appends nothing to the WAL (replay-equivalent — T-REC-05 / DC-WAL-02 preserved); a DIFFERENT block (different hash) at/before the last-applied slot MUST NOT be short-circuited — it MUST reach the unchanged BLUE header authority and fail closed (`SlotBeforeLastApplied` / `BlockNoOutOfOrder`); the gate MUST confirm `stored.slot == decoded.header_input.slot` before the no-op; and it MUST NOT skip-past or invoke fork-choice (DC-CONS-03 untouched). NO BLUE change — the gate is a deterministic RED-chokepoint durable-store query, not a new reducer input. `ci_check_receive_idempotency.sh`. (10) `mithril_import` (CN-MITHRIL-01) — route initial state through the single `bootstrap_initial_state` authority. (11) `genesis_bootstrap` (CN-NODE-01 / CN-CINPUT-02) — route through the single authority; the composer WRITES the sidecar, never consumes one. (12) `recovery::restart` — fail fast on `WalTailFingerprintMismatch`. (13) `mithril_bootstrap` (DC-MITHRIL-02) — the anchor `seed_point` minted from `MithrilSeedPointInputs`, never the manifest; `verify_mithril_binding` fail-closed first. **(14) `bootstrap::restore_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` (DC-CINPUT-01; strengthened T-REC-04 / DC-CINPUT-03):** fail closed on a missing sidecar / hash mismatch / non-canonical decode / binding mismatch / non-byte-identical re-encode — and MUST NOT fall back to the forge-time bundle. **N-F-G-N: the recovered `epoch_nonce` (eta0) MUST be read from the v2 sidecar and overlaid onto `chain_dep.epoch_nonce` at WarmStart (the forge VRF input is `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)`); a v1 sidecar (no `epoch_nonce`) MUST fail closed as `UnknownVersion`, NEVER default eta0 to zero (`ci_check_warmstart_eta0_overlay.sh`).** (15) `seed_consensus_provenance` (CN-CINPUT-02) — hash the EXACT A1 bytes; referenced only at the two composition sites. (16) `chaindb` seed-sidecar surface (CN-CINPUT-02) — anchor-fp-keyed namespace disjoint from the slot-keyed snapshot space; redb `SCHEMA_VERSION = 3`. (17)–(18) `producer::keys`/`ProducerShell`/parsers (CN-NODE-03 / OP-OPS-04) + `admission::{dial,pump}` (the SOLE N2N dial + pump). **(18b) `admission::wire_pump` feed tag-24 unwrap (CN-WIRE-12, N-F-G-O):** the feed-side WirePump MUST strip the BlockFetch `MsgBlock` tag-24 envelope via `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24` BEFORE the BLUE decode; it MUST NOT hand the wrapped bytes to the decoder and MUST NOT add a parallel / hand-rolled tag-24 parse (the single `CN-WIRE-08` authority is reused; `ci_check_feed_tag24_unwrap.sh`).** (19) `clock::checked_millis_to_slot` (N-F-G-A) — fail closed before-anchor; no float/wall-clock. (20)–(21) `consensus_inputs::{protocol_params, canonical}` (N-F-G-A) — no float path; `protocol_params_json` OUTSIDE the 15-field fingerprint. **(22) `admission::wire_pump` rollback signal preservation (DC-PUMP-01, PHASE4-N-AI):** a chain-sync `RollBackward` MUST be surfaced as the closed `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward {peer, point, tip}` (the rollback POINT preserved) — it MUST NOT be discarded or downgraded to a `TipUpdate`-only; a `RollBackward(Origin)` MUST fail closed (`UnsupportedRollbackPoint`, drop the peer), never surfaced as a point; the `AdmissionPeerEvent` surface stays closed/emit-only (no `AgreementVerdict` reference); `ci_check_wire_rollback_signal_preserved.sh`. |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_node`, `ade_core_interop`, `ade_testkit` (dev/integration). |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_types`, `ade_core`, `ade_crypto`, `ade_codec` (incl. `unwrap_tag24`, now also called by `admission::wire_pump`, N-F-G-O), `ade_ledger`, `ade_network`, `redb`, `serde`, `serde_json`, `bech32`, `base58`, `cardano-crypto` (`["vrf-draft03", "dsign"]`), `ed25519-dalek`, `tokio`. |
| **Entry points** | `ade_runtime::producer::{producer_shell::* (incl. the PHASE4-N-AC `kes_sign_header_advancing` evolve-then-sign method), keys::*, coordinator::*, served_chain_handle::*, genesis_parser::parse_shelley_genesis, opcert_envelope::parse_opcert_envelope, self_accepted_handoff::SelfAcceptedHandoff}`, `ade_runtime::admission::{dial_for_admission, run_admission_wire_pump, AdmissionPeerEvent}` (the WirePump now tag-24-unwraps, N-F-G-O), `ade_runtime::network::{n2n_listener::*, n2n_dialer::*, mux_pump::*, n2n_server::*, outbound_command::OutboundCommand, serve_dispatch::{ServedChainSource, *}, served_chain_projection::ChainDbServedSource}` (the last two NEW, PHASE4-N-U), `ade_runtime::orchestrator::*`, `ade_runtime::bootstrap::{bootstrap_initial_state, BootstrapInputs, BootstrapState, SeedEpochConsensusSource, BootstrapError}` (WarmStart overlays the recovered eta0, N-F-G-N), `ade_runtime::seed_consensus_merge::{merge_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs, SeedConsensusMergeError}` (carries eta0, N-F-G-N), `ade_runtime::consensus_inputs::*`, `ade_runtime::{forward_sync, mithril_import, genesis_bootstrap, mithril_bootstrap, recovery::restart, chaindb, clock, seed_import, wal, bootstrap_anchor}::*` (incl. the PHASE4-N-AA `chaindb::ChainDb::{range_bytes_capped, last_block_bytes}` bounded serve primitives + `chaindb::types::CappedSlotRange`), `ade_runtime::network::served_chain_projection::{ChainDbServedSource, ServeRangeOutcome, MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS}` (the last two NEW, PHASE4-N-AA). |
| **Key modules** | `producer/` (incl. **`producer_shell.rs`** — PHASE4-N-AC: the `kes_sign_header_advancing` evolve-then-sign RED method), `network/` (incl. **`served_chain_projection.rs`** — PHASE4-N-U: the NEW RED durable-chain serve projection; **PHASE4-N-AE: the FindIntersect-only forge-parent `intersect` clause + the private helper `earliest_servable_block_prev_hash`** (DC-NODE-14, serves no bytes); `serve_dispatch.rs` — PHASE4-N-U: the closed `ServedChainSource` read-source enum; `n2n_listener.rs`), `orchestrator/`, `admission/` (incl. **`wire_pump.rs`** — the N-F-G-O feed-side tag-24 unwrap; `dial_for_admission` + `run_admission_wire_pump`), `receive/`, `rollback/`, `seed_import/`, `consensus_inputs/`, `wal/`, `chaindb/` (redb schema v3; **PHASE4-N-AA**: the bounded hash-free serve primitives `range_bytes_capped` + `last_block_bytes` in `mod.rs`/`contract.rs`, the `CappedSlotRange` value type in `types.rs`, impls in `persistent.rs` + `in_memory.rs`, `iter_from_slot`/`tip` doc-fenced trusted-only), **`forward_sync/`** (incl. **`pump.rs`** — PHASE4-N-AE.F: the `pump_block` hash-exact already-have idempotency gate, DC-NODE-16), `mithril_import/`, `seed_consensus_merge.rs` (GREEN; carries eta0, N-F-G-N), `seed_consensus_provenance.rs`, `mithril_bootstrap.rs`, `genesis_bootstrap.rs`, `recovery/`, `bootstrap.rs` (GREEN composition + RED A3b restore; WarmStart eta0 overlay, N-F-G-N), `bootstrap_anchor.rs`, `clock.rs`, `admission/` (incl. **`wire_pump.rs`** — PHASE4-N-AI: the `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward {peer, point, tip}` rollback-signal preservation + `UnsupportedRollbackPoint`, DC-PUMP-01). |

> **RED sub-entries carried verbatim from the PHASE4-N-F-G-J inventory** (unchanged in shape across the G-K…G-R span): `ade_runtime::network::serve_dispatch` *(RED — N-F-G-H; the single shared coordinator-free `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound` over the borrowed `ServedChainView`; closed 4-variant `DispatchError`; `ServerPeerStates`; GREEN-by-content `ServedBlockEvidence`; `ci_check_single_serve_dispatch_authority.sh`)*. The serve sibling that DRIVES this core gained the G-K lifetime-decouple in `ade_node::node_lifecycle` (below); the G-R monotone serve gate (`serve_gate_admits`) it carried is **RETIRED by PHASE4-N-U S3** (superseded by serve-as-projection). The shared `serve_dispatch` core stays the ONE dispatch authority — PHASE4-N-U adds only the `ServedChainSource` read-source enum it reads from. **NEW RED sub-entry — `ade_runtime::network::served_chain_projection`** *(RED — PHASE4-N-U S3 / DC-NODE-13)*: `ChainDbServedSource<'a>` wraps a borrowed `&dyn ChainDb` and implements both BLUE serve seams (`ServedHeaderLookup::{next_after, intersect, tip}` + `ServedRangeLookup::range_bytes`) as a deterministic read-only projection of the durable ChainDb (`iter_from_slot` slot-ascending; `get_block_by_hash` for `intersect`/`tip`; `stored.bytes` served verbatim; `block_header_bytes` + `decode_block` reused for the header projection + `block_no`/`era`). It supersedes the G-R in-memory `ServedChainSnapshot` accumulator + `serve_gate_admits`: the extend-only durable chain (DC-CONS-23) holds exactly one block 0 by construction, so a follower fetches coherent history A→B (never B without A) and serving survives restart (the accumulator did not). Read-only — advances no tip, admits nothing, mutates no ChainDb. `ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh`. **PHASE4-N-AA (CHANGED — DC-SERVEMEM-01, bounded peer-driven serve):** `range_bytes` / `next_after` / `tip` now read via the S1 bounded hash-free `ChainDb` primitives `range_bytes_capped` / `last_block_bytes` (NEVER the unbounded `iter_from_slot` / O(N) `tip()` — those are doc-fenced trusted-only); each peer request is capped at the FIXED non-configurable `const MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS = 256`; the NEW closed RED enum `ServeRangeOutcome { Served(Vec<(SlotNo, Hash32, Vec<u8>)>) | Empty | CapExceeded | ReadError }` distinguishes the four internal reasons (every non-`Served` → empty `Vec` → reducer wire `NoBlocks`); each block's hash is derived from its bytes via the single BLUE `decode_block` (no `SLOT_BY_HASH` index, no second hash authority); and the serve fails closed on an oversized (`CapExceeded`, decided BY THE BOUND before any decode), out-of-chain / inverted (`Empty`), or undecodable (`ReadError`) range — never a panic, never wrong/partial bytes. It is the serve-side analog of `DC-LIVEMEM-01` and closes the N-U cross-slice security-review MEDIUM resource-amplification finding. `ci_check_serve_range_bounded.sh`. **PHASE4-N-AE (CHANGED — DC-NODE-14, recovered/forge-parent intersectability):** `intersect` gains a SECOND, FindIntersect-ONLY, proof-gated clause after the durable-StoredBlock match — the new private helper `earliest_servable_block_prev_hash` reads exactly the earliest servable StoredBlock (via the bounded `range_bytes_capped(0, u64::MAX, 1)`) and returns its `prev_hash` (reusing the single BLUE `decode_block` + the new `DecodedBlock.prev_hash`); a FindIntersect point that byte-equals that parent hash is returned (slot verbatim) so a relay holding the parent rolls forward onto the real successor. NO bytes are ever served for the projected point (`get_block_by_hash` / `serve_range` stay empty — BlockFetch refuses structurally); recover-only (no StoredBlock) or a `Genesis` earliest-parent ⇒ NO projection (fail-closed — never a synthetic StoredBlock, never the recovered anchor served as an un-intersectable head). Read-only — advances no tip, admits nothing. `ci_check_recovered_anchor_intersectable.sh`.

---
### `ade_node`

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | The node binary + library entry. Owns argv parsing, the node lifecycle, and the mode drivers dispatched by `main()`: `--mode wire_only` (default), `--mode admission`, `--mode key_gen_kes`, `--mode produce`, and (N-F-C) `--mode node` (`node_lifecycle`). `node_lifecycle` is the single `PHASE4-N-F-C-LIFECYCLE-OWNER`. Carries the full N-F-C…N-F-G-J `--mode node` live surface (bootstrap/recovery, forge-intent flip, real forge constants + the two fail-closed boundaries, the self-accept→serve handoff, the live WirePump feed, the bounded-memory caps, the rehearsal harness, the serve-to-peer sibling, and the genesis-successor cold-start forge). **G-K…G-R catch-up span (`--mode node` live serve/feed/forge wiring, all RED, no BLUE change):** **N-F-G-K** decouples the serve-listener lifetime from feed end — the serve sibling (`run_node_serve_task`, spawned OUTSIDE `run_relay_loop`) stays up serving past feed-end so a follower keeps fetching (DC-NODE-09). **N-F-G-P** sources the feed-side header-validation view (leader-threshold stake distribution + header-validation inputs for Steps 5 + 7) from the recovered consensus surface (`from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`), so a valid live block 0 is ingested (`VerificationFailed` gone; DC-CINPUT-04). **N-F-G-Q** derives the forge-SUCCESSOR position `(last_admitted_block_no + 1, PrevHash::Block(last_admitted_hash))` from the evolved admitted spine state (not the stale recovered tip) — the first stable node, block 1+, no successor crash (DC-NODE-10). **N-F-G-R** adds a monotone serve gate so the served tip never regresses once block 0 is served — a genesis-successor follower adopts a stable served block 0 (DC-NODE-11). The G-O feed tag-24 unwrap lands in `ade_runtime::admission::wire_pump` (above); `node_sync` carries the one-line consumer change. The G-L/G-M serve-side handshake/FindIntersect fixes land in the BLUE `ade_network` submodules (above) and are exercised by `ade_node` serve-loopback + real-node fixture tests. **PHASE4-N-U (forged-block durability, all RED, no BLUE authority change):** **S1 (DC-NODE-12 + DC-CONS-23 + DC-WAL-04 chaining)** adds the NEW fenced RED driver `node_sync::admit_forged_block_durably` — the ForgeTick arm feeds the self-accepted `accepted.into_bytes()` (no re-encode) into the SAME `forward_sync::pump_block` chokepoint received blocks use (extend-only admit → StoreBlockBytes → AppendWal → AdvanceTip), so the forge's own block becomes durable and the next forge builds N+1 on the durable tip; a stale-tip forge fails closed. **S2 (T-REC-05 + DC-WAL-04 no-orphan)** wires WAL-tail reconciliation + forward-replay into production `node_lifecycle::warm_start_recovery` (reusing the BLUE `bootstrap_initial_state` forward-replay), so a forged-block durable tip recovers byte-identically + a torn forge-admit orphan is dropped + a recovered-fp ≠ WAL-tail-`post_fp` is a fail-fast (`WarmStartWalTailFingerprintMismatch`). **S3 (DC-NODE-13)** makes the `--mode node` served view a deterministic READ-ONLY projection of the durable ChainDb: `chaindb` becomes `Arc<PersistentChainDb>` (redb MVCC reads — safe concurrent with the relay loop's writes), `run_node_serve_task` takes `Arc<dyn ChainDb>` and dispatches with `ServedChainSource::DurableChainDb` over a `ChainDbServedSource`, and the G-R node-path push sibling (`handoff_tx`/`handoff_rx`, the ForgeTick `tx.send` serve forward, `serve_gate_admits` + its in-module test) is **RETIRED**. The forge still advances no tip DIRECTLY (`pump_block` is the sole durable tip authority — DC-NODE-05 preserved + extended to forged blocks via DC-NODE-12). **PHASE4-N-AC (CHANGED, `produce_mode`; RED-only, no BLUE change):** the forge's single real KES sign (`produce_mode::run_real_forge_inner` step 3) now calls `shell.kes_sign_header_advancing(kes_period, &preimage)` instead of the raw `shell.kes_sign_header(...)`, so the RED signing shell evolves the minted-at-period-0 operator KES key forward to the chain's current KES period before signing — a leader slot in KES period > 0 no longer fails `KesPeriodNotCurrent`; on `Err(_)` it still returns the closed `CoordinatorEvent::ForgeFailed` (DC-CRYPTO-10). **PHASE4-N-AE (forge-on-followed-tip admissibility + recover→follow continuity, all RED, no BLUE authority change):** **AE.A (DC-NODE-15 + DC-CONS-24)** `node_sync` adds the GREEN-by-function classifier `forge_followed_tip_admission(durable_servable_tip, followed_peer_tip) -> ForgeFollowedTipAdmission` (closed `CaughtUp` | `NotCaughtUp(NotCaughtUpReason)`; pure / total / deterministic), the RED `FollowedPeerTipSignal` (observes the wire `TipUpdate`; an ADMISSIBILITY input only — never reaches `select_best_chain` / `chain_selector` / `fork_choice`), the typed `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp { local_servable_tip, followed_peer_tip, reason }` + `NodeForgeOutcome`; `node_lifecycle::run_relay_loop_with_sched`'s ForgeTick arm REMOVES the recovered-anchor forge-base fallback, calls the gate before the single fenced `forge_one_from_recovered`, and records a typed `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp` into `ForgeActivation.last_forge_refused` (no forge, no state transition, tip unchanged — distinct from a forge `Failed`); a `CaughtUp` forge sets `prev_hash = PrevHash::Block(selected_tip.hash)` with `block_no + 1` (DC-CONS-24). **AE.C (DC-WAL-02 + T-REC-05)** the first followed `AdmitBlock` seeds its WAL `prior_fp` from the recovered post-state fingerprint (recover→follow continuity — no orphan / fp break). The AE.B serve-side forge-parent projection lands in `ade_runtime::network::served_chain_projection` (above); `node_sync`/`node_lifecycle` supply the intersectable forged parent via the forge-on-followed-tip gate. **PHASE4-N-AF (single-producer extend-own-durable-spine — GREEN/RED, no BLUE authority change; SUPERSEDED by N-AH):** `node_sync` added the mode-aware `ForgeTick` gate (the `ForgeMode` enum + the GREEN transition fn, no booleans) letting a DECLARED single-producer venue forge on Ade's OWN durable spine WITHOUT a relay echo after an explicit RED venue-adoption certificate matched by CHAIN-POINT IDENTITY (hash + block_no), fail-closed `ForgeRefused::SingleProducerFenceViolation`; the cert was admissibility-only (never persisted; `DC-NODE-18`). The default `VenueRole::Unknown` path is the VERBATIM prior DC-NODE-15 gate. **PHASE4-N-AG (single-producer loop-continuation-after-feed-EOF — GREEN/RED, no BLUE change; DC-NODE-19, declared):** `run_loop_planner::plan_loop_step` gains the GREEN 5th `VenuePolicy` input (the 32-case total table; the `node_sync::venue_policy` projection), and `node_lifecycle`'s loop continues forging the certified own spine past a structural feed EOF (fenced to the certified single-producer run; fail-closed on the 7 conditions; only a CLEAN EOF is continued, a fatal source failure `Err`s; the same termination-authority move DC-NODE-09 made for the serve listener); `pump_block` stays the sole durable tip-advance authority + feed work still drains via `SyncOnce` before any `ForgeTick`. **PHASE4-N-AH (local selected durable chain forge-base authority — GREEN/RED, no BLUE change; DC-NODE-20/21/22, enforced):** **S1 (DC-NODE-20)** `node_sync::forge_mode_after_admit` enters `SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine{current_tip = own}` DIRECTLY on a real self-admit from `CaughtUpToPeerTip` (the `FirstOwnBlockServed` cert-wait intermediate is FOLDED OUT — `ForgeMode` is now 3-state), and `single_producer_forge_decision` derives the forge base from the local durable spine head (`ChainDb::tip`) under a 6-condition fence (`VenueRole::SingleProducer`; an OBSERVED-FEED competing-block fence — NOT fork-choice; relay non-producing; admitted via `pump_block`; spine contiguous/servable; no fork-choice required), failing closed (`ForgeRefused::SingleProducerFenceViolation`); `node_lifecycle` replaces the post-self-admit `durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip` re-check with the local-tip authority. `forge_followed_tip_admission` REMAINS the DC-NODE-15 INITIAL catch-up gate (the gate is phase-split, not removed — verified via `run_relay_loop_with_sched -> dc_node_15_refusal -> forge_followed_tip_admission`). **S2 (DC-NODE-21)** the `VenueAdoptionCertificate` type + the `read_adoption_cert` / `parse_hex32` parsers + the `--adoption-cert-path` CLI flag are FULLY DELETED from `ade_node` — the cert is rung-1 RED operator EVIDENCE parsed by the harness OUTSIDE the node, never a forge-base input. **S4b (DC-NODE-22)** the NEW GREEN `node_sync::warm_start_forge_mode(venue_role, recovered_tip, replayed_anchor_block_no)` re-enters the extend state on the recovered own-spine `ChainDb::tip` (when the recovered tip is ABOVE the replay anchor — recovery replayed ≥ 1 own block) WITHOUT a fresh followed-peer catch-up, fail-closed to `InitialCatchupRequired` otherwise; `node_lifecycle`'s warm-start arm calls it (the `replayed_anchor_block_no` summary comes from `ade_runtime::bootstrap::BootstrapState`). The DC-NODE-20 forge-base evidence is emitted via the closed `live_log::sched_event::NodeSchedEvent::ForgeBaseSelected` (S4a, CN-NODE-04). `single_producer_forge_decision` / `venue_policy` / `warm_start_forge_mode` / `forge_followed_tip_admission` are GREEN-by-function pure classifiers inside the RED crate. **DC-CONS-03 untouched.** **NO RO-LIVE flip** (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated — the run-4 cert-free local-tip forge a real Haskell relay adopted, sustained > k across a follow-link EOF + a restart, is the C2-LOCAL rung-1 mechanism, not operator-witnessed bounty acceptance). **PHASE4-N-AI (live fork-choice rollback-follow wiring — single-best-peer FOLLOW, NOT full ChainSel; RED/GREEN, +2 BLUE types live in `ade_ledger`, not here):** **AI-S2 (DC-NODE-23/24)** `node_sync` adds the GREEN-by-function `classify_receive(durable_tip, candidate: CandidateSummary) -> ReceiveClass {AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | Competing}` venue-blind detector (pure / total; an already-known peer echo is `AlreadyHave`, never competing merely because it is not a fresh extension) + `resolve_disposition(class, venue) -> ReceiveDisposition {AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | NeedsForkChoice | RefuseSingleProducer}` venue-split resolver (Participant ⇒ `NeedsForkChoice`; SingleProducer/Unknown ⇒ `RefuseSingleProducer` — the DC-NODE-20 fail-closed, byte-unchanged); the live feed now carries rollbacks as the ordered `NodeSyncItem {Block | RollBack(Point)}`, and `NodeSyncError` is extended to `{Pump | Capture | UnexpectedRollback | RollbackPointSlotMismatch}` (`run_node_sync`, the SingleProducer path, returns `UnexpectedRollback` on ANY `NodeSyncItem::RollBack` — it never adopts a peer rollback). **AI-S3 (DC-NODE-25/26)** `node_lifecycle::apply_chain_event` is the RED apply driver — a `ChainEvent::RolledBack` arm calls the EXISTING `materialize_rolled_back_state` (CN-STORE-07) → lockstep `commit_rollback` (DC-CONS-20) → an append-only `WalEntry::RollBack` MARKER, then reconciles the orchestrator tip to the durable `ChainDb::tip`; a roll-forward win is durably adopted ONLY when its BODIES validate+apply through `pump_block` (no header-only tip advance); new RED `AppliedTip` / `ApplyError`. **AI-S4a (DC-PUMP-01)** consumes the preserved `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward` point (the wire-pump change lands in `ade_runtime`). **AI-S4b (DC-NODE-28)** `node_lifecycle::declare_participant_venue` + `run_participant_sync` route the live Participant rollback-follow; `ForgeActivation.pending_reselection` + the ForgeTick gate (`pending_reselection_forge_refusal` → typed `ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending`) DISABLE forging while a fork-choice re-selection is unresolved (the forge never builds on a stale pre-resolution local tip). **AI-S6 (DC-NODE-29)** `run_participant_sync`'s RollBack arm binds the rollback target to the durable ChainDb's stored slot for the hash — the peer-supplied slot MUST equal the stored slot, else fail closed with a typed error BEFORE `commit_rollback`, BEFORE `WalEntry::RollBack`, BEFORE any ChainDb / LedgerState / PraosChainDepState mutation (closes the H-1 Byzantine-peer truncation finding). `classify_receive` / `resolve_disposition` / `pending_reselection_forge_refusal` / `durable_tip_matches` are GREEN-by-function pure classifiers inside the RED crate. **DC-CONS-03 stays the sole selector — the rollback-follow ROUTES a Participant candidate through the UNCHANGED `chain_selector` → `select_best_chain`, adds no second selector, maintains no multi-peer candidate set, and `CN-CONS-03` stays partial. NO RO-LIVE flip** (`RO-LIVE-01` operator-gated; CE-AI-6 is operator-pass convergence evidence, vacuous-until-committed). |
| **Creates (RED-only)** | `Cli` (incl. `peer_addrs`, `network_magic`), `CliError`, `ProduceCli`, `KeyGenKesCli`, `Mode` (closed: `WireOnly`/`Admission`/`KeyGenKes`/`Produce`/`Node`), `NodeStartupInputs`, `NodeShutdownEvidence`, `NodeRunError`, exit-code constants; the `produce_mode` slot-loop + admission-runner types. `node_lifecycle` (RED): `NodeStart` (closed), `NodeLifecycleError` (closed), `ForgeActivation<'a>`, `run_relay_loop` / `run_relay_loop_with_sched`, `spawn_live_wire_pump_source`, `run_node_serve_task`, `bind_serve_listener`, closed `ServeStartError`, the GREEN-by-function `may_cold_start_forge`. `node_sync` (RED): closed 2-variant `NodeBlockSource { WirePump, InMemory }`, `NodeSyncError`, `NodeForgeError` (incl. `RecoveredTipMissingBlockNo`), the GREEN-by-function `forge_epoch_admission` / `forge_header_position`, the `MAX_WIRE_PUMP_LOOKAHEAD = 256` cap. GREEN sub-trees `forge_intent` / `run_loop_planner` / `live_log::{sched_event,sched_writer}` / `ba02_evidence` / `rehearsal_evidence` (entries above). RED `operator_forge` / `ba02_pass` / `rehearsal_pass`. **PHASE4-N-U (RED):** NEW fenced driver `node_sync::admit_forged_block_durably` (generic `D: ChainDb`; feeds `handoff.accepted().as_bytes()` → `pump_block`); NEW `node_lifecycle` warm-start fail-fast `WarmStartWalTailFingerprintMismatch`; `chaindb` is now `Arc<PersistentChainDb>` and `run_node_serve_task` takes `Arc<dyn ChainDb>`. **RETIRED:** the G-R `serve_gate_admits` monotone-serve predicate + its in-module test, and the node-path serve push sibling (`handoff_tx`/`handoff_rx`, `serve_handle`/`serve_view`). NO new `WalEntry` variant, NO new `NodeBlockSource` variant (forged provenance is not conflated with received). **PHASE4-N-AE (RED node plumbing, NOT canonical-counted):** in `node_sync` — the RED `FollowedPeerTipSignal` (forge-admissibility signal), the closed `ForgeFollowedTipAdmission { CaughtUp | NotCaughtUp(NotCaughtUpReason) }`, the closed `NotCaughtUpReason`, the typed `ForgeRefused { NotCaughtUp { local_servable_tip, followed_peer_tip, reason } }`, `NodeForgeOutcome`, and the GREEN-by-function classifier `forge_followed_tip_admission`; in `node_lifecycle` — the `ForgeActivation.last_forge_refused` field. All RED — admissibility / refusal plumbing, NOT semantic/canonical types; NO new `WalEntry` / `NodeBlockSource` variant. **PHASE4-N-AI (RED/GREEN node plumbing, NOT canonical-counted):** in `node_sync` — the closed `NodeSyncItem {Block | RollBack(Point)}`, the closed `CandidateSummary`, the closed `ReceiveClass {AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | Competing}` + `ReceiveDisposition {AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | NeedsForkChoice | RefuseSingleProducer}`, the extended `NodeSyncError {Pump | Capture | UnexpectedRollback | RollbackPointSlotMismatch}`, the new `ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending` variant, the GREEN-by-function `classify_receive` / `resolve_disposition` / `pending_reselection_forge_refusal` / `durable_tip_matches`; in `node_lifecycle` — the RED apply-driver types `AppliedTip` / `ApplyError`, the `ForgeActivation.pending_reselection` field, `apply_chain_event` / `run_participant_sync` / `declare_participant_venue`. All RED/GREEN — detector / resolver / apply / refusal plumbing, NOT semantic/canonical types; NO new `WalEntry` / `NodeBlockSource` variant (the BLUE `WalEntry::RollBack` lives in `ade_ledger`). Never semantic/canonical types. |
| **Interprets** | argv (closed mode set); operator key/genesis/opcert file paths (delegated to `ade_runtime` parsers + `operator_forge`); evidence-manifest TOML schema; the admission runner interprets a peer's tag-24-wrapped BlockFetch `MsgBlock` via `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24`. **N-F-G-P:** the feed's header-validation interprets the recovered consensus surface's leader-threshold view (Steps 5 + 7). **N-F-G-Q:** the successor forge interprets the evolved admitted spine state to derive its `(block_number, prev_hash)`. **PHASE4-N-U:** `admit_forged_block_durably` interprets a `SelfAcceptedHandoff` (the BLUE self-accepted `AcceptedBlock` bytes) into the durable admit; `warm_start_recovery` interprets the recovered seed-epoch sidecar (`ChainDb::get_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` → `decode_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`) to reconstruct the recovery `era_schedule` + `ledger_view`; the `--mode node` served view reads (does not re-decode beyond `block_header_bytes`/`decode_block`) the durable ChainDb via `ChainDbServedSource`. **PHASE4-N-AI:** the live Participant receive path interprets each peer item as a `NodeSyncItem` (a `RollForward` header / block → `Block`, a `RollBackward(point)` → an ordered `RollBack(Point)`), classifies it via `classify_receive` over the durable tip, and on a Participant `NeedsForkChoice` routes the VALIDATED header summary (post `validate_and_apply_header`) into the EXISTING `chain_selector` orchestrator; `run_participant_sync` interprets a `RollBackward` against the durable `ChainDb` (`get_block_by_hash` → the stored slot+hash is the SOLE rollback-target authority, DC-NODE-29). |
| **MUST NOT** | All carry-forward `--mode node` prohibitions (closed mode set, single lifecycle owner via `bootstrap_initial_state`, durable-tip ONLY via `run_node_sync → pump_block`, `run_relay_loop` containment byte-unchanged, content-blind planner, the self-accept→serve handoff fence, the live-feed reuse + lookahead bound, the path-fidelity + rehearsal-evidence fences, the serve-to-peer DC-NODE-07 fence, the genesis-successor cold-start + PrevHash position fence). **`run_node_serve_task` lifetime (DC-NODE-09, N-F-G-K — PRESERVED):** the serve sibling is spawned OUTSIDE `run_relay_loop` and its lifetime is **independent of the feed source's end** (it MUST stay up serving past feed-end; `ci_check_node_serve_lifetime.sh`); it makes no peer-acceptance claim (`RO-LIVE-01` partial). **(DC-NODE-11 monotone-serve-gate clause, N-F-G-R — SUPERSEDED by PHASE4-N-U S3):** the `serve_gate_admits` monotone gate over an in-memory accumulator is RETIRED — its stability invariant (a follower sees a stable, coherent block 0) is now provided more strongly by serve-as-projection of the extend-only durable chain (which holds exactly one block 0 by DC-CONS-23); `ci_check_served_chain_stability.sh` is replaced by `ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh`. **(NEW) feed header-validation view (DC-CINPUT-04, N-F-G-P):** the feed's header-step + ledger Step-5/7 validation MUST derive its leader-threshold stake-distribution view from the recovered consensus surface (`from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`), never a defaulted / empty distribution (`ci_check_feed_leader_threshold_view.sh`); the verdict stays BLUE. **(NEW) forge-successor position (DC-NODE-10, N-F-G-Q):** the successor forge MUST derive `(block_number, prev_hash)` from the evolved admitted spine state `(last_admitted_block_no + 1, PrevHash::Block(last_admitted_hash))`, never the stale recovered tip; it reuses the single `forge_header_position` convention, and flips no RO-LIVE rule (`ci_check_forge_successor_evolved_spine.sh`). **(NEW) own-forged durable admit (DC-NODE-12 + DC-CONS-23 + DC-WAL-04, PHASE4-N-U S1):** the ForgeTick-arm forged block MUST reach the durable tip ONLY via the fenced `admit_forged_block_durably` driver → `forward_sync::pump_block` (durable-before-tip) — NO forge-specific `put_block` / `AdvanceTip` / `rollback`, NO second durable tip-advance path, NO new `NodeBlockSource` / `WalEntry` variant; the driver MUST feed `accepted.into_bytes()` VERBATIM (no re-encode — I-10); the durable admit MUST stay extend-only — a stale-tip forge MUST fail closed (header-position/`prev_hash` or `TipBeforeDurable` or WAL `prior_fp` mismatch), NEVER an own-block override, and `select_best_chain` / `fork_choice` MUST NOT appear on the driver / `receive` / `forward_sync` path (DC-CONS-03 stays the follow/`chain_selector` authority); the driver MUST be a sibling fn (not inlined in `run_relay_loop` / `run_node_sync` bodies — the containment gate fences those bodies, its allow-list extended only for the one driver call); `ci_check_forged_durable_admit_via_pump.sh` + `ci_check_node_run_loop_containment.sh`. **(NEW) forged-tip recovery (T-REC-05 + DC-WAL-04 no-orphan, PHASE4-N-U S2):** `warm_start_recovery` MUST recover a forged-block durable tip byte-identically (reusing the BLUE `bootstrap_initial_state` forward-replay — NOT a re-implemented forward-replay), MUST drop an un-WAL'd forged orphan via WAL-tail `rollback_to_slot` reconciliation, and MUST fail fast (`WarmStartWalTailFingerprintMismatch`) when the recovered fp ≠ WAL-tail `post_fp` — NEVER silently diverge (test-enforced; `T-REC-05.ci_script = ""`). **(NEW) serve-as-projection (DC-NODE-13 / CN-CONS-07 serve clause, PHASE4-N-U S3):** the `--mode node` served view MUST be a deterministic READ-ONLY projection of the durable ChainDb (`ServedChainSource::DurableChainDb` / `ChainDbServedSource`), NOT an in-memory accumulator; it MUST serve only bytes that entered through the single validated durable admit (`pump_block` / DC-NODE-12) or the validated warm-start replay (`bootstrap_initial_state`); it MUST NOT re-run `block_validity` to "prove" a byte safe (provenance is structural), MUST NOT serve raw arbitrary ChainDb bytes (serve ONLY via the BLUE reducers through the trait seams), MUST NOT reconstruct an `AcceptedBlock`, and MUST keep exactly one `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound` (DC-NODE-07; `ServedChainSource` is a read-source enum, not a second dispatch). `serve_gate_admits` + the node-path push sibling MUST be GONE from `node_lifecycle`; `ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh`. **(NEW) forge real KES sign evolves the key (DC-CRYPTO-10, PHASE4-N-AC):** the forge's single real KES sign MUST use `shell.kes_sign_header_advancing` (the evolve-then-sign variant), NEVER the raw `shell.kes_sign_header` / `shell.kes_sign_at` — so the operator KES key is evolved to the requested period before signing (the period-evolution + fail-closed semantics live in the RED `ade_runtime::producer::producer_shell` shell, above); `ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh`. **(NEW) forge-on-followed-tip admissibility (DC-NODE-15 + DC-CONS-24, PHASE4-N-AE):** a recovered/following `--mode node` forge MUST be admissible ONLY when `durable_servable_tip == followed_peer_tip` (canonical hash AND `block_no`) — via the GREEN-by-function `forge_followed_tip_admission` gate called BEFORE the single fenced `forge_one_from_recovered`; otherwise it MUST fail closed with the typed `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp { local_servable_tip, followed_peer_tip, reason }` (no forge, no state transition, tip unchanged — distinct from a forge `Failed`). The recovered anchor (`recovered.tip`) MUST NEVER be a forge base (the fallback is removed). The `FollowedPeerTipSignal` is a forge-ADMISSIBILITY input ONLY — it MUST NOT select, replace, reorder, or prefer chains and MUST NOT reach `select_best_chain` / `chain_selector` / `fork_choice` (DC-CONS-03 stays the follow authority). A `CaughtUp` forge MUST set `prev_hash = PrevHash::Block(selected_tip.hash)` with `block_no == followed_tip.block_no + 1` — parent identity by canonical hash, never block-number alone (DC-CONS-24); `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh`. **(NEW) recover→follow WAL prior-fp continuity (DC-WAL-02 + T-REC-05, PHASE4-N-AE):** the first followed `AdmitBlock` MUST seed its WAL `prior_fp` from the recovered post-state fingerprint, so the recover→follow WAL chain is continuous — no orphan, no fp break across the recover→serve handoff; `ci_check_recover_follow_wal_lineage.sh`. **(NEW) shared receive detector + venue-split resolver (DC-NODE-23/24, PHASE4-N-AI):** a peer-origin item MUST be classified ONCE, venue-blind, by `classify_receive` (a pure total predicate over `(durable_tip, candidate)` — it MUST NOT observe venue / wall-clock / network state and MUST NEVER select, reorder, or prefer chains — that is `select_best_chain` / DC-CONS-03); `resolve_disposition` MUST be TOTAL over the closed venue set with an unknown/undeclared venue taking the conservative `RefuseSingleProducer` arm; a SingleProducer venue MUST keep the DC-NODE-20 fail-closed (never adopt a peer candidate; `run_node_sync` returns `UnexpectedRollback` on any `NodeSyncItem::RollBack`); only a Participant venue's `NeedsForkChoice` reaches the orchestrator, and a RAW `followed_peer_tip` signal MUST NOT reach `select_best_chain`; `ci_check_receive_detector_venue_split.sh`. **(NEW) live fork-choice durable apply + reconciliation (DC-NODE-25/26, PHASE4-N-AI):** a `ChainSelected` / `RolledBack` outcome MUST be applied ONLY via the existing enforced authorities — lockstep receive reducer (DC-CONS-20) + `materialize_rolled_back_state` (CN-STORE-07) for the rollback target + `pump_block` (DC-NODE-05/12) for roll-forward — NO second apply / tip-advance / rollback-materialize path; a fork-choice win is provisional and durably adopted ONLY when its BODIES validate+apply (no header-only tip advance); after any applied decision the orchestrator `selector.current_tip` MUST EQUAL the durable `ChainDb::tip` (a mismatch fails fast); a rejected decision makes NO durable change; `ci_check_live_fork_choice_apply.sh` + `ci_check_live_fork_choice_wiring.sh`. **(NEW) no forge across unresolved re-selection (DC-NODE-28, PHASE4-N-AI):** once a candidate is `NeedsForkChoice` in a Participant venue, forging MUST be DISABLED until the outcome is durably applied+reconciled OR rejected-with-state-unchanged — a producer tick during a pending decision MUST fail closed (typed `ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending`), NEVER forge on the stale pre-resolution local tip; `ci_check_participant_venue_inert.sh` + `ci_check_live_fork_choice_wiring.sh`. **(NEW) live rollback-target canonical binding (DC-NODE-29, PHASE4-N-AI):** a peer `RollBackward(point)` rollback target MUST be resolved against the durable `ChainDb` and use the STORED chain point (stored slot + hash) as the SOLE authority — the peer-supplied slot MUST equal the stored slot for that hash; on any mismatch / unknown hash / `Origin` the path MUST fail closed with a typed error BEFORE `commit_rollback`, BEFORE `WalEntry::RollBack`, BEFORE any ChainDb / LedgerState / PraosChainDepState mutation; no rollback target may be built from mixed peer/local authority; `ci_check_rollback_target_canonical_binding.sh`. |
| **Inbound deps** | None (binary + integration tests). |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_types`, `ade_core`, `ade_crypto`, `ade_ledger`, `ade_runtime` (incl. `admission::{dial_for_admission, run_admission_wire_pump, AdmissionPeerEvent}`, the WirePump now tag-24-unwraps, N-F-G-O), `ade_network` (incl. `codec::chain_sync::Point`, the per-version `versionData` + the FindIntersect/Origin reply, N-F-G-L/M), `ade_codec`, `serde`, `serde_json`, `tokio`. Dev-deps: `ade_testkit`, `tempfile`. |
| **Entry points** | `main()`; `ade_node::run_node_lifecycle` (`--mode node`); `ade_node::node_lifecycle::{run_relay_loop, run_relay_loop_with_sched, ForgeActivation, spawn_live_wire_pump_source, run_node_serve_task, bind_serve_listener, ServeStartError, may_cold_start_forge}`; `ade_node::node_sync::{NodeBlockSource, run_node_sync, forge_one_from_recovered, admit_forged_block_durably, forge_epoch_admission, forge_header_position, forge_followed_tip_admission, ForgeFollowedTipAdmission, NotCaughtUpReason, ForgeRefused, NodeForgeOutcome, FollowedPeerTipSignal, NodeForgeError}` (`admit_forged_block_durably` NEW PHASE4-N-U S1; the last five NEW PHASE4-N-AE); `ade_node::node_lifecycle::{run_node_serve_task, warm_start_recovery}` (PHASE4-N-U: the serve task now reads an `Arc<dyn ChainDb>` durable projection; `warm_start_recovery` does forward-replay + WAL-tail reconciliation); `ade_node::run_loop_planner::*` (GREEN); `ade_node::live_log::{NodeSchedEvent, NodeSchedLogWriter, NodeSchedSink}` (GREEN); `ade_node::forge_intent::*` (GREEN); `ade_node::operator_forge::*` (RED); `ade_node::ba02_pass::*` + `ade_node::ba02_evidence::*`; `ade_node::rehearsal_pass::*` + `ade_node::rehearsal_evidence::*`; `ade_node::produce_mode::*`; `ade_node::cli::{Cli, ProduceCli, Mode}`; `ade_node::{admission, wire_only, key_gen}::*`; `ade_node::node_sync::{NodeSyncItem, classify_receive, resolve_disposition, ReceiveClass, ReceiveDisposition, CandidateSummary, pending_reselection_forge_refusal, durable_tip_matches, ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending}` (PHASE4-N-AI); `ade_node::node_lifecycle::{apply_chain_event, run_participant_sync, declare_participant_venue, AppliedTip, ApplyError}` (PHASE4-N-AI). |
| **Key modules** | `lib.rs`, `cli.rs`, `node.rs`, `main.rs`, **`node_lifecycle.rs`** (the `--mode node` owner + `run_relay_loop` + the carried N-F-C…N-F-G-J wiring + the **N-F-G-K** serve-lifetime decouple + the **N-F-G-P** feed header-validation view + the **N-F-G-Q** forge-successor position + **PHASE4-N-U**: the ForgeTick `admit_forged_block_durably` wiring (S1), `warm_start_recovery` forward-replay + WAL-tail reconciliation (S2), `chaindb` → `Arc<PersistentChainDb>` + `run_node_serve_task` over `ServedChainSource::DurableChainDb` (S3), and the **RETIRED** G-R `serve_gate_admits` + node-path push sibling; **PHASE4-N-AE**: the ForgeTick forge-on-followed-tip gate — recovered-anchor forge-base fallback removed, `forge_followed_tip_admission` called before the single fenced forge, typed `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp` recorded into `ForgeActivation.last_forge_refused` (AE.A) + the recover→follow WAL `prior_fp` seed (AE.C)), **`node_sync.rs`** (the sync driver + recovered-forge handoff + the carried caps/conventions; the N-F-G-Q evolved-spine successor position + the N-F-G-O feed-tag-24 consumer line + **PHASE4-N-U S1**: the NEW fenced `admit_forged_block_durably` driver + **PHASE4-N-AE**: the GREEN-by-function `forge_followed_tip_admission` classifier + `FollowedPeerTipSignal` + the closed `ForgeFollowedTipAdmission`/`NotCaughtUpReason`/`ForgeRefused`/`NodeForgeOutcome`), `forge_intent.rs` (GREEN), `operator_forge.rs` (RED), `run_loop_planner.rs` (GREEN), `ba02_evidence.rs` (GREEN), `live_log/` (GREEN sched vocabulary), `ba02_pass.rs` (RED), `rehearsal_evidence.rs` (GREEN), `rehearsal_pass.rs` (RED), **`produce_mode.rs`** (PHASE4-N-AC: the forge real KES sign now calls `shell.kes_sign_header_advancing`), `wire_only.rs`, `key_gen.rs`, `admission/`, `admission_log/`. **PHASE4-N-AI:** `node_sync.rs` (the `classify_receive` / `resolve_disposition` detector+resolver + `NodeSyncItem` / `NodeSyncError` extension + `ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending`); `node_lifecycle.rs` (the `apply_chain_event` RED apply driver + `run_participant_sync` rollback-follow routing + `declare_participant_venue` + `ForgeActivation.pending_reselection` ForgeTick gate). |

> **GREEN sub-classification (carried):** `forge_intent`, `run_loop_planner`, `ba02_evidence`, `live_log::{sched_event,sched_writer}`, `rehearsal_evidence` are GREEN-by-content; `node_sync::{forge_epoch_admission, forge_header_position, forge_followed_tip_admission}` (the last NEW, PHASE4-N-AE — the pure forge-on-followed-tip classifier) + `node_lifecycle::may_cold_start_forge` are GREEN-by-function. `node_lifecycle` + `node_sync` + `operator_forge` + `ba02_pass` + `rehearsal_pass` are RED. The G-K/G-P/G-Q/G-R changes are all RED wiring within `node_lifecycle` / `node_sync`. The PHASE4-N-U changes (`admit_forged_block_durably` driver, `warm_start_recovery` forward-replay, `Arc<PersistentChainDb>` + serve-as-projection wiring) are all RED within `node_lifecycle` / `node_sync`; the G-R `serve_gate_admits` GREEN-by-function predicate is RETIRED (superseded by the RED durable-chain serve projection in `ade_runtime`). **PHASE4-N-AI:** `node_sync::{classify_receive, resolve_disposition, pending_reselection_forge_refusal, durable_tip_matches}` are GREEN-by-function pure classifiers (like `forge_followed_tip_admission` / `forge_epoch_admission`); `node_lifecycle::{apply_chain_event, run_participant_sync}` + the ForgeTick `pending_reselection` gate are RED loop/apply wiring. The +2 new BLUE canonical types (`RollbackPoint` / `RollbackReason`) live in `ade_ledger::wal::event`, NOT in `ade_node`; the BLUE `select_best_chain` it routes to is byte-unchanged.

### `ade_core_interop`

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | Live cardano-node interop driver. Hosts the `live_*_session` RED binaries plus the N-E S4/S5 GREEN tx-submission bridges and the chain-follow driver (`follow`). `follow` strips the peer's ChainSync `RollForward` `[era_tag, tag24(header_cbor)]` envelope via `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24`. (Unchanged across the G-K…G-R span.) |
| **Creates (RED-only)** | Live-session drivers and transcript types; never semantic types. |
| **MUST NOT** | (1) Construct semantic types from raw bytes. (2) Be depended on by any BLUE/GREEN crate (RED leaf). (3) Overstate semantic truth in evidence. (4) `follow` (CN-WIRE-08) — strip via `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24`. |
| **Inbound deps** | None (RED leaf — binaries). |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_core`, `ade_codec`, `ade_crypto`, `ade_ledger`, `ade_runtime`, `ade_network`, `ade_testkit`, `ade_types`, `tokio`. |
| **Entry points** | `ade_core_interop::bin::{live_tx_submission_session, live_block_production_session, live_block_fetch_session, live_block_follow_session}`; `ade_core_interop::follow::*`; `ade_core_interop::{tx_submission, local_tx_submission}`. |
| **Key modules** | `bin/`, `follow.rs`, `tx_submission.rs`, `local_tx_submission.rs`. |

---

### `ade_network::mux::transport` *(RED)*

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | The only place inside `ade_network` where socket I/O happens. RED tokio shell over the BLUE mux frame primitive and the GREEN session reducer. Provides `MuxTransportHandle` + closed `TransportError` + `DuplexCapacity::DEFAULT` + `spawn_duplex`. (Unchanged across the span.) |
| **Creates (RED-only)** | `MuxTransportHandle`, `TransportError`, `DuplexCapacity`, `MuxTransport`. |
| **MUST NOT** | (1) Construct semantic types. (2) Bypass `mux::frame` for framing. (3) Live in BLUE scope. |
| **Inbound deps** | `ade_runtime::network::{mux_pump, n2n_dialer}`. |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_network::mux::frame` (BLUE), `ade_network::session` (GREEN), `tokio`. |
| **Entry points** | `ade_network::mux::transport::{MuxTransportHandle, spawn_duplex, open_tcp}`. |
| **Key modules** | `mux/transport.rs`. |

---

### `ade_network` *(RED capture binaries — non-session)*

| Attribute | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| **Purpose** | Operator-action capture binaries (live evidence harness) inside `ade_network`. The `ade_chain_sync_capture` binary supports `--intersect-slot` / `--intersect-hash` flags to capture a real Conway `RollForward` golden fixture; the G-L/G-M real-cardano-node handshake + FindIntersect fixtures were captured via this harness family. |
| **MUST NOT** | (1) Construct semantic types from raw bytes. (2) Overstate semantic truth in captured evidence. |
| **Outbound deps** | `ade_network` BLUE/GREEN submodules, `ade_codec`, `ade_types`, `tokio`. |
