## Cross-Module Rules (project-wide)

### Dependency direction (RED → GREEN → BLUE; never outward)

```
ade_types     → {}
ade_codec     → {ade_types}
ade_crypto    → {ade_types, blake2, ed25519-dalek, cardano-crypto[vrf-draft03,kes-sum(test-only),dsign]}
ade_core      → {ade_types, ade_crypto, minicbor}
ade_ledger    → {ade_core, ade_plutus, ade_crypto, ade_codec, ade_types, minicbor, num-*}   [BLUE; seed_consensus_inputs gains the epoch_nonce: Nonce field + SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION 1→2 (N-F-G-N); block_validity::header_input::DecodedBlock gains the additive prev_hash: PrevHash field from the already-parsed header (N-AE, no new type/decode change); wal::event gains the closed-sum variant WalEntry::RollBack {to_point, reason, prior_tip, selected_tip} at the reserved tag 1 + the NEW payload types RollbackPoint/RollbackReason (N-AI — the FIRST new BLUE canonical types since G-N; +2, 177→179) + WalError::RollbackTargetNotInChain; wal::replay re-anchors the fp chain to to_point's in-chain post_fp and re-invokes the EXISTING materialize_rolled_back_state + commit_rollback (a MARKER, NOT a second rollback impl)]
ade_plutus    → {ade_crypto, ade_codec, ade_types, aiken_uplc, pallas-primitives(internal)}
ade_network   → BLUE submodules → {ade_codec, ade_types} (incl. the N-F-G-L encode_n2n_version_params fn + the N-F-G-M ArrayHead enum + decode_array_head_two_form fn + the N-AE chain_sync::server producer_chain_sync_serve FindIntersect cursor last_announced set, DC-PROTO-10 — existing-field write, no new type); session(GREEN) → +BLUE submodules [PHASE4-N-AB: session::core handle_outbound segments > MAX_PAYLOAD outbound payloads into ordered <= MAX_PAYLOAD frames via the single encode_inner_frame authority over the unchanged BLUE mux::frame; NEW GREEN const MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES = 16 MiB fails closed above it (OutboundPayloadTooLarge); CN-SESS-05 — GREEN-only, no new BLUE/external dep]; transport(RED) → +tokio
ade_testkit   → {ade_core, ade_ledger, ade_plutus, ade_runtime, ade_crypto, ade_codec, ade_types, cardano-crypto}   [GREEN]
ade_runtime   → {ade_core, ade_crypto, ade_codec, ade_types, ade_ledger, ade_network, redb, serde*, bech32, base58, cardano-crypto[vrf-draft03,dsign], ed25519-dalek, tokio}   [RED; admission::wire_pump calls ade_codec::unwrap_tag24 on the feed side (N-F-G-O); bootstrap/seed_consensus_merge thread the recovered epoch_nonce/eta0 (N-F-G-N); network::serve_dispatch (N-F-G-H) is the single shared serve-dispatch core, now reading a closed ServedChainSource{Snapshot|DurableChainDb} read-source enum; PHASE4-N-U adds the NEW RED network::served_chain_projection (ChainDbServedSource — read-only durable-ChainDb projection over the BLUE serve seams, reusing ade_ledger::block_validity::{block_header_bytes,decode_block}); PHASE4-N-AA adds the bounded hash-free chaindb serve primitives range_bytes_capped/last_block_bytes + the served_chain_projection MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS=256 cap + the closed ServeRangeOutcome enum (DC-SERVEMEM-01 — RED-only, no new BLUE/external dep; hash still derived via the single BLUE decode_block); PHASE4-N-AC adds the RED producer::producer_shell::kes_sign_header_advancing evolve-then-sign method (DC-CRYPTO-10 — kes_advance_to(period) then kes_sign_header; the deterministic Sum6KES kes_update is reused, signing stays RED, no new BLUE/external dep); PHASE4-N-AE adds the served_chain_projection FindIntersect-only forge-parent intersect clause + private helper earliest_servable_block_prev_hash (DC-NODE-14 — reuses the bounded range_bytes_capped + the single BLUE decode_block + the new DecodedBlock.prev_hash; serves no bytes; RED-only, no new BLUE/external dep); PHASE4-N-AE.F adds the forward_sync::pump::pump_block hash-exact already-have idempotency gate (DC-NODE-16 — get_block_by_hash before the BLUE forward_sync_step reducer, Ok(None) no-op for a same-hash same-slot re-announce; RED-only, no new BLUE/external dep); PHASE4-N-AH adds the additive bootstrap::BootstrapState.replayed_anchor_block_no: Option<u64> derived warm-start recovery summary (recovered_tip.block_no − admit_count; DC-NODE-22 — NOT an independently persisted chain point, no new authority, no new persistence, RED-only, no new BLUE/external dep); PHASE4-N-AI adds the admission::wire_pump AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward {peer, point, tip} rollback-signal preservation + UnsupportedRollbackPoint (DC-PUMP-01 — the rollback POINT preserved as a closed event, no longer downgraded to TipUpdate; Origin fails closed; RED-only, no new BLUE/external dep)]
ade_node      → {ade_types, ade_core, ade_crypto, ade_ledger, ade_runtime, ade_network, ade_codec, serde, serde_json, tokio}   [RED; node_lifecycle gains the N-F-G-K serve-lifetime decouple + N-F-G-P feed-view + N-F-G-Q forge-successor; PHASE4-N-U adds the ForgeTick admit_forged_block_durably wiring + warm_start_recovery forward-replay + Arc<PersistentChainDb> serve-as-projection (ServedChainSource::DurableChainDb), and RETIRES the N-F-G-R serve_gate_admits + node-path push sibling; PHASE4-N-AC the produce_mode forge real KES sign now calls shell.kes_sign_header_advancing (DC-CRYPTO-10 — evolve-then-sign); PHASE4-N-AE adds the ForgeTick forge-on-followed-tip gate (recovered-anchor forge-base fallback removed; forge_followed_tip_admission before the single fenced forge; typed ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp; DC-NODE-15 + DC-CONS-24) + the recover→follow WAL prior-fp seed (DC-WAL-02 + T-REC-05); PHASE4-N-AF/N-AG/N-AH (RED/GREEN, 0 BLUE change): node_sync gains the DC-NODE-20 forge-base rewire (forge_mode_after_admit enters SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine DIRECTLY on self-admit — FirstOwnBlockServed folded out, ForgeMode now 3-state; single_producer_forge_decision reads no cert; the observed-feed competing-block fence) + the DC-NODE-22 warm_start_forge_mode re-entry + the DC-NODE-19 venue_policy projection; run_loop_planner::plan_loop_step gains the 5th VenuePolicy input (DC-NODE-19); node_lifecycle gains dc_node_15_refusal + run_relay_loop_with_sched + the warm-start arm (read_adoption_cert / parse_hex32 / --adoption-cert-path REMOVED); live_log::sched_event gains the closed ForgeBaseSelected evidence variant (CN-NODE-04 / DC-NODE-20); cli drops --adoption-cert-path (keeps --single-producer-venue); the VenueAdoptionCertificate type is REMOVED. forge_intent + run_loop_planner + ba02_evidence + live_log + rehearsal_evidence + node_sync::{forge_epoch_admission,forge_header_position,forge_followed_tip_admission,single_producer_forge_decision,venue_policy,warm_start_forge_mode,forge_mode_after_admit} + node_lifecycle::may_cold_start_forge are GREEN-by-content/function. PHASE4-N-AI (RED/GREEN; the +2 new BLUE types live in ade_ledger, not here): node_sync gains the classify_receive venue-blind detector + resolve_disposition venue-split resolver (DC-NODE-23/24) + NodeSyncItem{Block|RollBack(Point)} + NodeSyncError{Pump|Capture|UnexpectedRollback|RollbackPointSlotMismatch} + ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending + pending_reselection_forge_refusal; node_lifecycle gains the apply_chain_event RED apply driver (RolledBack via materialize_rolled_back_state + commit_rollback + WalEntry::RollBack; DC-NODE-25/26) + run_participant_sync rollback-follow routing (DC-NODE-29 canonical target binding) + declare_participant_venue + ForgeActivation.pending_reselection ForgeTick gate (DC-NODE-28); the live path ROUTES a Participant candidate through the EXISTING chain_selector -> UNCHANGED select_best_chain (DC-CONS-03 — single-best-peer FOLLOW, NOT full ChainSel; CN-CONS-03 stays partial)]
ade_core_interop → {ade_core, ade_codec, ade_crypto, ade_ledger, ade_runtime, ade_network, ade_testkit, ade_types, tokio}   [RED leaf]
```

**Forbidden directions (carried + the G-K…G-R span).** Any BLUE crate (or BLUE `ade_network` submodule) depending on `ade_runtime`, `ade_node`, `ade_core_interop`, or the RED half of `ade_network` is a CI failure (`ci_check_dependency_boundary.sh`). Any non-`ade_plutus` crate referring to `pallas_*` is a CI failure. A second block-envelope encoder, a second `leader_vrf_input` authority, a second `wrap_tag24`/`unwrap_tag24` definition or a hand-rolled tag-24 parse in RED, a forward-sync `AdvanceTip` before durability, a Mithril/genesis bootstrap path bypassing the single `bootstrap_initial_state`, an internal-fingerprint-vs-Haskell-hash equality assertion, a registry rule citing a non-existent `code_locus`, and a Mithril-bootstrap path sourcing the anchor `seed_point` from the manifest are all CI failures (the carried N-A…N-F-G-J fences). The N-F-G-J fences (`ci_check_prevhash_single_wire_authority.sh`, `ci_check_genesis_successor_reachability.sh`, `ci_check_node_sched_events_emit_only.sh`) stay in force. **NEW (this catch-up span):**
- **N-F-G-K (DC-NODE-09):** a `--mode node` serve listener whose lifetime is coupled to the feed source's end (tears down when the feed ends) is a CI failure (`ci_check_node_serve_lifetime.sh`). The serve task is spawned OUTSIDE `run_relay_loop` and stays up past feed-end; `run_relay_loop` containment is byte-unchanged. `RO-LIVE-01` stays partial.
- **N-F-G-L (CN-WIRE-10):** a serve-side N2N `versionData` emitted by any path but the single per-version `encode_n2n_version_params`, or a per-version field shape that a real cardano-node rejects (the `TInt 1` shape), or a widening of the closed `N2N_SUPPORTED` version SET, is a CI failure (`ci_check_n2n_handshake_versiondata_authority.sh`). A successful handshake is a wire event, not peer acceptance.
- **N-F-G-M (CN-WIRE-11):** a ChainSync `FindIntersect` decode that rejects the real cardano-node's indefinite-length points list, a `decode_array_head_two_form` that becomes a general definite/indefinite decoder for the rest of the closed grammar (the acceptance is SCOPED to FindIntersect), or an `Origin` point answered anything but `IntersectFound[Origin]` (or a served chain widened beyond the Origin intersect), is a CI failure (`ci_check_chainsync_findintersect_compat.sh`).
- **N-F-G-N (T-REC-04 / DC-CINPUT-03):** a recovered seed-epoch sidecar that omits `epoch_nonce`, a v1 sidecar accepted as anything but `UnknownVersion` (a default-to-zero eta0), or a WarmStart forge whose VRF input is not `praos_vrf_input(slot, epoch_nonce)` from the overlaid recovered eta0, is a CI failure (`ci_check_warmstart_eta0_overlay.sh`). The `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` `epoch_nonce` field is additive ONLY behind the `SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION 1 → 2` gate.
- **N-F-G-O (CN-WIRE-12):** a feed-side WirePump that hands a tag-24-wrapped BlockFetch `MsgBlock` payload to the BLUE decode without stripping it via `ade_codec::unwrap_tag24`, or that adds a parallel / hand-rolled tag-24 parse, is a CI failure (`ci_check_feed_tag24_unwrap.sh`). The single `CN-WIRE-08` tag-24 authority is reused.
- **N-F-G-P (DC-CINPUT-04):** a feed header-validation (Step 5 + Step 7) view derived from a defaulted / empty stake distribution instead of the recovered consensus surface (`from_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`) is a CI failure (`ci_check_feed_leader_threshold_view.sh`). The verdict stays BLUE.
- **N-F-G-Q (DC-NODE-10):** a successor forge that derives its `(block_number, prev_hash)` from the stale recovered tip instead of the evolved admitted spine state, a successor forge that takes a `ChainDb` handle / advances a durable tip, is a CI failure (`ci_check_forge_successor_evolved_spine.sh`).
- **N-F-G-R (DC-NODE-11) — SUPERSEDED by N-U S3:** the G-R monotone serve gate is RETIRED (its `ci_check_served_chain_stability.sh` gate replaced by `ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh`); the served-chain stability invariant is now enforced by serve-as-projection of the extend-only durable chain (DC-NODE-13).

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AI — live fork-choice rollback-follow wiring; single-best-peer FOLLOW, NOT full ChainSel):**
- **N-AI AI-S1 (DC-NODE-27 / CN-WAL-01 / CN-STORE-07 / DC-CONS-20):** a `WalEntry::RollBack` that implements a SECOND rollback (instead of re-invoking the EXISTING `materialize_rolled_back_state` + lockstep `commit_rollback` on replay), a replay re-anchor that sets the durable tip from the `selected_tip` / `prior_tip` audit fields (instead of re-anchoring to `to_point`'s EXISTING in-chain `post_fp`), a non-append-only WAL change (a tag-1 reuse for a different class, a re-numbering, or consuming the reserved tag 2), or a rollback target not in the active chain that does not fail closed (`RollbackTargetNotInChain`) is a CI failure (`ci_check_wal_rollback_replay_equiv.sh`). The marker re-invokes the existing rollback authority; it is NOT a second rollback implementation.
- **N-AI AI-S2 (DC-NODE-23/24):** a peer-origin item classified more than once or NOT venue-blind, a `classify_receive` that observes venue / wall-clock / network state or that selects/reorders/prefers chains (that is `select_best_chain` / DC-CONS-03), a `resolve_disposition` that is not TOTAL over the closed venue set or whose unknown/undeclared venue does NOT take the conservative `RefuseSingleProducer` arm, a SingleProducer venue that adopts a peer candidate / a peer rollback (instead of the DC-NODE-20 fail-closed — `run_node_sync` returns `UnexpectedRollback`), or a RAW `followed_peer_tip` signal reaching `select_best_chain` is a CI failure (`ci_check_receive_detector_venue_split.sh`).
- **N-AI AI-S3 (DC-NODE-25/26):** a `ChainSelected` / `RolledBack` outcome applied by ANY path but the existing enforced authorities (lockstep receive reducer DC-CONS-20 + `materialize_rolled_back_state` CN-STORE-07 + `pump_block` DC-NODE-05/12), a second apply / durable-tip-advance / rollback-materialize path, a header-only tip advance (a fork-choice win adopted before its BODIES validate+apply through `pump_block`), an applied decision that leaves the orchestrator `selector.current_tip` ≠ the durable `ChainDb::tip` (instead of failing fast), or a rejected decision that makes a durable change is a CI failure (`ci_check_live_fork_choice_apply.sh` + `ci_check_live_fork_choice_wiring.sh`). DC-CONS-03 stays the sole selector — N-AI adds no second selection authority.
- **N-AI AI-S4a (DC-PUMP-01):** a chain-sync `RollBackward` discarded or surfaced only as a `TipUpdate` (instead of the closed `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward {peer, point, tip}` preserving the rollback POINT), or a `RollBackward(Origin)` surfaced as a point (instead of failing closed `UnsupportedRollbackPoint`, drop the peer) is a CI failure (`ci_check_wire_rollback_signal_preserved.sh`).
- **N-AI AI-S4b (DC-NODE-28):** a producer tick that fires during a pending fork-choice re-selection and forges on the stale pre-resolution local tip (instead of failing closed with the typed `ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending`), forging that is not DISABLED until the re-selection is durably applied+reconciled or rejected-with-state-unchanged, or a Participant-venue declaration that is not inert before the live flip is a CI failure (`ci_check_participant_venue_inert.sh` + `ci_check_live_fork_choice_wiring.sh`).
- **N-AI AI-S5 (CN-CONS-01):** a `select_best_chain` that picks a different fork-choice-maximal tip depending on candidate presentation order (an arrival-order-dependence — a determinism failure), or a convergence-evidence manifest that does not match the closed schema, is a CI failure (`ci_check_chain_selection_arrival_order_independent.sh` + `ci_check_convergence_evidence_schema.sh`). `RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated — CE-AI-6 is operator-pass convergence evidence, vacuous-until-committed; `CN-CONS-03` stays partial (single-best-peer venue only, full multi-peer ChainSel out of scope).
- **N-AI AI-S6 (DC-NODE-29):** a live peer `RollBackward(point)` whose rollback target is built from mixed peer/local authority (a peer-supplied slot + a locally-verified hash), or that mutates the durable ChainDb / LedgerState / PraosChainDepState (via `commit_rollback` / `WalEntry::RollBack`) BEFORE the peer slot is verified to equal the durable stored slot for that hash (a Byzantine peer naming a real in-chain hash with an arbitrary lower slot would truncate the chain to a peer-chosen depth), is a CI failure (`ci_check_rollback_target_canonical_binding.sh`). The stored chain point is the SOLE rollback-target authority; the path fails closed pre-mutation on any mismatch / unknown hash / `Origin`.

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AE — recover→serve continuity + forge-on-followed-tip admissibility):**
- **N-AE AE.A (DC-NODE-15 + DC-CONS-24):** a recovered/following `--mode node` forge that builds on the recovered anchor (`recovered.tip`) instead of the followed peer tip, a forge admitted when `durable_servable_tip != followed_peer_tip` (instead of failing closed with the typed `ForgeRefused::NotCaughtUp`), a `FollowedPeerTipSignal` that reaches `select_best_chain` / `chain_selector` / `fork_choice` (instead of being an admissibility-only input that may only PREVENT a forge), or a forged successor whose `prev_hash` does not byte-equal the followed peer tip hash / whose `block_no != followed_tip.block_no + 1` (or that infers parent identity from the block number alone) is a CI failure (`ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh`). DC-CONS-03 stays the follow authority.
- **N-AE AE.B (DC-NODE-14):** a `--mode node` serve forge-parent projection that serves BYTES for the projected point (instead of FindIntersect-only — `get_block_by_hash` / `serve_range` must stay empty), that mints a synthetic StoredBlock or serves the recovered snapshot anchor as an un-intersectable chain head, that projects more than the `prev_hash` of the earliest servable StoredBlock or uses a second decode/hash authority / an unbounded scan (instead of the single `decode_block` over the bounded `range_bytes_capped`), or that projects anything when recover-only (no StoredBlock) / when the earliest parent is `Genesis` (instead of failing closed) is a CI failure (`ci_check_recovered_anchor_intersectable.sh`). DC-SERVEMEM-01 (bounded serve) is preserved.
- **N-AE AE.C (DC-WAL-02 + T-REC-05):** a recover→follow handoff whose first followed `AdmitBlock` does not seed its WAL `prior_fp` from the recovered post-state fingerprint (an orphan / fp break across the handoff) is a CI failure (`ci_check_recover_follow_wal_lineage.sh`).
- **N-AE AE.E (DC-PROTO-10):** a `producer_chain_sync_serve` FindIntersect handler that, after `IntersectFound(point)` at a non-Origin point, leaves the read cursor unset (serving block 0 / `next_after(None)` to a client whose read pointer is its own tip → `UnexpectedBlockNo(tip_block_no + 1)(0)`) instead of setting `last_announced = point` (so the next `RequestNext` serves `next_after(point)`), or that fails to keep an `Origin` intersect's cursor `None` (serve-from-start), is a correctness failure (test-enforced; `DC-PROTO-10.ci_script = ""`). RO-LIVE-01 stays partial — a recovered node that forges a peer-adoptable successor is the C2 mechanism, not operator-witnessed acceptance.

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AE.F — receive idempotency):**
- **N-AE.F (DC-NODE-16):** a `pump_block` already-have skip gated on SLOT alone (instead of HASH equality via `get_block_by_hash(&decoded.block_hash)`), a skip placed AFTER the BLUE chokepoint reducer (`forward_sync_step`) so the no-op still runs a reducer step / appends to the WAL, a skip that short-circuits a DIFFERENT block (different hash) at/before the last-applied slot (instead of letting it reach the unchanged BLUE authority and fail closed `SlotBeforeLastApplied` / `BlockNoOutOfOrder`), a missing `stored.slot == decoded.header_input.slot` slot-consistency check, or any skip-past / fork-choice on the receive path (DC-CONS-03 stays the follow authority) is a CI failure (`ci_check_receive_idempotency.sh`). AE.F closes the post-CE-A5 echo (the relay re-announcing Ade's own adopted forged tip); it is a deterministic RED-chokepoint durable-store query, makes NO BLUE change, and the no-op is replay-equivalent (T-REC-05 / DC-WAL-02 preserved). `RO-LIVE-01` stays partial.

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AH — local selected durable chain forge-base authority + cert evidence-only + warm-start re-entry):**
- **N-AH S1 (DC-NODE-20):** a declared rung-1 single-producer `--mode node` post-self-admit forge that derives its forge base from `followed_peer_tip` or the adoption cert instead of Ade's LOCAL selected durable tip (`ChainDb::tip`), a `CaughtUpToPeerTip -> SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine` transition that still parks on a `FirstOwnBlockServed` cert-wait (the intermediate MUST be folded out — `ForgeMode` is 3-state), a competing-block check that RESOLVES a fork instead of FAILING CLOSED (the observed-feed fence is admissibility, NOT fork-choice — that is rung 2), a silent fallback to `followed_peer_tip` / the cert when the 6-condition fence fails, a forge advancing a durable tip outside `pump_block` (the sole durable admit authority — `DC-NODE-05`/`DC-NODE-12`), or a weakening of the DC-NODE-15 INITIAL catch-up gate (it stays for `InitialCatchupRequired -> CaughtUpToPeerTip` — phase-split, not removed; the call chain `run_relay_loop_with_sched -> dc_node_15_refusal -> forge_followed_tip_admission` must hold) is a CI failure (`ci_check_local_durable_forge_base.sh` + the phase-split half of `ci_check_forge_followed_tip_admission.sh`). DC-CONS-03 stays the rung-2 fork-choice authority, untouched.
- **N-AH S2 (DC-NODE-21):** any `ade_node` production code that reads / parses / names the adoption certificate in the forge-authority surface — a `read_adoption_cert` / `parse_hex32` / `VenueAdoptionCertificate` / `--adoption-cert-path` token surviving in the forge path, or the cert feeding forge-base selection / appearing in any multi-producer / preprod / production forge path — is a CI failure (`ci_check_cert_evidence_only.sh` + `ci_check_node_path_fidelity.sh`). The cert is rung-1 RED operator EVIDENCE parsed by the harness OUTSIDE the node (the parser is GONE from `ade_node`, not just demoted); it can never become chain-selection or durable authority, and must be removed/replaced before rung 2 / preprod.
- **N-AH S4b (DC-NODE-22):** a single-producer warm-start that re-initializes `forge_mode = InitialCatchupRequired` when the recovered durable tip is ABOVE the replay anchor (re-introducing, through restart, the exact follow-link dependency DC-NODE-20 retired — a stall in `NoTipAvailable` if the follow link EOFs first), a re-entry that engages without ALL of (single-producer venue; a SUCCESSFUL warm-start; a contiguous/servable recovered spine; the recovered tip BEYOND the bootstrap anchor; no competing peer block observed; relay non-producing; no cert read; no fork-choice; `pump_block` the sole durable admit authority), or a re-entry that admits anything (it only SETS the forge MODE / reads the recovered tip) is a CI failure (`ci_check_warm_start_re_entry.sh`). Any unmet condition FAILS CLOSED to `InitialCatchupRequired` (never a guessed extend). The `replayed_anchor_block_no` is a DERIVED recovery summary (`recovered_tip.block_no − admit_count`), never an independently persisted chain point.
- **N-AH S4a (CN-NODE-04 / DC-NODE-20 evidence):** a `NodeSchedEvent::ForgeBaseSelected` carrying a `ForgeBaseSource` other than `LocalChaindbTip` (the closed set is `LocalChaindbTip` only in rung-1 — a peer-tip / cert source is fail-closed by DC-NODE-20/21), a sched event READ by the planner / any authority path (the vocabulary is emit-only — `ci_check_node_sched_events_emit_only.sh`), or a forge-base evidence event that is not wired to the `--log` JSONL transcript is a CI failure (`ci_check_live_transcript_forge_base.sh`). RED evidence ONLY — it serializes the decision already made; it never alters the forge scheduling / base / authority. `RO-LIVE-01` stays partial — the run-4 live transcript is the C2-LOCAL rung-1 mechanism, not operator-witnessed bounty acceptance.

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AG — single-producer loop-continuation-after-feed-EOF):**
- **N-AG (DC-NODE-19, declared):** a RED `LoopState` re-derivation / "lie" to the planner instead of an explicit GREEN 5th `VenuePolicy` input, a numeric "max blind forges" cap (an artificial operator policy, not a Cardano semantic invariant — the continuation is fenced to the certified single-producer run, not a magic number), a new durable tip-advance path (`pump_block` stays sole authority — `DC-NODE-05`/`DC-NODE-12`), a RED signal selecting / replacing / reordering / preferring chains (DC-CONS-03 untouched), a continuation OUTSIDE the certified single-producer extend state (each of the 7 certified-run conditions must FAIL CLOSED: not `VenueRole::SingleProducer`; not `SingleProducerExtendOwnDurableSpine`; operator shutdown; a forge-validity bound fails — off-epoch DC-EPOCH-03 / beyond forecast horizon DC-CONS-09 / KES-period invalid; a competing chain observed before EOF; relay-producing evidence; the certificate absent/malformed), a continuation of a NON-EOF `Ending` (a fatal source failure must `Err`/fail-fast), a busy-spin under a dead feed (the `Idle` wait is clock-tick / shutdown-bounded), or any persisted / replay-visible state from the policy or the continuation (`VenuePolicy` + the planner decision are RED/GREEN scheduling, never WAL'd) is a CI failure (`ci_check_single_producer_loop_continuation.sh`). The default `VenueRole::Unknown` venue takes the verbatim prior `HaltCleanly`-on-feed-end path. A loop-lifecycle refinement, NOT a fork-choice change — feed work still drains via `SyncOnce` before any `ForgeTick`. DC-NODE-19 is `declared` (the gate landed; full enforcement — the sustained-past-k live transcript CE-AF-6b — is operator-gated and was re-homed onto the DC-NODE-20 local-tip path at N-AH).

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AF — single-producer extend-own-durable-spine; SUPERSEDED by N-AH):**
- **N-AF (DC-NODE-18):** a single-producer extend-forge that proceeds WITHOUT a declared `VenueRole::SingleProducer`, that infers the venue-adoption certificate from a self-admit (the cert was matched by CHAIN-POINT IDENTITY — hash + block_no — NEVER inferred), that persists / replay-exposes the certificate (it was ADMISSIBILITY-ONLY), that uses booleans instead of the closed `ForgeMode` enum + its GREEN transition fn, or that lets the default `VenueRole::Unknown` path diverge from the VERBATIM prior DC-NODE-15 gate is a CI failure (`ci_check_single_producer_extend_own_spine.sh`). DC-CONS-03 untouched (the decision never references a chain selector). **SUPERSEDED:** N-AH folded out the `FirstOwnBlockServed` cert-wait + REMOVED the `VenueAdoptionCertificate` type + parser — the extend state is now entered DIRECTLY on local self-admit (`DC-NODE-20`); the N-AF cert-promotion mechanism is gone. `DC-NODE-17` (the OQ-1 SAFETY-only observation invariant — the real cardano-node relay does not re-announce Ade's own adopted block over the follow link) is RETAINED as observation only, no gate.

**NEW (PHASE4-N-U — forged-block durability):**
- **N-U S1 (DC-NODE-12 / DC-CONS-23 / DC-WAL-04):** a ForgeTick-arm forged block reaching the durable tip by ANY path but the fenced `admit_forged_block_durably` driver → `forward_sync::pump_block` — a forge-specific `put_block` / `AdvanceTip` / `rollback`, a second durable tip-advance path, a re-encode (not feeding `accepted.into_bytes()` verbatim), a new `NodeBlockSource` / `WalEntry` variant, an admit-time `select_best_chain` / `fork_choice`, or a stale-tip own-block override (instead of fail-closed) — is a CI failure (`ci_check_forged_durable_admit_via_pump.sh` + the containment gate `ci_check_node_run_loop_containment.sh`). `pump_block` stays the sole durable tip authority; DC-CONS-03 stays the follow/`chain_selector` authority (the durable admit is extend-only).
- **N-U S2 (T-REC-05 / DC-WAL-04 no-orphan):** a `warm_start_recovery` that does not recover a forged-block durable tip byte-identically, that re-implements forward-replay instead of reusing `bootstrap_initial_state`, that fails to drop an un-WAL'd forged orphan, or that silently diverges instead of failing fast on a recovered-fp ≠ WAL-tail-`post_fp` (`WarmStartWalTailFingerprintMismatch`) is a recovery-correctness failure (test-enforced; `T-REC-05.ci_script = ""`).
- **N-U S3 (DC-NODE-13 / CN-CONS-07 serve clause):** a `--mode node` served view backed by an in-memory accumulator instead of the durable-ChainDb projection, a serve path that re-runs `block_validity` to "prove" provenance (instead of structural provenance), that serves raw arbitrary ChainDb bytes outside the BLUE reducers, that reconstructs an `AcceptedBlock`, that re-encodes (not serving `stored.bytes` verbatim), or that adds a second `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound` is a CI failure (`ci_check_served_chain_projection.sh` + `ci_check_single_serve_dispatch_authority.sh`). `serve_gate_admits` + the node-path push sibling MUST be gone from `node_lifecycle`. `RO-LIVE-01` stays partial — durability + coherent serve ≠ peer acceptance.

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AB — outbound mux segmentation):**
- **N-AB (CN-SESS-05):** an outbound mini-protocol payload larger than `MAX_PAYLOAD` that is NOT segmented into ordered `<= MAX_PAYLOAD` mux frames (so it hits `encode_inner_frame`'s single-frame `MAX_PAYLOAD` guard and fails), a segmentation path that introduces a SECOND / parallel frame encoder (instead of reusing the single `encode_inner_frame` authority over the BLUE `mux::frame`), a segmentation that truncates / drops / reorders bytes (`concat(segments) != payload`) or changes the mini-protocol id / mode across segments, a per-segment clock read (instead of reusing the one captured timestamp — a determinism break), or a payload above the FIXED non-configurable GREEN const `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES = 16 MiB` that is NOT failed closed (`OutboundPayloadTooLarge`) — incl. any CLI/env/config escape that disables/widens the ceiling or an unbounded outbound buffer — is a CI failure (`ci_check_outbound_segmentation.sh`). N-AB is the GREEN, deterministic, lossless inverse of `CN-SESS-04` inbound reassembly; it transmits bytes the producer already produced and makes no peer-acceptance claim (`RO-LIVE-01` stays partial).

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AC — KES signing evolves key to current period):**
- **N-AC (DC-CRYPTO-10):** a forge real KES sign that uses the raw `shell.kes_sign_header` / `shell.kes_sign_at` instead of the evolve-then-sign `kes_sign_header_advancing` (so the minted-at-period-0 key is never evolved and a leader slot in KES period > 0 fails `KesPeriodNotCurrent`), a `kes_sign_header_advancing` that manually adjusts the period (`period ± N`) instead of passing it verbatim, a re-implemented KES evolution instead of the existing deterministic Sum6KES `kes_update`, a `kes_update` that loses either fail-closed guard (`EvolutionBackwards` on a backwards period / `EvolutionExhausted` beyond the key lifetime), or any signing that leaks into BLUE (`T-KEY-01` — `ci_check_no_signing_in_blue.sh`) is a CI failure (`ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh`). The Sum6KES evolution is reused (not re-implemented); signing stays RED; the BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + KES verifier are unchanged. `RO-LIVE-01` stays partial — a period-1 block the real cardano-node downloads with no KES/parse rejection is a header-acceptance event, not operator-witnessed bounty acceptance.

**NEW (PHASE4-N-AA — bounded peer-driven serve range):**
- **N-AA (DC-SERVEMEM-01):** a peer-driven `--mode node` serve path that materializes an unbounded chain range, performs a per-block full-index (`SLOT_BY_HASH`) scan, reads more than `MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS = 256` blocks for a single peer request, reads via the unbounded `iter_from_slot` / O(N) `chaindb.tip()` instead of the bounded `range_bytes_capped` / `last_block_bytes` primitives, introduces a CLI/env/config escape to disable/widen the cap, adds a second hash authority (instead of deriving the hash via the single BLUE `decode_block`), or fails to fail-closed (a panic, or wrong/partial bytes) on an oversized / inverted (`from > to`) / undecodable range is a CI failure (`ci_check_serve_range_bounded.sh`). The cap is a defensive implementation bound, not a Cardano semantic parameter; the trusted recovery/rollback `iter_from_slot` internals are out of scope. `RO-LIVE-01` stays partial.

### Naming convention

All crates are prefixed `ade_`. TCB color is not encoded in the crate name. The authoritative classifier is `.idd-config.json` `core_paths` + the per-file `// Core Contract:` / `//! BLUE|GREEN|RED` banner + the cluster TCB Color Maps; CI scripts hard-code their BLUE list.

### Closed enums / registries (for SEAMS cross-reference)

Closed semantic surfaces detected at HEAD (carried + the G-K…G-R span): `AcceptedMiniProtocol` (`ade_network::session`), `TagEnvelopeError` (`ade_codec::cbor::tag24`), `ExpectedVrfInput` / `LeaderCheckVerdict` (`ade_core::consensus`), `OutboundCommand` + `DispatchError` (`ade_runtime::network`), `KesError` / `KesParseError`, the admission/wire-only/live-log JSONL vocabularies (incl. the N-F-G-J emit-only `NodeSchedEvent`), the operator-evidence manifest TOML schema, the closed `CardanoEra` / Conway cert + governance enums, `PrevHash` (`ade_types::shelley::block`, the N-F-G-J closed `Genesis | Block(Hash32)` wire grammar). **N-F-A:** `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` (version-gated; the SOLE codec) + `SeedConsensusInputsError` / `SeedConsensusMergeError` / `SeedEpochConsensusSource` + the WAL variant `WalEntry::SeedEpochConsensusInputsImported`. **N-F-C:** `Mode` (5-variant), `NodeStart`, `NodeBlockSource` (2-variant), the BA-02 evidence vocabulary. **N-F-D/E:** `LoopStep` (4-variant) + `ForgeSlotStatus` + the additive `SessionError::ReassemblyBufferOverflow`. **N-F-F:** `ForgeIntent` / `ForgeIntentError` / `OperatorForgeError`. **N-F-G-A:** `SlotAlignmentError` / `ProtocolParamsParseError` / `ForgeCurrentPParamsError` / `ForgeEpochAdmission`. **N-F-G-B:** `SelfAcceptedHandoff`. **N-F-G-D:** `RehearsalVenue` (1-variant) + `PrivateRehearsalManifest`. **N-F-G-H:** `DispatchError` (4-variant) + `ServeStartError` (2-variant). **NEW (the catch-up span):** the closed BLUE `ArrayHead { Definite(u64), Indefinite }` (`ade_network::codec::primitives`, N-F-G-M / CN-WIRE-11 — the SOLE new closed type in the span; the indefinite-length acceptance is SCOPED to ChainSync `FindIntersect`); the `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` closed record gains the additive `epoch_nonce: Nonce` field under the **bumped `SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION = 2`** version gate (N-F-G-N — a versioned-gate extension of an existing closed type, NOT a new type); `Mode` (5-variant) / `NodeBlockSource` (2-variant) / `NodeForgeError` / `ServeStartError` / the N2N `N2N_SUPPORTED` version SET all stay **unchanged** (G-K…G-R add no `--mode node` flag and no new variant — the serve-lifetime / feed-view / forge-successor / serve-stability fixes are new RED code paths through the existing closed surfaces, and the G-L `encode_n2n_version_params` + G-M `decode_array_head_two_form` are additive fns over the unchanged closed version SET / wire grammar). **Governance:** `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` stays a single closed canonical type with a SOLE codec — the `epoch_nonce` field is a **version-GATED** addition (a v1 sidecar fails closed as `UnknownVersion`, never a silent zero-eta0); the eight catch-up-span rules are all `tier = derived` EXCEPT `T-REC-04` (`tier = true` — the recovered eta0 must be replay-equivalent), and none is BLUE consensus law that flips an RO-LIVE rule (the serve/feed/forge fixes are mechanical; the live operator ACCEPT stays `RO-LIVE-01` partial / operator-gated). `ArrayHead`'s indefinite-length acceptance is deliberately SCOPED (CN-WIRE-11), not a general grammar widening. **PHASE4-N-U:** the NEW closed read-source enum `ServedChainSource { Snapshot(&ServedChainView) | DurableChainDb(&dyn ChainDb) }` (`ade_runtime::network::serve_dispatch`) — a closed 2-variant selector for WHERE the single `dispatch_server_frame_event_to_outbound` reads, NOT a second dispatch authority (DC-NODE-07 preserved). NO new `WalEntry` variant, NO new `NodeBlockSource` variant (forged provenance is NOT conflated with received). The G-R `serve_gate_admits` monotone-serve predicate + its in-module test are **RETIRED** (a surface REDUCTION — the in-memory accumulator + its gate are gone; serve is now a read-only projection of the extend-only durable chain, DC-NODE-13). **Governance:** N-U adds no new canonical type and no new BLUE authority; the five N-U rules are `tier = derived` EXCEPT `T-REC-05` (`tier = true` — the recovered forged tip must be replay-equivalent); none flips an RO-LIVE rule (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated). **PHASE4-N-AA:** the NEW closed RED enum `ServeRangeOutcome { Served(Vec<(SlotNo, Hash32, Vec<u8>)>) | Empty | CapExceeded | ReadError }` (`ade_runtime::network::served_chain_projection`) — a closed 4-variant serve-read outcome (every non-`Served` variant → the reducer wire `NoBlocks`), NOT a dispatch authority (DC-NODE-07 preserved). The RED value type `CappedSlotRange { blocks, truncated }` (`ade_runtime::chaindb::types`) is a closed 2-field struct. The `const MAX_SERVE_RANGE_BLOCKS = 256` cap is a FIXED, non-configurable literal (no runtime escape). All RED — bounded storage/serve plumbing, NOT canonical types; NO new `WalEntry` / `NodeBlockSource` variant. **Governance:** N-AA adds no new canonical type and no new BLUE authority; the lone N-AA rule `DC-SERVEMEM-01` is `tier = derived`; it does not flip an RO-LIVE rule (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated). **PHASE4-N-AB:** NO new closed type — `CN-SESS-05` adds the GREEN const `MAX_OUTBOUND_PAYLOAD_BYTES = 16 MiB` (a FIXED, non-configurable upper bound on the GREEN session reducer's `handle_outbound`, the outbound counterpart of the receive-side `MAX_REASSEMBLY_TAIL_BYTES`) and reuses the existing closed `SessionError` (the `OutboundPayloadTooLarge { len }` variant was already present) + the single `encode_inner_frame` frame-encode authority over the unchanged BLUE `mux::frame`. **Governance:** N-AB adds no new canonical type and no new BLUE authority; the lone N-AB rule `CN-SESS-05` is `tier = derived`; it does not flip an RO-LIVE rule (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated). **PHASE4-N-AC:** NO new closed type — `DC-CRYPTO-10` adds the RED `&mut self` method `ProducerShell::kes_sign_header_advancing` (a RED key-custody method, NOT a type) and reuses the EXISTING deterministic Sum6KES `kes_update` evolution + the closed `SigningError` (the `EvolutionBackwards` / `EvolutionExhausted` fail-closed variants were already present) + the branded `KesSignature` / `UnsignedHeaderPreImage` types over the unchanged BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + KES verifier. **Governance:** N-AC adds no new canonical type and no new BLUE authority (signing stays RED — `T-KEY-01` preserved); the lone N-AC rule `DC-CRYPTO-10` is `tier = derived` (it strengthens `CN-KES-HEADER-01`); it does not flip an RO-LIVE rule (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated — a period-1 block the real cardano-node downloads with no KES/parse rejection is a header-acceptance event, not bounty acceptance). **PHASE4-N-AE:** the NEW closed RED `ForgeFollowedTipAdmission { CaughtUp | NotCaughtUp(NotCaughtUpReason) }` + the closed `NotCaughtUpReason` + the typed `ForgeRefused { NotCaughtUp { … } }` + `NodeForgeOutcome` + the RED `FollowedPeerTipSignal` (all `ade_node::node_sync`) — closed forge-admissibility / refusal surfaces, NOT canonical types, NOT a chain-selection authority (the followed-tip signal may only PREVENT a forge — it never reaches `select_best_chain` / `chain_selector` / `fork_choice`). The BLUE `DecodedBlock` gains the additive `prev_hash: PrevHash` field (a field on the existing record, NOT a new type; `PrevHash` stays the closed `Genesis | Block(Hash32)` wire grammar owned by `ade_types`); `ProducerChainSyncServerState` is unchanged (an existing `last_announced` field is written, DC-PROTO-10). NO new `WalEntry` / `NodeBlockSource` variant. **Governance:** N-AE adds NO new canonical type and NO new BLUE authority (the two BLUE-tree touches are an additive field + an existing-field cursor write); the four N-AE rules are all `tier = derived`; none flips an RO-LIVE rule (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated — a recovered node that forges a peer-adoptable successor is the C2 mechanism, not operator-witnessed acceptance). **PHASE4-N-AE.F:** NO new closed type — `DC-NODE-16` adds the RED `pump_block` hash-exact already-have idempotency gate (a deterministic durable-store `get_block_by_hash` query + an `Ok(None)` early return, NOT a type) and reuses the existing `ChainDb::get_block_by_hash` + `StoredBlock` over the unchanged BLUE chokepoint reducer; NO new `WalEntry` / `NodeBlockSource` variant. **Governance:** AE.F adds NO new canonical type and NO new BLUE authority (the gate is a RED-chokepoint query, the BLUE header authority is untouched); the lone AE.F rule `DC-NODE-16` is `tier = derived`; it does not flip an RO-LIVE rule (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated). **PHASE4-N-AI:** the NEW BLUE closed-sum variant `WalEntry::RollBack {to_point, reason, prior_tip, selected_tip}` (`ade_ledger::wal::event`, tag 1 — the reserved RollBackward slot; tag 2 `CaptureSnapshot` stays reserved) with the NEW closed payload enum `RollbackReason {ForkChoiceWin | PeerRollBackward}` (uint wire code; unknown code fails closed) + the closed struct `RollbackPoint {slot, hash, block_no}` (the +2 new BLUE canonical types) + the NEW closed `WalError::RollbackTargetNotInChain` variant; the closed RED `node_sync` surfaces `NodeSyncItem {Block | RollBack(Point)}` / `ReceiveClass {AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | Competing}` / `ReceiveDisposition {AlreadyHave | LinearExtend | NeedsForkChoice | RefuseSingleProducer}` + the extended `NodeSyncError {Pump | Capture | UnexpectedRollback | RollbackPointSlotMismatch}` + the new `ForgeRefused::ReselectionPending` variant; and the closed RED `ade_runtime::admission::wire_pump` `AdmissionPeerEvent::RollBackward {peer, point, tip}` + `AdmissionWirePumpError::UnsupportedRollbackPoint`. **Governance:** `WalEntry::RollBack` is a version-gated APPEND-ONLY additive variant (tag 1 reserved; tag 2 untouched) — a DURABLE MARKER re-invoking the EXISTING rollback authority on replay, NOT a second rollback implementation; the seven N-AI rules `DC-NODE-23`…`DC-NODE-29` are all `tier = derived`; **`CN-CONS-03` was NOT flipped to enforced** (it stays `partial` — single-best-peer rollback-follow only; full multi-peer ChainSel out of scope); none flips an RO-LIVE rule (`RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated). `select_best_chain` (the sole DC-CONS-03 selector) is byte-unchanged — N-AI routes to it, adds no second selector.

### CI enforcement (157 scripts under `ci/`)

The full list is mechanically obtainable via `ls ci/ci_check_*.sh` (157 at HEAD `5ec841c8`). CI lives entirely under `ci/` (`ci_dirs = ["ci"]`); there is no `.github/workflows/` invariant gate at HEAD. The NINE NEW gates since the prior on-disk CODEMAP (148 scripts at `5858288e`) are ALL from PHASE4-N-AI and ALL ADDED (0 modified, 0 removed; `git diff --name-status 8e2c3672..HEAD -- 'ci/ci_check_*.sh'` lists exactly 9 `A`): `ci_check_wal_rollback_replay_equiv.sh` (DC-NODE-27), `ci_check_receive_detector_venue_split.sh` (DC-NODE-23/24), `ci_check_live_fork_choice_apply.sh` + `ci_check_live_fork_choice_wiring.sh` (DC-NODE-25/26/28), `ci_check_wire_rollback_signal_preserved.sh` (DC-PUMP-01 / AI-S4a), `ci_check_participant_venue_inert.sh` (DC-NODE-28 / AI-S4b-i), `ci_check_rollback_target_canonical_binding.sh` (DC-NODE-29 / AI-S6), `ci_check_chain_selection_arrival_order_independent.sh` (CN-CONS-01 / AI-S5), `ci_check_convergence_evidence_schema.sh` (CE-AI-5 / AI-S5). The earlier-span gates carried below (N-AF/N-AG/N-AH and back) are unchanged. The PHASE4-N-AI + carried N-AF / N-AG / N-AH + AE.F + N-AE + N-AC / N-AB / N-AA / G-K…G-R / N-U new gates:
